### [1] [Hazard or Anomaly? Evaluating VLMs for Understanding Dangers and Discrepancies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18325)
*Murali Indukuri,Mohammad Eskandari,Sree Nitya Kollu,Stephanie Lukin,Cynthia Matuszek*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了视觉语言模型（VLMs）在安全关键系统中的人机交互应用，提出区分‘危险’与‘异常’的概念，以更准确评估模型的安全推理能力。通过多数据集和多种提示策略的实验发现，现有VLMs常将异常场景误判为危险，说明其过度依赖上下文不规则性作为危险判断依据。明确分离异常与危险可揭示二元判断无法暴露的模型缺陷，提升评估的透明度和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLMs在安全场景中的评估多采用二元判断（安全/不安全），难以区分真正的物理危险与非危险的异常情况，导致对模型安全推理能力的评估不准确。因此需要引入‘危险’与‘异常’的明确区分，以更真实地评估模型的可靠性。

Method: 提出并实施了危险与异常的分离框架，在两个数据集上测试多个SOTA VLMs，并采用不同提示策略进行对比分析，验证该区分是否影响模型行为。

Result: 实验表明，多数VLMs会将异常视为危险，显示出对上下文不规则性的过度依赖；而显式分离异常与危险能更全面揭示模型的错误模式，提供更细致的评估视角。

Conclusion: 显式区分危险与异常有助于更准确地评估VLMs在安全关键任务中的推理能力，避免因二元判断掩盖潜在缺陷，推动更可靠的人机协作安全系统发展。

Abstract: Modern safety-critical systems increasingly rely on human-robot interaction to reduce disaster risk and support decision-making during emergencies. Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are promising for these settings because they can interpret complex scenes and communicate safety-relevant information, but they still require careful evaluation to ensure reliable safety reasoning. In particular, current evaluations often frame danger recognition as a binary decision (Safe/Unsafe), making it unclear whether a model is identifying true physical hazards or merely reacting to unusual scene elements. We address this limitation by introducing an explicit distinction between hazard and anomaly, and by separately recognizing hazardous and anomalous states. We evaluate several state-of-the-art VLMs across two datasets and multiple prompting strategies to test whether this distinction changes model behavior. Our results show that VLMs frequently misinterpret anomalousness as hazardousness, revealing an over-reliance on contextual irregularity as a proxy for danger. We further show that explicitly separating anomaly from hazard provides a more informative evaluation of VLM safety reasoning and exposes failure modes that binary safety judgments can obscure. Our public dataset is available on Roboflow https://app.roboflow.com/vlm-in-context-anomaly-and-hazard-detection/camera-ready-roman-ds.

</details>


### [2] [From Pixel to Prognosis: Convolutional and GLCM Feature Fusion for Automated Four-Class Cataract Severity Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18349)
*K. Mithra,Prem Kumar Santhanam*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种低成本、自动化的白内障严重程度分类系统，利用普通消费级彩色眼图进行四类分级（正常、未成熟、成熟、过熟），通过融合CNN深度特征与手工提取的GLCM及强度描述符，并使用RBF核SVM分类，准确率达95.0%，优于纯纹理或纯CNN基线，适用于资源有限地区的基层医疗和远程医疗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一种无需专业眼科设备、成本低廉且可部署于资源有限环境的白内障严重程度自动分类系统，以支持基层医疗和远程医疗应用。

Method: 设计了一种混合框架，结合CNN提取的深层特征与从霍夫圆检测定位的瞳孔区域中提取的五种手工纹理特征（GLCM及均值、均匀性、标准差、对比度、能量），并采用带有RBF核的多类SVM进行分类。

Result: 在300张图像（每类75张）组成的专家标注测试集上，该融合系统达到95.0%准确率、93.8%敏感性和96.1%特异性，优于仅使用纹理（88.5%）或仅使用CNN（91.3%）的基线方法，并超越已有深度学习研究结果。

Conclusion: CNN-GLCM-SVM融合框架在无需GPU加速或专用相机的情况下实现了具有竞争力的四类白内障分级性能，适合在资源受限环境中用于初级保健和远程医疗场景。

Abstract: Objective: To develop a low-cost automated cataract severity classification system operating on standard consumer-grade colour photographs of the eye, without specialised ophthalmic hardware. Methods: A hybrid framework was designed that fuses deep features from a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) with five handcrafted Grey-Level Co-occurrence Matrix (GLCM) and intensity descriptors - mean intensity, uniformity, standard deviation, contrast, and energy - extracted from a Hough-circle-localised pupil Region of Interest (ROI). A multi-class Support Vector Machine (SVM) with Radial Basis Function (RBF) kernel classifies each image into one of four severity grades: normal, immature, mature, or hypermature cataract. Results: The proposed fused system achieved 95.0% accuracy, 93.8% sensitivity, and 96.1% specificity on an ophthalmologist-labelled test set drawn from 300 images (75 per class) collected at an ophthalmology clinic, outperforming texture-only (88.5%) and CNN-only (91.3%) baselines and surpassing recently published deep learning approaches. Conclusion: The CNN-GLCM-SVM fusion framework provides competitive four-class cataract grading without GPU acceleration or specialised cameras, making it suitable for primary-care and telemedicine deployment in resource-limited settings.

</details>


### [3] [Surprise Forcing: What to Remember, When to Skip in Long Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18436)
*Shuwei Shi,Zhen Li,Muyao Niu,Chuanhao Li,Bo Zheng,Kaipeng Zhang,Yinqiang Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Surprise Forcing 提出一种无需训练的框架，解决流式自回归扩散模型在长视频生成中的资源分配不均问题。通过引入基于意外度的内存银行和自适应去噪机制，动态调整关键帧记忆与去噪步骤，提升长时序一致性与视觉质量，同时保持实时流式处理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流式自回归扩散模型存在上下文受限和固定去噪调度的问题，导致资源分配不合理：远距离重要视觉信息被遗忘，且所有生成块均接受相同去噪次数，忽略实际难度差异。

Method: 提出 Surprise Forcing 框架，包含两个核心模块：1）Surprise-Gated Memory Bank，利用全局偏差与最近邻新颖性信号评估被驱逐帧的价值，通过反馈控制预算在归一化得分空间中决定是否保留；2）Surprise-Aware Denoising，根据首轮去噪后相邻帧的最大余弦距离估计块难度，采用局部百分位调度跳过简单块的中间去噪步骤。

Result: 在 VBench、VBench-Long 与 VBench-2.0 上实验表明，该方法显著提升长序列生成的一致性与视觉质量，同时维持实时流式吞吐性能。

Conclusion: Surprise Forcing 有效将资源分配从静态均匀模式转向动态优先级驱动模式，为分钟级视频生成提供了高效、高质量的解决方案。

Abstract: Streaming autoregressive diffusion makes minute-scale video synthesis practical, but its bounded context and fixed denoising schedule allocate resources uniformly across a highly non-stationary sequence. A rolling key-value cache forgets distant visual evidence even when that evidence remains important, while every generated chunk receives the same number of denoising passes irrespective of its actual difficulty. We introduce Surprise Forcing, a training-free framework that treats both limitations as online resource-allocation problems. A Surprise-Gated Memory Bank summarizes evicted frames with value-token descriptors, evaluates them using complementary global-deviation and nearest-neighbor novelty signals, and regulates admission through a feedback-controlled budget in normalized score space. Priority-based replacement and relevance-aware routing then keep the external memory compact and useful. In parallel, Surprise-Aware Denoising estimates chunk difficulty from the maximum adjacent-frame cosine distance after the first denoising pass and uses a local percentile scheduler to skip intermediate steps for comparatively easy chunks. Experiments on VBench, VBench-Long, and VBench-2.0 show that the proposed allocation strategy improves long-horizon consistency and visual quality while retaining real-time streaming throughput.

</details>


### [4] [ECoNGS: Efficient Compressive Neural Gaussian Splats for Volume Visualization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18466)
*Kaiyuan Tang,Chaoli Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ECoNGS提出了一种高效的压缩神经高斯点云框架，用于体积可视化场景表示。通过轻量级神经网络从显式锚点动态预测隐式可编辑的高斯点，结合了隐式表示的紧凑性和显式基元的高性能渲染。采用联合学习策略对几何相似场景进行聚类并共享参数，显著减少训练时间和模型大小，同时保持重建保真度。进一步使用神经熵模型压缩显式锚点属性，实现基于熵编码的紧凑存储。提出一种针对体积可视化场景的简单但有效的高斯初始化方案，提升重建精度并加速收敛。在多种单变量和多变量体积可视化场景中，ECoNGS在训练时间、重建质量和模型尺寸方面均优于现有方法，相比iVR-GS，PSNR提升最高达2.2 dB，模型大小缩小6.1倍，训练时间减少5.9倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于基元的体积可视化方法存在显式表示冗余、非紧凑的问题，且每个场景独立优化导致效率低下。需要一种兼具紧凑性、高效训练和高质量渲染的新型场景表示方法。

Method: ECoNGS采用轻量级神经网络动态生成隐式可编辑的高斯点；通过联合学习策略聚类几何相似场景并共享参数；利用神经熵模型估计锚点属性的概率分布，实现熵编码压缩；设计适用于体积可视化场景的高斯初始化策略以提升重建精度与收敛速度。

Result: 在多个单变量和多变量体积可视化数据集上，ECoNGS在重建质量（最高提升2.2 dB PSNR）、模型尺寸（最大压缩6.1倍）和训练时间（最多减少5.9倍）方面均显著优于现有方法，尤其在iVR-GS对比中表现突出。

Conclusion: ECoNGS成功实现了体积可视化场景表示的高效压缩与快速训练，在保持高质量渲染的同时大幅降低存储与计算开销，为大规模体积数据的交互式可视化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in differentiable Gaussian splatting have highlighted the potential of primitive-based approaches as alternative scene representations for interactive, high-quality, volume visualization (VolVis) of large datasets. However, the explicit nature of current primitive-based methods, combined with isolated optimization for each VolVis scene, results in redundant, non-compact representations. We present ECoNGS, an efficient compressive neural Gaussian splatting framework for VolVis scene representation. ECoNGS employs lightweight neural networks to dynamically predict implicit, editable Gaussian splats from explicit anchor points, effectively combining model compactness and parameter efficiency of implicit representations with high-performance rendering of explicit primitives. We explore a joint learning strategy that clusters geometrically similar scenes and shares parameters across them, significantly reducing overall training time and model size while maintaining reconstruction fidelity. To achieve a more compact scene representation, we further compress the explicit anchor attributes using a neural entropy model that estimates their probability distributions, enabling compact storage via entropy coding. We systematically investigate Gaussian initialization strategies and propose a simple yet effective scheme tailored for VolVis scenes, improving reconstruction accuracy and accelerating convergence. We evaluate ECoNGS qualitatively and quantitatively across various univariate and multivariate VolVis scenes, highlighting its superior performance over prior methods in training time, reconstruction quality, and model size. In particular, compared with the prior method iVR-GS, ECoNGS improves reconstruction quality by up to 2.2 dB in PSNR while reducing the model size by up to 6.1x and the training time by up to 5.9x. The code is available at https://github.com/TouKaienn/ECoNGS.

</details>


### [5] [Style over Substance: A Shortcut Audit of Emotion-Description Preference Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18508)
*Jiabing Yang,Yixiang Chen,Yuan Xu,Qisen Ma,Tao Yu,Peiyan Li,Yingda Li,Yan Huang,Liang Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究对EmoPrefer基准进行了系统性捷径审计，发现仅通过描述长度和生成器身份的简单逻辑回归模型即可达到与微调的7B多模态判别器相当的性能（65.8 vs 66.8 WAF），表明当前评估指标可能受生成风格偏差影响，而非真正基于跨模态内容理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态情绪理解评估依赖人类偏好作为标准，但该研究质疑其是否真正反映对视频内容的接地理解，是否存在可被利用的模型生成风格捷径。

Method: 采用内容无关探测器（content-blind probes）分析人类偏好数据，通过逻辑回归模型仅使用描述长度和生成器身份进行预测，并验证生成器身份在文本中可高度恢复；进一步分析偏好与生成器胜率先验的一致性，并测试去偏后的诊断模型表现。

Result: 生成器身份可从文本中以99.5%准确率恢复，人类偏好在66%的样本上与生成器胜率先验一致；即使在去除冗长性偏差的长度匹配子集上，多模态模型也无显著优势；去风格化诊断模型的内容头表现接近随机水平。

Conclusion: 当前的偏好评分可不依赖对视频内容的真实理解而达成，提示现有评估存在严重风格捷径问题。建议未来评估应采用源平衡配对、严格长度控制、反刻板切片报告及多标注者共识机制。

Abstract: Preference over model-generated emotion descriptions is emerging as a standard evaluation metric for multimodal emotion understanding, exemplified by the MER2026 MER-Prefer track on EmoPrefer. Such benchmarks assume that predicting the preferred description requires grounded cross-modal understanding of the video. We conduct a systematic shortcut audit of EmoPrefer using content-blind probes. A simple logistic regression using only description length and generator identity, without processing the text, video, or audio, performs comparably to LoRA-finetuned 7B text and audio-visual judges (65.8 versus 66.8 WAF on EmoPrefer-V2). Generator identity is recoverable from description text with 99.5 percent accuracy, every candidate pair contrasts two distinct generators, and the human preference labels agree with a fold-exclusive per-generator win-rate prior on 66 percent of the evaluated pairs. When the human label conflicts with this prior, trained judges still follow the style prior on 63 to 80 percent of the pairs. On a length-matched subset that neutralizes verbosity bias, the tested media configurations yield no statistically significant improvement, while an ODIN-inspired diagnostic that decouples the style shortcut leaves its content head near chance. These results do not imply that human preferences are inherently stylistic or that the descriptions contain no emotional information. Instead, they show that the current scores can be reached without verifying either description against the video. We recommend source-balanced pairing, strict length control, counter-stereotypical sliced reporting, and multi-annotator consensus for future cross-generator evaluations. Code is available at https://github.com/jiabingyang01/EmoPrefer-Audit.

</details>


### [6] [DuSPiT: Dual-Branch Sub-Patch Pixel Diffusion Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18510)
*Yunpeng Bai,Yossi Gandelsman,Michaël Gharbi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DuSPiT 是一种新的像素空间扩散变压器，通过双分支结构分离全局结构推理与局部外观建模，实现更丰富的细节和更强的细粒度结构生成，同时在质量与效率之间取得更好平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有像素空间扩散模型将每个图像块映射为单一标记，难以兼顾全局通信与细粒度细节，导致信息表达受限。

Method: 提出 DuSPiT 架构，包含紧凑的基础分支用于高效全局推理，以及并行的高容量像素分支，按子块分组以保留细节，并通过交叉注意力实现两分支交互。

Result: 生成图像具有更丰富的细节和更强的细粒度结构，且在质量-效率权衡上优于先前的像素空间扩散变压器。

Conclusion: DuSPiT 通过分离全局与局部建模，有效提升了像素空间扩散生成的质量与效率，为高质量图像生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers achieve strong image generation performance, but most operate in compressed latent spaces. Pixel-space diffusion avoids this information loss, yet existing approaches map each raw image patch to a single token, forcing one representation to handle both global communication and fine-grained details. We address this issue by proposing a new architecture, \textbf{DuSPiT}, a \textbf{Du}al-branch \textbf{S}ub\textbf{P}atch \textbf{Pi}xel \textbf{T}ransformer. This model separates global structural reasoning from local appearance modeling. DuSPiT uses a compact base branch for efficient global reasoning and a parallel, high-capacity pixel branch, organized into subpatch groups, to preserve detailed appearance, with the two branches interacting through cross-attention. Our results show that DuSPiT generates images with richer details and stronger fine-grained structures, while also achieving a better quality--efficiency trade-off than prior pixel-space diffusion transformers.

</details>


### [7] [AniGS: Bridging Rendering and Diffusion Prior for 3D Scene Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18539)
*Yen-Chi Cheng,Chen Gao,Chuhan Chen,Tuotuo Li,Rajvi Shah,Ayush Saraf,Changil Kim,Liangyan Gui,Alexander Schwing,Johannes Kopf,Hung-Yu Tseng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AniGS 是一种用于 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) 重建场景的全局动画方法，能够为大型复杂户外场景添加自然的环境动态（如植被摆动），同时保持刚性结构不变。它通过时间条件的形变场建模运动，并结合预训练视频扩散模型与迭代式数据-模型更新策略，逐步扩展视角覆盖范围并优化动画质量。此外，引入视频到视频的精炼机制以限制运动仅作用于目标区域，避免静态区域出现异常运动。在五个真实大规模室外场景上的实验表明，该方法能生成高质量、逼真的新视角视频，显著提升场景沉浸感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 3D 动画技术多局限于物体中心或小范围区域，难以应用于大型、复杂且可导航的场景；而真实环境中的细微动态（如风吹树叶）对沉浸感至关重要，因此需要一种能全局、自然地为大规模 3D 重建场景添加环境动画的方法。

Method: AniGS 使用一个标准 3DGS 表示场景的几何与外观，并引入时间条件的形变场来建模动态。通过预训练视频扩散模型生成初始动画，采用迭代的‘渲染-精炼’策略不断更新相机固定的训练视频，逐步扩大视角覆盖。同时，设计了一种组合式视频到视频精炼方案，利用空间掩码控制运动分布，确保仅在期望区域产生动态。

Result: 在五个真实世界的大规模户外场景上验证，AniGS 能生成自然、分布均匀的环境动态，如植被晃动，且新视角视频保真度高、视觉连贯性强，显著增强了场景的沉浸感和真实感。

Conclusion: AniGS 成功实现了大规模 3DGS 场景的全局环境动画，突破了传统方法在范围和自然性上的局限，为高保真虚拟游览和沉浸式内容创作提供了新范式。

Abstract: Novel view rendering of large and complex reconstructed scenes is becoming increasingly photorealistic. However, most reconstructions remain static and lack the ambient motion that makes environments immersive. We present AniGS, a method for scene-level animation of 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) reconstructions that adds subtle, distributed dynamics, e.g., vegetation motion, while preserving rigid structures. Unlike existing 3D animation techniques which are limited to object-centric subjects or small regions, AniGS is designed for large, cluttered, navigable scenes. AniGS represents the scene with a canonical 3DGS and models motion using a time-conditioned deformation field. To animate the entire scene, we leverage a pretrained video diffusion model and introduce an iterative dataset--model update strategy that progressively expands viewpoint coverage and repeatedly updates camera-fixed training videos using a render-and-refine scheme. To prevent artifacts from unintended motion in static areas, we further introduce a composed video-to-video refinement scheme that restricts motion to desired regions. Experiments on five real-world, large-scale outdoor scenes demonstrate that AniGS produces natural ambient dynamics and high-quality novel view videos, enabling more immersive viewing experiences of reconstructed environments.

</details>


### [8] [Recti-Q: Feature-Space Rectification for Out-of-Distribution-Robust Quantized Perception in Edge Robotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18540)
*Hamidreza Yaghoubi Araghi,Parastoo Pilevar,Ming C. Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出Recti-Q，一种轻量级的特征空间校正框架，用于解决后训练量化（PTQ）在部署相关分布偏移下导致的鲁棒性下降问题。通过仅使用源数据训练一个小型分类头LoRA适配器，可在几乎不增加参数和计算开销的情况下，显著恢复因量化损失的鲁棒性，甚至超过原始浮点模型表现。该方法适用于CNN与Transformer架构，支持无教师训练，并具备低带宽OTA更新能力，适合部署于资源受限的机器人系统中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人感知系统依赖大型视觉骨干网络在资源受限的边缘设备上运行，后训练量化（PTQ）虽能保持干净分布内的准确率，但在实际部署中面对传感器噪声、恶劣天气等分布外变化时，鲁棒性严重下降，形成‘量化诱导的鲁棒性差距’。因此需要一种高效且可部署的解决方案来恢复量化后的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出Recti-Q，冻结量化后的骨干网络，仅训练一个小型分类头LoRA适配器，利用源数据进行无教师监督的微调。该方法无需额外教师模型，兼容CNN与Transformer，实现特征空间的轻量级校正。

Result: 在ImageNet-C和PACS等基准测试中，4比特PTQ模型经Recti-Q修复后，显著恢复了鲁棒性，在某些情况下达到或超过原始FP32模型性能；参数增加低于1%（最小仅6KB），保留超过99%的量化内存节省，计算开销极小，支持低带宽OTA远程更新。

Conclusion: Recti-Q有效缓解了量化带来的鲁棒性损失，是一种高效、通用、可部署的轻量级修复方案，特别适用于在不可预测物理环境中运行的机器人集群的持续更新与维护。

Abstract: Robotic perception pipelines increasingly rely on large vision backbones deployed on SWaP-constrained edge platforms, making post-training quantization (PTQ) attractive for real-time inference. However, while PTQ often preserves clean in-distribution accuracy, we show that it can substantially degrade reliability under deployment-relevant distribution shifts (e.g., sensor noise, severe weather, and novel operating environments), creating a Quantization-Induced Robustness Gap. Across foundational vision benchmarks (ImageNet-C and PACS), 4-bit PTQ models exhibit pronounced robustness degradation despite negligible ID accuracy loss. To address this, we propose Recti-Q, a lightweight feature-space rectification framework that freezes the quantized backbone and trains a small classifier-head LoRA adapter using only source data. Recti-Q is architecture-agnostic across CNNs and Transformers, supports efficient teacher-free training, and recovers a significant portion of the lost robustness, in some cases matching or exceeding FP32 performance. At less than 1% parameter overhead (as small as 6 KB), Recti-Q preserves over 99% of PTQ memory savings, adds negligible compute, and enables low-bandwidth Over-The-Air (OTA) resilience patching for deployed robotic fleets operating in unpredictable physical environments.

### [9] [Physics Closure Matters for Machine Olfaction: A Maxwell--Stefan Graph Solver for Identifiable Dynamic Gas Unmixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18544)
*Yue Shi,Liangxiu Han,Xin Zhang,Tam Sobeih*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出UnMixNet，一种基于多物理场约束的图神经网络，用于解决机器嗅觉中的气体解混问题。通过将Maxwell-Stefan多组分传输、竞争性吸附和非线性传感器响应等物理过程嵌入模型，实现了端到端的气体成分推断。该方法在空间图上离散化跨扩散，并保证局部可微与通量守恒，显著提升单气体识别、已知混合物解混及未知混合物泛化能力。实验验证表明，其推断浓度过程与真实浓度设定值高度一致，且模型学习到的动态物理指纹满足质量守恒、传输与读出闭合性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器嗅觉中的气体解混面临物理闭合性误设问题，即神经网络仅拟合传感器信号而未反映真实的物理过程。因此需要一种能融合多物理机制、保证过程一致性并具备强泛化能力的建模方法。

Method: 提出UnMixNet，将多组分扩散（Maxwell-Stefan PDE）、吸附动力学（ODE）与传感器响应（ODE）联合建模为耦合系统；通过空间图离散化跨扩散过程，构建局部可微、通量守恒的图神经结构，实现端到端的气体成分推断。

Result: 在SmellNet数据集上，UnMixNet在单气体识别、已知/未知混合物解混任务中表现更优；外部验证在UCI动态气体混合数据集上显示推断浓度与真实设定值高度一致；过程一致性分析表明模型学习到了符合物理闭合性的动态特征。

Conclusion: UnMixNet成功将多物理场先验知识融入神经网络，实现了物理闭合的气体解混，提升了模型的可解释性、泛化能力和对真实物理过程的逼近精度。

Abstract: Machine olfaction for gas unmixing is an underconstrained inverse problem in which gas compositions must be inferred from low-dimensional, delayed, and entangled sensor responses produced by interacting chemical transport, surface adsorption, and sensor transduction. One of the key obstacles is physics closure misspecification, where a neural network is designed to fit sensor traces rather than infer a physically closed olfactory process. In this work, we formulate gas unmixing as a multi-physics-constrained inverse problem governed by Maxwell--Stefan multicomponent transport PDEs, competitive adsorption ODEs, and nonlinear sensor transduction ODEs. Directly solving such a high-dimensional coupled system is computationally expensive and often numerically unstable. To this end, we propose UnMixNet, a physics-closed graph neural solver that embeds this multi-physics forward process into end-to-end gas unmixing. UnMixNet discretizes Maxwell--Stefan cross-diffusion on spatial graphs and formulates the multicomponent flux on each edge. This design enables local, differentiable, and flux-conservative inference for multicomponent cross-diffusion. Evaluations on SmellNet show improved single-odor recognition, seen-mixture unmixing, and unseen-mixture generalization. In addition, an external validation on UCI Dynamic Gas Mixtures shows that the inferred concentration process agrees with ground truth concentration set points under dynamic transitions. Process-consistency diagnostics further show that the proposed model learns transferable dynamic physical fingerprints that better satisfies transport, conservation, adsorption, and readout closure.

### [11] [Attention Without Grounding: Causal Evaluation of Visual Explanations in Medical VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18577)
*Binesh Sadanandan,Vahid Behzadan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究通过多重因果评估方法（包括与放射科医生标注框的重叠、归因质量在医生掩码内的分布、以及16×16图像块遮挡图）系统检验了医学视觉语言模型（VLM）在胸部X光片上的注意力热图和显著性图的可信度。研究涵盖多个MedGemma、LLaVA-RAD、Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct及CheXagent-2-3b模型，对比两个专门训练的CXRs分类器（DenseNet121、ResNet50）。结果表明：所有被测VLM均未同时满足‘注意力集中在影响预测的区域’且‘热图与真实病灶重合’这两个忠实性标准；部分模型虽使用图像但注意力与遮挡重要性负相关；另一些模型注意力虽正相关却几乎完全依赖文本。所有VLM的热图在定位真实解剖结构方面表现差，其归因质量远低于随机或偏移控制组。而两个专用分类器则通过所有评估指标，说明问题出在VLM热图本身而非评估方法。结论：当前VLM热图虽视觉上令人安心，但缺乏因果真实性，临床解释必须依赖受控的定位指标和因果扰动测试，而非仅凭视觉观察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学视觉语言模型（VLM）在胸部X光诊断中广泛应用，其注意力热图和显著性图常被用作可解释性工具。然而，这些热图是否真正反映模型决策所依据的真实图像证据尚未经过严格的因果验证。现有方法多依赖视觉直观判断，缺乏对热图忠实性的量化评估，可能导致误导性解释。因此，亟需一种基于因果扰动和真实标注的系统性审计框架来评估VLM输出的可信度。

Method: 采用三种因果评估策略：(1) 与放射科医生标注边界框的重叠分析；(2) 在放射科医生掩码内计算归因质量（attribution mass）；(3) 使用16×16像素块遮挡生成扰动图，记录哪些区域被隐藏时会改变预测结果。评估对象包括三种MedGemma-4B变体、跨家族探针（LLaVA-RAD、Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct）、CheXagent-2-3b，并以两个专用于胸部X光的分类器（DenseNet121、ResNet50）作为正向对照。通过统计相关性（如皮尔逊相关系数）、置信区间（95% bootstrap CI）和归因质量占比进行分析。

Result: 所有评估的VLM均未同时满足注意力集中于关键区域且热图与实际病变位置一致的双重标准。部分模型（如MedGemma、Qwen3-VL）虽利用图像信息，但注意力与遮挡重要性呈负相关（rho < 0，95% CI低于零）；另一些模型（如LLaVA-RAD）注意力与遮挡重要性正相关，但模型几乎为纯文本驱动（99.1%文本一致性，近零因果质量），相关性仅为两个微弱信号间的虚假关联。所有模型在定位真实解剖结构方面表现不佳：与放射科医生标注的重叠始终低于随机或偏移控制组；归因质量最多仅占22%在医生掩码内。相比之下，两个专用分类器在所有指标上均表现优异，证明问题并非出在评估方法，而是特定于VLM热图的不可靠性。

Conclusion: 当前医学视觉语言模型的注意力热图和显著性图虽在视觉上具有说服力，但缺乏因果真实性。它们不能可靠地揭示模型决策所依赖的真实图像证据。临床应用中的可解释性必须建立在严格的定位指标和因果扰动实验基础上，而非仅依赖视觉检查。未来模型设计应强化图像感知能力并引入可验证的可解释性机制。

Abstract: Attention and saliency heatmaps are widely used to explain medical Vision-Language Model (VLM) outputs on chest X-rays, yet whether they truly highlight the image evidence driving predictions has not been causally tested. We audit faithfulness via overlap with radiologist bounding boxes on PadChest (n=637), attribution mass within radiologist masks on CheXlocalize (n=643), and 16x16 patch-occlusion maps that record which regions, when hidden, change the answer. We study three MedGemma-4B variants, cross-family probes on LLaVA-RAD and Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct, and the specialist CheXagent-2-3b, with two CXR-trained classifiers (DenseNet121, ResNet50) as positive controls. A heatmap is faithful only if the model uses the image and attention concentrates on regions whose occlusion alters the prediction. No evaluated VLM meets both criteria. MedGemma and Qwen3-VL use the image, but attention anti-correlates with patch-occlusion importance (rho < 0 with 95% bootstrap CIs below zero). LLaVA-RAD's attention correlates positively, but the model is almost text-only (99.1% text-only agreement, near-zero causal mass), so correlation ties two near-zero signals. Attention also misses annotated anatomy: overlap with true regions never beats shifted or random controls, and no method places more than 22% of its mass inside radiologist masks. The two CXR classifiers pass all metrics, indicating the failure is specific to VLM heatmaps, not the evaluation. These heatmaps are visually reassuring but not faithful; clinical explanations require controlled localization metrics and causal perturbation, not visual inspection alone.

### [12] [Norm or Direction? Decoding Vision Mambas for High-Resolution Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18625)
*Jin Yu,Juyoun Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究通过交叉模型中心核对齐（CKA）分析，比较了Vision Mamba（VMamba）与MambaOut在视觉表征上的差异。发现VMamba的最终阶段块形成与前级块及MambaOut显著不同的表示；其高范数特征主要集中在背景区域，与Grad-CAM不一致，但判别性信息更多体现在特征方向上；而MambaOut则依赖前景中高范数的稀疏关键令牌。在密集预测任务如语义分割中，VMamba因更均匀地分布语义支持而表现更优。结论指出，令牌的幅度与方向结构是提升视觉骨干网络性能的关键维度，尤其在密集监督下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究VMamba与MambaOut在视觉表征层面是否存在本质差异，验证SSMs在视觉任务中的必要性，并理解不同编码策略对密集预测任务的影响。

Method: 采用跨模型中心核对齐（CKA）分析表征相似性，对空间令牌进行幅度与方向分解，结合Grad-CAM可视化对比判别性信息分布，并在图像分类与语义分割任务中评估模型性能。

Result: VMamba的最终块产生与MambaOut显著不同的表示，其判别性信息主要存在于令牌方向而非幅度，且在高分辨率任务和全微调语义分割中持续优于MambaOut；MambaOut依赖稀疏主导令牌，在大规模令牌下稳定性下降。

Conclusion: VMamba在密集预测任务中的优势源于其在令牌幅度与方向上的独特组织方式，而非单纯依赖SSM机制或序列长度。令牌的幅度与方向结构是设计高效视觉骨干的重要依据，尤其适用于密集监督场景。

Abstract: Vision Mamba models replace quadratic self-attention with linear complexity selective state space models (SSMs), emerging as efficient visual backbones. However, MambaOut demonstrates that a Gated CNN block can match or exceed VMamba on image classification, questioning the necessity of SSMs for vision. This raises a fundamental question: do VMamba and MambaOut encode visual information differently at the representation level? To investigate, we apply cross model centered kernel alignment (CKA) analysis and find that VMamba's final stage blocks form representations distinctly different from both MambaOut and its own preceding blocks. We therefore focus on the final block features, decomposing each spatial token into magnitude and direction. MambaOut concentrates class-discriminative information in high-norm foreground tokens that align with Grad-CAM attribution. VMamba, by contrast, produces high-norm tokens predominantly in background regions, misaligned with Grad-CAM, yet preserves discriminative signals primarily in token directions. These observations reveal that the two models rely on different encoding strategies. We connect this difference to high-resolution classification and semantic segmentation. VMamba distributes logit support broadly across object regions, whereas MambaOut relies on sparse dominant tokens, a strategy that becomes less stable as token counts grow. Under full fine-tuning for segmentation, VMamba consistently outperforms MambaOut. These results suggest that VMamba's advantage in dense prediction stems not merely from the SSM mechanism or sequence length, but from how semantic evidence is organized across token magnitude, direction. Ultimately, we conclude that token magnitude and directional structure serve as critical axes for improving visual backbones, particularly under dense supervision.

### [14] [Deep Learning Estimation of Sex, Age, Height, and Weight from CT-derived Digitally Reconstructed Radiographs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18638)
*Tomohiro Kikuchi,Kohei Yamamoto,Yukihiro Nomura,Yosuke Yamagishi,Takeharu Yoshikawa,Toshiaki Akashi,Jun Kamohara,Hiroyuki Fujii,Harushi Mori*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究开发并验证了一种深度学习集成模型，用于从诊断CT生成的冠状面数字化重建放射图像（DRRs）中估计成人的性别、年龄、身高和体重。研究使用了来自日本九家机构的128,621例成人CT检查数据，采用三种多任务模型（ConvNeXt-Base、ViT-Base/16、MaxViT-Base）在冠状面DRRs上进行微调，并通过加权平均融合。模型在测试集上表现出优异性能：性别分类准确率高达0.997，年龄、身高和体重的平均绝对误差（MAE）分别为3.57年、2.59厘米和3.40公斤。在覆盖胸至盆腔范围的检查中，性能更优，各项误差进一步降低。基于估算身高体重计算的体表面积（BSA）能准确反映心脏和肝脏体积随年龄的变化趋势。在非日本数据集上，身高误差有所上升，但通过持续微调可改善。结论表明，该集成模型可高效、准确地从CT-D RR中估计人体基本参数，且在解剖覆盖范围更广时表现更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在缺乏直接人体测量数据的情况下难以准确估计个体的基本生理参数（如性别、年龄、身高、体重）。而临床常规的CT扫描常伴随数字化重建放射图像（DRRs），这些图像蕴含丰富的解剖信息，具备作为输入特征进行参数估计的潜力。因此，亟需一种基于影像的自动化、高精度估计方法，以支持临床决策、流行病学研究及个性化医疗。

Method: 研究采用三类预训练多任务深度学习模型（ConvNeXt-Base、ViT-Base/16、MaxViT-Base）对冠状面数字化重建放射图像（DRRs）进行微调。模型通过加权平均方式集成，形成一个深度学习集成系统。数据按机构划分：训练集（114,147例，7家机构）、调参集（4,305例，1家机构）、测试集（10,169例，1家机构）。评估指标包括性别分类准确率与年龄、身高、体重的平均绝对误差（MAE）。此外，还通过比较真实值与估计值计算的体表面积（BSA）所反映的心脏和肝脏体积趋势，验证估计结果的生物学合理性。模型泛化能力在两个非日本数据集上进行了评估，并通过持续微调优化跨人群表现。

Result: 在测试集中，性别分类准确率达到0.997（95% CI: 0.996–0.998），年龄、身高、体重的平均绝对误差（MAE）分别为3.57年（3.51–3.63）、2.59厘米（2.54–2.64）、3.40公斤（3.34–3.47）。当图像覆盖范围从胸部至盆腔时，性能显著提升：性别分类准确率为1.000，各参数的MAE分别降至3.15年、2.28厘米、3.18公斤。基于估计值计算的体表面积（BSA）能够重现真实值下观察到的心脏和肝脏体积随年龄变化的趋势，说明估计结果具有良好的生物学一致性。在非日本数据集上，身高估计误差略有增加，但通过额外微调可有效缓解。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建并验证了一个基于深度学习集成的模型，能够从诊断性CT生成的冠状面数字化重建放射图像（DRRs）中高精度估计成人的性别、年龄、身高和体重。模型在广泛解剖覆盖的图像上表现尤为出色，且在跨人群场景中展现出良好泛化潜力。该方法为无直接测量数据的临床环境提供了一种可靠、自动化的人体参数估计工具，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Purpose: To develop and validate a deep learning ensemble for estimating adult sex, age, height, and weight from coronal digitally reconstructed radiographs (DRRs) generated from diagnostic CT. Materials and Methods: This retrospective study included 128,621 CT examinations from 80,004 adults at nine institutions in Japan. Three multitask models-ConvNeXt-Base, ViT-Base/16, and MaxViT-Base-were fine-tuned using coronal DRRs and combined by weighted averaging. Data were split by institution into training (114,147 examinations; seven institutions), tuning (4,305; one institution), and test (10,169; one institution) sets; generalizability was assessed on two non-Japanese datasets. Accuracy and mean absolute error (MAE) were used to evaluate sex classification and age, height, and weight regression, respectively. Body surface area (BSA)-corrected heart and liver volume trends were compared using true versus estimated height and weight. Results: In the test set (median age, 69.9 years; 4,899 of 10,169 [48.2%] male), overall sex-classification accuracy was 0.997 (95% CI, 0.996-0.998), and MAEs were 3.57 years (3.51-3.63), 2.59 cm (2.54-2.64), and 3.40 kg (3.34-3.47) for age, height, and weight, respectively. In examinations covering the chest through pelvis, accuracy was 1.000, and MAEs were 3.15 years, 2.28 cm, and 3.18 kg, respectively. BSA calculated from estimated values reproduced age-related heart and liver volume trends obtained using true values. On non-Japanese datasets, height error increased but was reduced by continued fine-tuning. Conclusion: The ensemble estimated adult sex, age, height, and weight from CT-derived DRRs, with generally lower errors in examinations with broader anatomical coverage.

</details>


### [15] [Fluid-SDF: Ultra-Lightweight and Editable Implicit Shape Representation via Differentiable Primitives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18646)
*Pradyumna Sripada,Chinmay Nadgir,Ksheer Agrawal,Krishna Kanth Kodanganti*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Fluid-SDF 是一种高度压缩的可微分构造实体几何（CSG）框架，使用平滑最小函数混合显式几何原语来建模形状。它用参数化原语引擎替代传统多层感知机（MLP），以少于100个参数重建复杂非凸拓扑，性能媲美或优于标准神经基线，并具备对高频噪声的强鲁棒性。其显式参数空间支持无需重新训练的零样本用户编辑，适用于移动AI、增强现实和资源受限嵌入式环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决隐式神经表示（INRs）在可编辑性、抗噪性和参数量方面的局限，尤其是在边缘设备部署中的挑战。

Method: 采用参数化几何原语结合平滑最小函数构建形状，通过显式几何结构替代神经网络，实现高效压缩与可解释性。

Result: Fluid-SDF 仅需不到100个参数即可达到与神经基线相当或更好的交并比（mIoU），对高频率噪声具有显著鲁棒性，支持零样本用户编辑且无需梯度更新。

Conclusion: Fluid-SDF 提供了一种高效、可解释、可编辑且适合边缘部署的2D形状建模新范式，为移动AI和嵌入式系统提供了理想解决方案。

Abstract: Implicit Neural Representations (INRs) have become the standard for continuous 2D shape modeling, but they suffer from black-box uneditability, vulnerability to noise, and high parameter counts that severely hinder deployment on edge devices. We introduce Fluid-SDF, a highly compressed, differentiable Constructive Solid Geometry (CSG) framework that models shapes using explicit geometric primitives blended via a smooth minimum function. By replacing traditional multi-layer perceptrons (MLPs) with a parameterized primitive engine, Fluid-SDF reconstructs complex, non-convex topologies using strictly under 100 parameters, achieving comparable or superior intersection-over-union (mIoU) to standard neural baselines. Furthermore, we demonstrate that Fluid-SDF acts as a powerful geometric prior, inherently resisting high-frequency dataset noise where capacity-matched neural networks catastrophically overfit. Finally, unlike standard INRs, Fluid-SDF's explicit parameter space allows for direct, zero-shot user editing of local and global shape features without retraining. By bypassing expensive on-device gradient updates entirely, Fluid-SDF is uniquely suited for mobile AI, augmented reality, and resource-constrained embedded environments

### [16] [DeforM: Reasoning-Guided Physics-Aware Video Generation via Spatial-Temporal Masking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18664)
*Yunyi Li,Yu Qiao,Yaohui Wang,Xinyuan Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出DeforM框架，通过引入视觉语言模型（VLM）引导的物理推理模块，实现对视频生成中物理关键区域的精准定位，从而提升复杂形变动态的生成质量。该方法在无需训练的DeforM-Free和基于训练的DeforM-Injection两种策略下均表现出色，在视觉真实性和物理一致性方面优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成模型虽然视觉质量高，但在生成物理感知视频时表现不佳，尤其在处理复杂形变动态时，由于缺乏对动态区域的物理推理能力，导致模型注意力被无关区域分散，影响生成效果。

Method: 提出DeforM框架，包含一个VLM引导的物理推理模块DeforM-Reason，用于识别目标物体并生成时空掩码；设计两种物理引导策略：DeforM-Free（无需训练）和DeforM-Injection（基于训练），以指导模型聚焦于物理关键区域。

Result: 实验结果表明，DeforM显著提升了生成视频在形变场景中的真实感，相较于基线模型，在视觉质量和物理一致性方面均有明显优势。

Conclusion: DeforM通过引入物理推理机制有效引导模型关注物理关键区域，解决了复杂形变视频生成中的注意力稀释问题，为高质量、物理一致的视频生成提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Video generation models achieve high visual quality but often struggle to generate physics-aware videos. Unlike rigid-body motion, which can be described by explicit trajectories or formulas, complex deformation dynamics remain challenging to synthesize. We observe that a lack of physical reasoning for localizing dynamic areas allows irrelevant regions to dilute the model's attention, leading to generation failure. In this paper, we propose DeforM, a reasoning-guided image-to-video generation framework that directs the model's focus toward physics-critical regions. To reason about and localize these critical regions, we introduce a VLM-guided physical reasoning module, DeforM-Reason, to identify target objects and generate spatial-temporal masks. For physical guidance, we develop two alternative strategies: DeforM-Free for training-free mechanism analysis and DeforM-Injection as a powerful training-based generator. Experimental results demonstrate that DeforM improves the realism of generated deformation scenarios, outperforming baseline models in both visual quality and physical consistency.

### [17] [MissingBench-Verified: Probing Vision-Language Models' Inability to Detect Missing Object Parts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18673)
*Wenqi Marshall Guo,Qingyun Qian,Shiyu Zhou,Guoping Luo,Shan Du*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出MissingBench-Verified基准，评估视觉语言模型在识别物体缺失关键部件时的失败情况。实验发现十种主流模型均存在显著且持续的识别失败，即使有外部工具证据反驳其视觉判断。尽管尝试了工具辅助验证、自主推理、延长推理时间及微调等方法，改进效果微乎其微，表明当前提示或后处理技术无法解决此问题。研究揭示了现有VLM在检测与监控任务中的根本缺陷，强调需从架构或训练层面进行干预以突破内在预期偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在面对物体缺失关键部分时容易产生幻觉，而这类场景在真实世界中具有实际意义，但因训练数据稀缺和知识偏见导致模型表现不佳。亟需系统性评估此类失败模式，并探索有效缓解手段。

Method: 构建MissingBench-Verified基准，针对物体缺失部件的识别任务，测试十种主流视觉语言模型的表现；引入图像处理工具（如裁剪、对比度调整）评估工具辅助下的模型能力；对比多种缓解策略（工具辅助、自主推理、长推理、微调）的效果。

Result: 所有模型在缺失部件识别任务中均表现出显著失败率，且即使有外部工具证据支持，仍难以纠正错误判断；现有缓解策略改善效果极小，无法有效提升模型性能。

Conclusion: 当前视觉语言模型在面对与内部预期矛盾的视觉证据时，缺乏自我修正能力，暴露出根本性缺陷。仅靠提示工程或后处理无法解决该问题，必须通过架构设计或训练机制的根本性改进来实现可靠感知与判断。

Abstract: Vision Language Models (VLMs) are well known for hallucinating non-existent objects in images. Objects with missing parts present a unique challenge for VLMs, stemming from both real-world knowledge bias and the scarcity of such images in training data. We present MissingBench-Verified, a benchmark designed to evaluate a specific and practically relevant scenario: when vision-language models fail to recognize that an essential component of an object has been removed. Across ten leading models, we observe consistent and significant failure rates that persist even when external tool evidence explicitly contradicts the model's visual perception. We further ask whether granting models access to image processing tools (e.g., cropping, contrast adjustment) enables autonomous inspection to resolve these failures. We find that existing mitigation strategies, including tool-assisted verification, autonomous visual reasoning, longer reasoning durations, and fine-tuning on an easier dataset, provide negligible improvement, indicating that this failure mode cannot be addressed through current prompting or post-hoc correction techniques. Our findings highlight a fundamental limitation of current VLM for inspection and monitoring tasks and underscore the need for architectural or training-level interventions that enable models to override internal expectations when confronted with contradictory evidence.

*Mohammad Ali Dadrast,Hamid Usefi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了深度学习模型在跨机构乳腺MRI肿瘤分类中的表现，发现即使在内部数据集上表现优异，模型在外部独立数据集上仍可能因领域偏移和数据来源偏差而失败。通过在训练中混合来自不同数据源的样本，并控制患者级分割和数据泄露，显著提升了模型在MAMA-MIA多中心数据集上的准确率与F1分数，表明控制数据来源偏差对可靠分类至关重要。

Method: 采用EfficientNet-B3和WaveViT-Small模型，在杜克大学乳腺癌MRI与fastMRI数据集上训练，评估仅在独立的多中心MAMA-MIA数据集上进行。通过构建混合训练集（每类包含来自杜克与fastMRI的样本），同时保持患者级分割、增强策略与数据泄露控制，对比模型性能。

Conclusion: 控制数据来源偏差对于实现可靠的乳腺MRI肿瘤分类至关重要，混合训练策略可有效缓解跨机构泛化问题。

Abstract: Breast MRI is highly sensitive for detecting breast tumors, but exams contain many slices and require substantial reading time. Deep learning models often perform well on internal splits but can fail across institutions because of domain shift and dataset-origin bias. We study this failure mode for binary breast MRI tumor classification. EfficientNet-B3 and WaveViT-Small are trained using Duke Breast Cancer MRI and fastMRI, and evaluated only on the independent multi-center MAMA-MIA cohort. In a deliberately confounded setup, where label is perfectly correlated with dataset origin, external accuracy is near chance (0.5048--0.5265), despite very high recall. We then construct a mixed training set in which each class contains samples from both Duke and fastMRI, while preserving patient-level splitting, augmentation, and leakage controls. On MAMA-MIA, dataset mixing improves accuracy/F1 to 0.8463/0.8625 for WaveViT-Small and 0.8884/0.8994 for EfficientNet-B3. These results show that controlling dataset-origin bias is important for reliable breast MRI classification.

### [19] [Dual-Edged Homogeneous-Modality Similarity: Towards Visible-Infrared Modality-Incomplete Person Re-Identification with Modality Adaptive Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18688)
*Xin Xu,Shuhao Zhan,Wei Liu,Zheng Wang,Kui Jiang,Chia-Wen Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对可见光-红外行人重识别（VI-ReID）在开放世界场景下的可信性挑战，提出模态不完整重识别（VIMI-ReID）任务，并构建了SYSU-VIMI和RegDB-VIMI基准。针对同模态相似性高、模态不确定性干扰及未知模态组合导致的性能下降问题，提出模态自适应匹配变压器（MAMT），通过差异变换模块（DTM）和共享变换模块（STM）分别提取模态特异性与共享特征，并利用模态自适应匹配模块（MAM）动态融合特征以实现稳定匹配。实验验证了MAMT在复杂多模态条件下的有效性与适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VI-ReID方法基于异构模态检索范式，在开放世界场景下面临同模态相似性高、模态不确定性干扰及未知模态组合导致的匹配冲突、干扰和鲁棒性下降问题，难以满足可靠、一致和动态适应的可信视觉识别需求。

Method: 提出模态自适应匹配变压器（MAMT），包含差异变换模块（DTM）用于增强模态特异性特征的判别能力，共享变换模块（STM）提取模态共享特征，以及模态自适应匹配模块（MAM）根据查询与图库的模态关系动态融合特征，实现对任意和不确定模态条件的稳定匹配。

Result: 在新构建的SYSU-VIMI和RegDB-VIMI基准上，MAMT显著优于现有VI-ReID方法，表现出更强的性能与适应性，尤其在复杂多模态组合条件下表现优异。

Conclusion: 本文通过定义VIMI-ReID任务并提出MAMT模型，有效应对开放世界中模态不完整带来的可信性挑战，为未来多模态行人重识别提供了更可靠、灵活且自适应的解决方案。

Abstract: Visible-Infrared Person Re-Identification (VI-ReID) operates under a closed-world assumption, where queries and galleries are from heterogeneous modalities. However, in open-world scenarios, both sets are likely to contain homogeneous and heterogeneous modality images. A query may consist of visible-only, infrared-only, or mixed-modality images, while galleries present multi-modal images over long-term collection. Under these conditions, VI-ReID methods, built on a heterogeneous-modality retrieval paradigm, suffer from three trustworthiness challenges: matching conflicts due to high homogeneous-modality similarity, interference from modality uncertainty, and robustness degradation induced by unknown modality combinations. They fail to meet the requirements of trustworthy visual recognition in reliability, consistency, and dynamic adaptability. To address these challenges, we formalize the Visible-Infrared Modality-Incomplete Re-Identification (VIMI-ReID) task. We reorganize existing datasets to construct the SYSU-VIMI and RegDB-VIMI benchmarks. The unpredictable modality combinations and inherent similarity of homogeneous-modality samples in VIMI-ReID cause a significant performance drop in existing VI-ReID methods. We propose the Modality Adaptive Matching Transformer (MAMT). It employs a Divergence Transformer Module (DTM) and a Shared Transformer Module (STM) to extract modality-specific and modality-shared features, respectively. Guided by a divergence loss, the DTM enriches modality-specific features with modality-style information to enhance discriminability within the same modality. A Modality Adaptive Matching Module (MAM) dynamically fuses features according to the query-gallery modality relationship, enabling stable matching under arbitrary and uncertain modality conditions. Extensive experiments on the VIMI benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness and adaptability of MAMT.

### [20] [Attributes Should Come from Images, Not Class Names: Distribution-Conditioned Attribute Selection for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18695)
*Gautam Rajendrakumar Gare,Jia Shi,Zhiqiu Lin,Deepak Pathak,John Galeotti,Deva Ramanan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需类别名称的可解释零样本分类方法，通过在CLIP嵌入空间中从图像数据中选择高得分属性作为提示，显著提升分类性能。相比LLM生成的描述符（准确率仅15.5%），新方法在ImageNet上达到23.8%准确率，并在多个分布偏移数据集上保持优势。该方法高效（每类只需一张图，不到一分钟完成），且不依赖可学习的软提示，具备可读性，可用来描述数据分布变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本分类方法依赖大语言模型（LLM）生成类别描述，但这些描述往往受标签影响而非真实视觉特征，导致在数据分布变化时表现严重下降。例如，LLM认为草莓是红色的，但在线稿图像中则无颜色信息，造成误导。因此需要更忠实于图像数据的提示生成机制。

Method: 从目标图像集合中提取属性：在CLIP联合嵌入空间中对大量候选属性进行评分，选取每类得分最高的属性作为提示；不使用类别名称，也不依赖LLM生成描述，而是基于真实图像特征选择最相关属性。

Result: 所选属性提示在ImageNet上实现23.8%准确率，远超LLM描述符的15.5%；在四个分布偏移的ImageNet变体上均表现更优；仅需一张图像/类，运行时间不足一分钟，优于需14小时的CoOp方法，且无需学习参数。

Conclusion: 基于图像数据自动选择的属性提示不仅提升了零样本分类性能，还提供了可读的数据摘要，可用于描述和理解分布偏移现象，是一种高效、透明且可解释的零样本分类新范式。

Abstract: A popular route to interpretable zero-shot classification asks a large language model (LLM) to describe each class name and prompts CLIP with the resulting descriptors. We show that these descriptors carry little visual evidence of their own: removing the class name from the prompt collapses ImageNet accuracy from 59.5% to 15.5%. The diagnosis is that the descriptors are conditioned on the label rather than on the images, so they describe the concept in general and mislead exactly when the data shifts; an LLM insists that strawberries are red, but every strawberry in ImageNet-Sketch is a colorless line drawing. We therefore select attributes from the target image collection instead: we score a large attribute pool against the images in CLIP's joint embedding space and keep the top-scoring attributes per class. Selected this way, class-name-free attribute prompts reach 23.8% on ImageNet (against 15.5% for LLM descriptors), the gain holds on four shifted ImageNet variants, and reselecting from the LLM's own pool isolates the selection mechanism as the cause. With one image per class, the selected attributes outperform the prompt-tuning method CoOp by 3 points while fitting in under a minute instead of 14 hours, with no learned soft prompt to obscure the decision. Because the attribute set is chosen by the data, it doubles as a readable summary of a dataset, which we use to describe distribution shift in words.

</details>


### [21] [Decoupled Pipeline with Proposal Reranking and Score Fusion for Positive-Unlabeled Marine Species Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18700)
*Robert James Brock,Sebastian Maximilian Krupa,Jason Kahei Tam*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DS@GT ARC's multi-stage system for FathomNetCLEF 2026 uses a frozen Megalodon YOLOv8x detector for class-agnostic proposals, combines global and tiled inference with edge filtering, classifies proposals with a LoRA-finetuned DINOv3 ViT-H classifier, and ranks predictions via weighted geometric fusion. The approach achieved 12th place out of 102 teams. A variant with a TTN-inspired validity head improved public and proxy performance but slightly hurt private leaderboard results. Key insights: train-derived metrics are unreliable; proxy datasets and leaderboard feedback are crucial for model selection; focus on proposal recall, filtering, and ranking over detector fine-tuning or noisy pseudo-label training.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The competition presents challenges due to sparse training labels and out-of-distribution test data, making traditional annotation and model evaluation methods ineffective. The goal is to develop robust underwater object detection and fine-grained species classification under positive-unlabeled learning with limited labeled data and domain shift.

Method: A multi-stage pipeline: (1) use a frozen Megalodon YOLOv8x as a class-agnostic proposal generator; (2) apply global and tiled inference with tile-edge filtering to handle large images; (3) classify expanded proposal crops using a LoRA-finetuned DINOv3 ViT-H; (4) rank predictions via weighted geometric fusion of detector and classifier confidence. A secondary variant adds a TTN-inspired validity head for reranking.

Result: The final model placed 12th out of 102 teams. The variant with the validity head improved public and proxy evaluation performance but reduced private leaderboard performance. Experiments confirmed that proxy validation and leaderboard feedback are more reliable than internal train-validation metrics.

Conclusion: For out-of-distribution, low-label settings like FathomNetCLEF 2026, model selection should rely on proxy datasets and real leaderboard feedback rather than train-derived metrics. Optimizing proposal recall, careful filtering, and downstream ranking yield better results than detector fine-tuning or training on noisy pseudo-labels.

Abstract: The FathomNetCLEF 2026 competition combines underwater object detection and fine-grained marine species classification under a positive-unlabeled evaluation setting. The provided training labels are sparse, while the hidden test set is out-of-distribution relative to the training imagery, creating both annotation incompleteness and source-shift challenges. We describe DS@GT ARC's multi-stage system developed for this setting while keeping model training restricted to the data provided by the competition. The final private-leaderboard model uses a frozen Megalodon YOLOv8x detector as a class-agnostic proposal generator, combines global and tiled inference with tile-edge filtering, classifies expanded proposal crops with a LoRA-finetuned DINOv3 ViT-H classifier, and ranks predictions using weighted geometric fusion of detector and classifier confidence. This system placed 12th out of 102 teams. A closely related variant added a locally trained TTN-inspired validity head as a light reranking signal, improving public-leaderboard and proxy-evaluation performance but slightly reducing private-leaderboard performance. Across experiments, the strongest lesson was that train-derived validation and detector-only metrics were not reliable enough for model selection. Instead, we used proxy datasets only for validation and comparison, and combined those signals with leaderboard feedback and targeted ablations. These experiments showed that reserving proposal recall, avoiding over-aggressive filtering, and improving downstream ranking were more effective than fine-tuning the detector or directly training on noisy pseudo-labels. Code: https://github.com/dsgt-arc/fathomnetclef-2026.

</details>


### [22] [Generative World Renderer at the Speed of Play](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18703)

Method: 将 AlayaRenderer 重构为多步自回归流式生成模型，采用轻量级蒸馏编码器进行潜空间编码与帧重建，保留教师模型的 G-buffer 输入和文本提示接口，支持连续长序列输入流的高效处理。

Abstract: Generative world renderer AlayaRenderer receives structured world states exported from physics engines and synthesizes RGB frames. Unlike models that generate frames from text/control-hints prompts, AlayaRenderer preserves scene structure without altering the underlying world dynamics. This demonstrates an alternative path toward interactive world modeling and user-controllable play. However, the original AlayaRenderer is too computationally expensive for real-time deployment. This technical report introduces AlayaRenderer-Flash, a real-time-oriented generative forward world renderer that pushes AlayaRenderer from 0.56 FPS to 31.54 FPS, reaching the speed of play. AlayaRenderer-Flash reformulates the original renderer as a few-step autoregressive streaming model and introduces lightweight distilled codecs for efficient latent encoding and frame reconstruction. It retains the teacher model's G-buffer and text-prompt interfaces while enabling continuous rendering over input streams of unbounded length. We evaluate AlayaRenderer-Flash on G-buffer streams across content preservation, temporal consistency, cross-window stability, prompt controllability, and runtime efficiency. Our results show that AlayaRenderer-Flash substantially reduces inference cost while preserving the core rendering capabilities of the teacher model. By integrating AlayaRenderer-Flash with a physics engine, we build a fully playable generative world running at 30 FPS.

### [23] [Continual Video-MLLM Adaptation over Evolving Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18716)
*Rui Cheng,Meixing Shi,Yuxiang Cai,Jingcai Guo,Jianwei Yin,Zhi Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为分布感知专家路由（DAER）的参数高效框架，用于在连续演变的视频领域中持续适应视频多模态大语言模型（Video-MLLM）。该方法通过保持预训练模型冻结并引入领域隔离的轻量级专家，避免了跨领域干扰和灾难性遗忘。利用最大均值差异（MMD）进行细粒度的领域内专家匹配，并设计了判别性子空间中的领域间路由机制以应对推理时任务身份缺失问题。此外，采用自适应领域合并与两阶段优化策略提升参数可扩展性和专家特化稳定性。在十个不同视频问答数据集构建的增量领域基准上验证，DAER 在两个强基线模型上均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续学习方法依赖共享适应空间，容易导致跨领域干扰和灾难性遗忘；而真实场景下的视频数据来自异构且持续演进的领域，需要模型在不丢失已有知识的前提下不断学习新领域知识。因此，亟需一种能有效解耦通用多模态知识与特定领域知识、支持高效、稳定、可扩展持续学习的框架。

Method: 提出分布感知专家路由（DAER），包含：1）领域隔离的轻量级专家模块，保持预训练视频-多模态大模型主干冻结；2）基于最大均值差异（MMD）的领域内分布感知路由，实现输入与专家原型库的细粒度匹配；3）判别性子空间中的领域间路由机制，用于无任务标识情况下的鲁棒领域识别；4）自适应领域合并策略以控制参数增长；5）两阶段优化策略稳定专家特化过程。

Result: 在由十个不同视频问答数据集构成的领域增量基准上评估，DAER 在两个主流视频-多模态大语言模型（Video-MLLM）主干上均显著优于现有持续学习方法，在多个指标上实现了性能提升，证明了其有效性、鲁棒性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: DAER 通过解耦通用知识与领域知识、引入分布感知路由与动态管理机制，成功实现了对视频-多模态大语言模型在持续演化领域的高效适应，为复杂现实场景下的视频理解提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: Video multimodal large language models have shown strong capability in video understanding, yet their adaptation to sequentially evolving domains remains underexplored. In real-world deployments, video data often arrives continuously from heterogeneous domains, requiring the model to acquire new domain-specific knowledge without overwriting previously learned capabilities. Existing continual learning methods typically rely on shared adaptation spaces, which can induce severe cross-domain interference and catastrophic forgetting. We propose Distribution-Aware Expert Routing, a parameter-efficient framework for continual Video-MLLM adaptation over evolving domains. DAER maintains domain-isolated lightweight experts while keeping the pretrained Video-MLLM backbone frozen, thereby decoupling domain-specific adaptation from the general multimodal knowledge of the pretrained model. To enable fine-grained specialization, we introduce an intra-domain distribution-aware routing mechanism that matches each input to expert-level prototype reservoirs using MMD. To address the absence of task identities at inference time, we further propose an inter-domain routing mechanism that performs prototype matching in a discriminative subspace for robust domain identification. In addition, we introduce adaptive domain merging to improve parameter scalability and adopt a two-stage optimization strategy to stabilize expert specialization during continual learning. We evaluate DAER by curating a domain-incremental benchmark built from ten VidQA datasets covering diverse visual environments and reasoning demands. Experiments on two strong Video-MLLM backbones show that DAER consistently outperforms prior methods.

### [26] [Posterior Samplings are Missing Modalities Generators for Medical Image Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18763)

Abstract: Magnetic resonance imaging comes in various modality contrasts that provide complementary anatomical and pathological information. Complete multimodal acquisitions are often unavailable due to time and protocol constraints. This leads to real-world datasets with missing modalities, where conventional medical image translation methods are typically limited to fixed source-target settings or require retraining for each observed source-target pair. We propose a unified framework that formulates missing-modality generation as a linear inverse problem under a joint distribution and solves it via posterior sampling with a flow matching model. By learning a joint prior over the complete modality set, our method can reconstruct arbitrary missing modalities at inference time by guiding the sampling trajectory to enforce measurement consistency with observed modalities. We further mitigate inter-modality error propagation in multi-target generation by adopting a many-to-one sampling strategy. Experiments on BraTS and IXI datasets show that our method achieves the best performance over baselines across most missing-modality scenarios. ### [28] [Cross-Modal UAV Object Tracking: State-Aware Representation Learning and A Unified Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18768)
*Yun Xiao,Zhihong Hong,Jiandong Jin,Chenglong Li,Jin Tang,Amir Hussain*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为SARLA的新型状态感知表示学习方法，用于解决无人机在可见光与热红外模态切换时因外观和位置突变导致的跟踪难题。通过设计模态状态感知表示模块（MSARM）和空间状态感知表示模块（SSARM），分别处理跨模态差异和帧间空间变化，并引入空间位移预测损失以增强鲁棒性。同时构建了大规模基准数据集CM-UOT，包含超过671,000帧的1079个跨模态视频序列。实验表明，SARLA在20种先进跟踪方法中表现卓越。代码、数据集与评估协议已公开。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机目标跟踪系统受限于通信带宽、计算资源和功耗，常采用单模态工作并频繁切换模态，导致外观和位置发生显著突变，对跟踪算法造成严重挑战。因此亟需一种能适应模态切换带来的不连续性的鲁棒跟踪方法。

Method: 提出SARLA框架，包含两个核心模块：模态状态感知表示模块（MSARM）用于学习跨模态外观相关性，缓解模态差异；空间状态感知表示模块（SSARM）用于建模跨帧空间相关性，减少空间突变影响。此外，设计空间位移预测损失以进一步抑制模态切换引发的空间变化。

Result: 在自建的CM-UOT大规模跨模态视频数据集上，SARLA在多个指标上均优于20种现有先进跟踪方法，验证了其在复杂场景下跨模态跟踪的优越性能。

Conclusion: SARLA通过状态感知机制有效应对模态切换带来的外观与空间突变问题，显著提升了无人机跨模态目标跟踪的鲁棒性；所构建的CM-UOT数据集将推动该领域研究发展，研究成果已开源，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) object tracking has emerged as a popular research field with broad practical applications. Modern UAVs are increasingly equipped with both visible light and thermal infrared sensors. However, due to constraints in communication bandwidth, computational resources and power consumption, current systems often activate one modality and switch between modalities to maintain robust tracking in complex scenarios. Such modality switch inevitably leads to significant appearance change and sudden spatial shift, posing great challenges for existing tracking algorithms. To handle this problem, we propose a novel State-Aware Representation Learning Approach called SARLA, which perceives the inconsistent modality states of current frame with template and last frame in the target representations to adapt to the sudden changes in both appearance and position, for robust cross-modal object tracking. In particular, we propose the Modality State Aware Representation Module (MSARM) and Spatial State Aware Representation Module (SSARM). MSARM guides the model to learn appearance correlation, bridging the modality gap, while SSARM models cross-frame spatial correlation to mitigate sudden spatial shift impacts. In addition, we design a spatial shift prediction loss to further handle the effects of spatial variation caused by modality switch. To promote the development of this research field, we establish a large-scale video benchmark called CM-UOT, which consists of 1079 cross-modal sequences with an average video length greater than 621 frames and encompasses over 671K frames in total. Extensive experiments on CM-UOT dataset demonstrate the superior performance of the proposed SARLA against 20 excellent tracking methods. The source code, datasets, and evaluation protocols associated with this work are publicly available at: https://github.com/hongsmile365/sarla-.

</details>


### [29] [Privileged Lesion-Context Relational Distillation for Mask-Free Skin Lesion Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18773)
*Abu Mukaddim Rahi,Md Mithun Hossain,Md Zulficar Hasan Joy,M. F. Mridha,Md. Jakir Hossen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Privileged Lesion-Context Relational Distillation (PLCRD)框架，利用训练时的病变掩码信息，在推理阶段仅需原始图像即可实现高精度皮肤病变分类。该方法通过教师-学生架构，将病变与上下文特征解耦，并通过关系对齐、亲和性匹配等机制传递诊断结构知识，避免直接特征匹配，提升模型可解释性与临床实用性。在HAM10000和ISIC 2018数据集上均取得优异性能，验证了掩码信息可转化为可迁移的关系知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有皮肤病变分类方法依赖于分割掩码或额外分割模型进行推理，降低了临床实用性并增加计算开销。如何在不使用掩码的前提下，有效利用训练阶段的标注信息以提升分类性能，是亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出PLCRD框架，利用训练时的病变掩码构建教师模型，学习病变特异性与上下文诊断表示；通过分解深层特征为病变与上下文嵌入，采用关系对齐、亲和性匹配、分离正则化及类别感知关系学习等方式，将教师的诊断结构知识以关系形式转移给仅依赖图像的学生模型。

Result: 在HAM10000数据集上达到0.773±0.018的病变级宏F1、0.764±0.023的平衡准确率和0.976±0.002的宏AUROC；在外部验证集ISIC 2018上获得0.732±0.008的宏F1，显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: PLCRD成功将训练阶段的病变掩码信息转化为可迁移的关系知识，使学生模型在无需掩码的情况下仍具备强大分类能力，为实际临床部署提供了高效、可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate skin lesion classification can benefit from lesion segmentation masks, but requiring masks or an auxiliary segmentation model during inference reduces clinical practicality and increases computational complexity. This work introduces Privileged Lesion-Context Relational Distillation (PLCRD), a teacher-student framework that exploits lesion masks exclusively during training while preserving image-only inference. The privileged teacher jointly analyzes the original dermoscopic image and its mask-guided lesion region to learn lesion-specific and contextual diagnostic representations. An image-only student is then trained through complementary knowledge-transfer mechanisms that convey the teacher's diagnostic distribution, lesion-focused attention, inter-lesion relational geometry, and lesion-context structure. PLCRD decomposes deep representations into lesion and contextual embeddings and transfers their relational organization through inter-lesion similarity alignment, lesion-context affinity matching, separation regularization, and class-aware relational learning. This formulation avoids direct feature matching between heterogeneous teacher and student architectures and enables the student to internalize mask-informed diagnostic structure without accessing masks at deployment. The framework was evaluated on HAM10000 using lesion-disjoint data partitioning and externally validated on ISIC 2018 without retraining. PLCRD achieved a lesion-level macro-F1 of 0.773 +/- 0.018, balanced accuracy of 0.764 +/- 0.023, and macro-AUROC of 0.976 +/- 0.002 on HAM10000, together with a macro-F1 of 0.732 +/- 0.008 on ISIC 2018. The results indicate that privileged lesion annotations can be transformed into transferable relational knowledge, yielding a practical and interpretable approach to mask-free skin lesion classification.

Hence, support proper allocation of resources, avoid wastage, and enhance long-term sustainability.

### [31] [Image Editing Models are Numerical Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18787)
*Ulysse Mizrahi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究探索了预训练生成图像编辑模型是否可作为数值模拟的通用接口。通过将物理输入和解以图像形式呈现，并使用轻量级适配器引入材料属性、扩散率等标量参数，利用已有的数值与解析求解器进行监督，同一架构和训练流程被应用于多种物理系统，包括椭圆方程、热传导与伯格斯方程、复高斯动力学、二维纳维-斯托克斯预测、势流、弹性力学、射线传播时间、相场断裂及熵最优传输。结果显示，预训练图像模型能够表示多样化的静态与时变物理映射，包括不稳定和冲击行为，前提是任务具有合适的视觉编码。本工作为能力验证而非超越专用求解器，同时揭示了局限性：图像与潜在表示增加了数值范围选择的复杂性，难以直接施加控制方程或守恒律；且柯尔莫戈洛夫-西瓦辛斯基实验失败表明，表示误差会阻碍混沌系统的长期模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索预训练生成模型在数值模拟中的通用性，尝试统一不同物理问题的求解框架，减少对专用求解器的依赖，并检验其在多样化物理现象建模中的潜力。

Method: 将物理输入与解转化为图像，通过轻量级适配器注入参数，采用统一的预训练图像生成模型与训练策略，在多个物理系统上进行监督学习，基于视觉编码实现不同物理过程的建模。

Result: 预训练图像模型成功表征了多种静态与动态物理过程，包括非线性、不稳定性及冲击行为，但存在表示误差导致的长期模拟失效，尤其在混沌系统中表现不佳。

Conclusion: 预训练生成模型可作为跨物理领域的通用接口，具备建模多样性物理现象的能力，但受限于图像表示的精度与表达能力，难以实现精确的方程约束与长时序模拟，尤其对混沌系统无效。

Abstract: We investigate whether a pretrained generative image-editing model can provide a common interface for numerical simulation. Physical inputs and solutions are rendered as images, while scalar quantities such as material properties, diffusivity, and loading parameters enter through lightweight adapters. Using established numerical and analytic solvers for supervision, we apply the same architecture and training protocol to heterogeneous elliptic equations, forced heat and Burgers evolution, complex Ginzburg-Landau dynamics, two-dimensional Navier-Stokes prediction, potential flow, elasticity, eikonal travel time, phase-field fracture, and entropic optimal transport. The results show that a pretrained image model can represent diverse static and time-dependent physical mappings, including unstable and shock-like behavior, when each task is expressed through a suitable visual encoding. This work is a capability study rather than an attempt to surpass specialized solvers. It also identifies fundamental constraints: image and latent representations complicate numerical range selection and direct enforcement of governing equations or invariants, while a failed Kuramoto-Sivashinsky experiment indicates that representation errors prevent meaningful long-horizon simulation of chaotic systems.

### [32] [Moving Alphabet: A Controlled Study of Training Data for Text-to-Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18789)
*Amber Yijia Zheng,Lu Liu,Raymond A. Yeh,Xi Yin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了数据分布和字幕质量对文本到视频生成模型的影响，提出Moving Alphabet测试平台以实现受控实验。实验发现：1）视频内容和时长的多样性和均衡性对泛化至关重要；2）字幕质量显著影响模型性能和训练效率，表明模型受限于视频理解能力；3）无分类器引导和在高质量数据上的微调可部分弥补低质量预训练数据的问题，但无法完全补偿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本到视频生成模型虽在规模、数据和计算上取得进展，但训练数据的探索不足，真实世界数据的整理复杂且非平凡，因此需要系统研究数据分布和字幕质量对模型的影响。

Method: 提出Moving Alphabet这一程序化测试平台，通过控制字体、颜色、大小、位置、运动方向和速度等变量，生成带注释的视频-文本对，并通过破坏真实元数据来模拟不同质量的字幕，从而进行受控实验。

Result: 1）多样且均衡的数据分布有助于模型泛化；2）字幕质量对模型性能和训练效率有显著影响，表明模型受制于视频理解能力；3）无分类器引导和高质量数据微调可部分缓解问题，但无法完全弥补劣质预训练数据带来的缺陷。

Conclusion: 研究强调预训练数据科学的重要性，建议未来在构建大规模文本到视频模型时应更加重视数据质量和分布设计。

Abstract: Text-to-video generation has advanced significantly over the past five years through scaling of model size, data, and compute. Unlike model architecture, training data is often underexplored. Real-world data curation is complex and non-trivial, involving clip selection from raw videos and captioning to create video-text pairs for learning text-to-video mappings. We study how data distribution and caption quality impact text-to-video models. To enable controlled experiments, we introduce Moving Alphabet, a procedural testbed that renders letters with varying fonts, colors, sizes, and positions, moving in different directions and speeds against a black background. This design allows precise control over data distribution and caption quality by corrupting ground-truth metadata. Our experiments yield three findings: a) a diverse and balanced distribution of video content and duration is critical for generalization; b) caption quality significantly affects both model performance and training efficiency, suggesting that text-to-video models are bounded by video understanding capabilities; and c) classifier-free guidance and fine-tuning on high-quality data provide partial recovery from models trained on corrupted captions, but cannot fully compensate for poor pre-training data. We believe these insights can inform the development of large-scale text-to-video models, and we advocate for greater attention to the science of pre-training data.

### [33] [STS-NET: Spatio-Temporal Stress Network for Self-Supervised Crop Stress Detection using Satellite Image Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18791)
*Pradeep Dalal,Rajiv Ranjan,Sushil Ghildiyal,Shashank Tamaskar,Neeraj Goel*

Conclusion: STS-NET在减少对人工标注数据依赖的前提下，实现了对甘蔗作物胁迫的高精度检测，具备良好的实际应用潜力，同时可作为轻量级模型的通用特征提取工具。

Abstract: Early and accurate detection of crop stress is essential to improve agricultural productivity and ensure global food security. However, collecting a large labeled crop stress dataset is a challenging task. To address this challenge, we introduce a novel spatial-temporal stress network (STS-NET), built on a self-supervised 3D-convolutional autoencoder (3D-CAE), designed to utilize Satellite Image Time Series (SITS) data for crop stress detection. STS-NET exploits four vegetation indices: Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI), Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (GNDVI), Red-Edge Chlorophyll Index (RECI) and Normalized Difference Red-Edge Index (NDRE) obtained from high resolution Planetscope imagery to capture spatiotemporal stress patterns. The model is trained on our BSPT (Barnala Spatial-Temporal) dataset and evaluated on a real-world sugarcane dataset collected over a year from a 2.5-acre test plot located in Lakhimpur-Kheri (LK) district in Uttar Pradesh in India. STS-NET achieved a precision of 97. 98\% for water stress, 85.08\% for nitrogen stress, and 83.47\% for combined stress. The results demonstrate the potential of STS-NET in effectively detecting stress in sugarcane crops with minimal reliance on labeled data. Furthermore, STS-NET can serve as a robust feature extractor for simpler models.

### [34] [UVFaceFusion: Fast Multi-view Topologically Consistent Face Reconstruction in the Wild via UV-space Neural Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18798)
*Xin Ming,Yuxuan Han,Junhai Yong,Feng Xu*

TL;DR: UVFaceFusion提出了一种前馈框架，用于从日常图像中进行多视角、固定拓扑的面部重建。通过在规范的UV空间中使用可学习的神经融合替代启发式拓扑优化，实现了高保真几何重建。该方法在仅用Ava-256训练的情况下，仍能良好泛化到多个公开基准和真实场景数据，且在单张RTX 4090上16视图输入下重建时间少于3秒，达到当前最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化面部重建方法在几何保真度与野外场景泛化能力之间存在权衡，缺乏一种既能保持高精度又能适应多样拍摄条件的方法。

Method: 首先利用VGGT和Pixel3DMM分别获取多视角图像的密集点图和面部UV对应关系；然后将各视角点图提升至规范的UV域，并通过新型掩码感知神经融合网络进行融合，生成完整的UV空间点图，最终直接采样得到固定拓扑网格。

Abstract: Reconstructing high-fidelity facial geometry with an assigned topology is essential for digital avatar creation and animation, yet existing automated methods often trade off geometric fidelity and in-the-wild generalization. We present UVFaceFusion, a feed-forward framework for multi-view, fixed-topology face reconstruction from daily images. Our key idea is to replace heuristic topological optimization with learnable neural fusion in a canonical UV space. Given multi-view images, we first obtain dense point maps and facial UV correspondences of each view using VGGT and Pixel3DMM, respectively. Then, the view-specific point maps are lifted into the canonical UV domain and fused with a novel mask-aware neural fusion network. The network predicts a complete UV-space point map, from which a fixed-topology mesh is directly sampled. Although trained only on Ava-256, UVFaceFusion generalizes well to multiple public benchmarks and in-the-wild captures, benefiting from its canonical UV-space geometry-to-geometry fusion that reduces dependence on dataset-specific appearance and capture conditions. Experiments on various benchmarks show that UVFaceFusion achieves state-of-the-art reconstruction accuracy while reconstructing a mesh from 16 input views in less than 3 seconds on a single RTX 4090. Code is available at https://github.com/grignarder/UVFaceFusion.

Result: 在GR-LERF和GR-ScanNet两个新基准上显著优于现有方法，兼顾性能与效率，适用于单目标和泛化场景。

Conclusion: ZeroSplat成功突破了传统R3DGS方法在灵活性与效率上的限制，为通用语言引导3D场景理解提供了高效可行的新范式。

Abstract: Recent advancements in 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled language-guided scene understanding. However, existing Referring 3D Gaussian Splatting (R3DGS) methods are fundamentally restricted to single-target queries. To reflect the ambiguity of real-world instructions, we introduce the Generalized Referring 3D Gaussian Splatting Segmentation (GR3DGS) task, which requires dynamically segmenting an arbitrary number of targets (0, 1, or $N$). To facilitate comprehensive evaluation of this new task, we construct two new benchmarks: GR-LERF and GR-ScanNet. Crucially, existing R3DGS paradigms exhibit fundamental technical bottlenecks that severely limit their performance on the GR3DGS task: they lack intrinsic 3D point-level understanding by operating merely on 2D rendered pixels, and they incur prohibitive computational overhead by requiring per-scene optimization to embed heavy semantic features. To dismantle these bottlenecks, we propose ZeroSplat, a novel training-free and zero-feature framework. ZeroSplat lifts 2D Vision-Language Model (VLM) priors into 3D space through robust multi-view geometric constraints. This strategy enables intrinsic point-level understanding without incurring any additional feature storage. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ZeroSplat significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods across generalized and single-target scenarios while maintaining exceptional efficiency. Project Page: https://inkmind-ai.github.io/ZeroSplat

</details>


### [36] [In-Context Learning for Wound Classification with Small Multimodal Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18819)
*George Martvel,Oskar Gustafsson,John Pavia,Ernst Ahlberg*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究探索了小型多模态语言模型（SMLMs）在无需训练的情况下，通过基于检索的上下文学习（ICL）实现伤口图像分类的可行性。在Kaggle和Medetec两个公开数据集上评估了11个来自Qwen 3.5、Ministral 3和Gemma 4系列的SMLMs，结果表明，基于检索的ICL显著优于零样本提示和随机少样本提示。最佳模型Qwen 3.5 27B结合kNN+MMR策略，在Kaggle数据集上达到0.872准确率和0.871 F1分数，在Medetec上达到0.678准确率和0.670 F1分数。性能随模型规模增大而提升，且在8-10个支持样本时性能趋于饱和。该方法无需重新训练，具备良好的适应性和隐私友好性，但表现仍依赖于模型规模、检索策略和数据集难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统伤口图像分类依赖大量人工标注数据和任务特定的再训练，灵活性差。本研究旨在探索无需训练的小型多模态语言模型是否可通过检索式上下文学习实现灵活、高效的伤口分类，以减少对标注数据和重训练的依赖。

Method: 采用零样本提示、随机少样本提示、基于嵌入的k近邻（kNN）检索以及kNN结合最大边际相关性重排序（MMR）的检索策略，在Kaggle和Medetec两个数据集上评估11个SMLMs。通过控制实验（如检索仅加权kNN对照、支持集缩减、支持上下文大小变化）分析检索、模型规模和提示长度的影响。

Result: 在Kaggle数据集上，Qwen 3.5 27B结合kNN+MMR策略达到0.872准确率和0.871 F1分数；在Medetec数据集上达到0.678准确率和0.670 F1分数。更大模型优于匹配的加权kNN基线，说明模型不仅使用最近邻投票，还利用了上下文信息。性能在8-10个支持样本时趋于饱和，支持集缩减导致性能轻微下降。

Conclusion: 基于检索的上下文学习为伤口图像分类提供了一种无需任务特定再训练的灵活替代方案。小型多模态语言模型结合高效检索策略可在不依赖大量标注数据的前提下实现良好性能，适用于实际部署，尤其在注重隐私的场景中具有优势，但其性能仍受模型规模、检索策略和数据复杂度影响。

Abstract: Wound image classification is often treated as a task-specific supervised learning problem, requiring substantial amounts of manually labelled data and retraining when the label space or deployment setting changes. This study evaluated whether small multimodal language models (SMLMs) can provide a training-free alternative for wound classification through retrieval-based in-context learning (ICL). Experiments used two public wound-image datasets: the Kaggle wound dataset (1469 images, 10 classes) and the Medetec dataset (560 images, 9 classes). Eleven SMLMs from the Qwen 3.5, Ministral 3, and Gemma 4 families were evaluated under zero-shot prompting and few-shot prompting with random support examples, embedding-based k-nearest-neighbour (kNN) retrieval, and kNN retrieval followed by maximal marginal relevance reranking (MMR). Retrieval-only weighted-kNN controls, support-set reduction experiments, and support-context size sweeps were used to assess the effects of retrieval, model scale, and prompt length. Query-conditioned ICL consistently outperformed zero-shot and random few-shot prompting. On the Kaggle dataset, the best result was achieved by Qwen 3.5 27B with kNN+MMR, reaching 0.872 accuracy and 0.871 F1 score. On Medetec, Qwen 3.5 27B with kNN+MMR reached 0.678 accuracy and 0.670 F1. Larger models exceeded matched weighted-kNN controls, indicating use of retrieved examples beyond nearest-neighbour voting. Retrieval-based ICL degraded modestly under support-set reduction, and most gains saturated with 8-10 support images. Retrieval-based ICL allows SMLMs to perform adaptable wound image classification without task-specific retraining. Compact retrieved contexts may support practical and privacy-conscious deployment, although performance remains dependent on model scale, retrieval strategy, and dataset difficulty.

Abstract: Gaze Object Prediction (GOP) aims to localize and recognize the objects humans attend to, a task crucial for understanding human-centric interactions. However, existing methods are typically trained under a closed-vocabulary paradigm with a fixed label space and evaluated on scene-specific datasets, limiting their applicability to real-world scenarios where gaze targets often follow a long-tail distribution or belong to unseen categories. To address this gap, we introduce Diverse Scenes for Gaze object prediction (DiSG), a benchmark containing 86 in-the-wild categories that facilitates the evaluation of Open-Vocabulary GOP (OVGOP). Building on DiSG, we propose a framework that leverages text-driven object discovery to localize potential gaze candidates, with a gaze-guided selection module to pinpoint the intended target from the candidate objects. Furthermore, to better capture semantic knowledge across diverse in-the-wild categories, we introduce Gradient-Informed Selection Tuning (GIST) to selectively update parameters most relevant to a given class vocabulary. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our proposed model performs effectively in open-vocabulary settings and also outperforms existing methods in the conventional closed-vocabulary setting. The benchmark and code is available at https://github.com/sensniu/ovgop.

### [38] [OPD-IAD: From Language Judgment to Industrial Anomaly Detection via On-Policy Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18850)
*Shuimu Chen,Jing Jin,Nan Su,Hongbo Xu,Zebang Cheng,Wenming Yang,Fei Ma,Guijin Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OPD-IAD提出一种基于证据优先的密集在线策略自蒸馏框架，通过语言引导视觉锚定实现精确像素级异常定位。该方法利用语言判断生成语义条件，并结合对比热图头将语义锚点与密集视觉特征对齐，从而生成高精度异常图。语言仅提供紧凑的语义指导，不主导视觉响应，保持视觉特征在像素级评分中的核心地位。实验表明，该方法在图像级、像素级和问答类指标上均优于现有LVLM-based IAD方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大视觉-语言模型（LVLM）的工业异常检测方法难以从语言判断中生成精确的像素级异常图，且容易受语言质量影响。如何在利用语言提供可解释性的同时，确保像素级定位的准确性，是当前研究的关键挑战。

Method: 提出OPD-IAD框架，包含两个核心组件：1）证据优先的密集在线策略自蒸馏机制，将缺陷证据注入模型自身的判断轨迹，实现密集监督；2）语言引导的视觉锚定（Language-guided Visual Anchoring），通过重新编码图像与问题以生成语义锚点，并与密集视觉特征进行对比，生成异常热图。

Result: 在多个图像级、像素级和问答评估指标上，OPD-IAD显著优于现有基于LVLM的IAD方法，实现了最佳的整体性能，尤其在像素级异常定位精度方面表现突出。

Conclusion: OPD-IAD成功实现了语言作为语义引导而非主导因素的像素级异常定位，有效平衡了语言解释性与视觉精度，为基于大模型的工业异常检测提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large vision-language models (LVLMs) have recently shown strong potential for industrial anomaly detection (IAD) by providing image-level anomaly judgments and interpretable defect reasoning. However, current LVLM-based IAD methods still struggle to produce precise pixel-level anomaly maps from generated language judgments. We aim to achieve precise pixel-level localization while using language as guidance rather than letting it dominate the visual response. Specifically, we propose \textbf{OPD-IAD}, an evidence-privileged dense on-policy self-distillation framework for LVLM-based IAD. OPD-IAD distills privileged defect evidence onto the model's own on-policy judgment trajectory, enabling the final generated judgment to be learned under dense supervision rather than treated only as a textual answer. The resulting judgment serves as a semantic condition for dense anomaly perception. To turn this condition into dense visual evidence, we introduce \textbf{Language-guided Visual Anchoring}, which uses a judgment reforward to re-encode the image and question under the final-judgment condition into semantic anchors and contrasts them with dense visual features through a contrastive heatmap head to generate anomaly maps. The language judgment therefore provides compact semantic guidance, while dense visual features remain the basis for pixel-level scoring, allowing language to guide anomaly localization without letting language quality directly dictate the pixel-level response. Extensive experiments show that OPD-IAD achieves the best overall performance among LVLM-based IAD methods, leading on most image-level, pixel-level, and QA metrics.

</details>


### [39] [Think Sparse, Predict Dense: Continuous Thought Machines for Image Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18856)
*Zekai Shi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于连续思维机器（CTM）的窗口级机制DQ-CTM，用于密集视觉预测任务如图像超分辨率。通过局部窗口内的共享思维动态生成紧凑的思想表示，并将其转化为窗口对齐的密集查询，实现逐位置的精细化重建。在ThinkSR框架中，特征图被分块处理，经多轮思维迭代后恢复原空间结构并解码为高分辨率图像。实验显示，在4个思维周期内，PSNR-Y和PSNR-RGB持续提升，均方误差下降，所有图像均得到改善，验证了稀疏潜在思维在密集空间重建中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在密集视觉任务中难以保持空间信息完整性，而传统全局表征压缩了局部细节。本文旨在通过引入具有时间维度的连续思维机制，使局部窗口能保留空间证据并逐步优化重建质量。

Method: 采用窗口级连续思维机器（CTM），将输入特征划分为局部窗口；利用共享的思维动态生成每个窗口的紧凑思想表示；通过低秩、参数高效的紧凑到密集查询转换机制（DQ-CTM）生成每个位置的独立查询；在多个思维周期内进行迭代精炼，最终恢复完整特征场并解码为高分辨率图像。

Result: 在固定四周期训练下，PSNR-Y从28.1045 dB升至30.2817 dB，PSNR-RGB从26.6271 dB升至28.7781 dB，均方ℓ₁误差从0.034602降至0.023545；所有100张测试图像在T=1至T=4期间均有提升，表明该方法能有效实现渐进式高质量重建。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了基于稀疏潜在思维的连续思考机制可用于密集视觉重建任务，展示了其在图像超分辨率中的有效性与潜力，为未来构建更广泛适用的连续思考视觉架构提供了新思路。

Abstract: Continuous Thought Machines introduce an internal temporal dimension in which neuron-level histories and synchronization-derived representations evolve over a sequence of thought ticks. Extending this mechanism to dense visual prediction is non-trivial, because tasks such as image super-resolution require spatial evidence to remain available at every output location rather than being compressed into a single global representation. In the proposed window-level use of CTM, the thought dynamics produce a compact summary representation for each local window. DQ-CTM transforms this compact thought representation into window-aligned dense queries through a structured low-rank, parameter-efficient compact-to-dense query mechanism. Each position within a window receives its own query, while shared thought dynamics progressively refine the dense representation across ticks. In its super-resolution instantiation, termed ThinkSR, encoded feature maps are partitioned into local visual windows without token pooling, restored to the original feature field after shared refinement, and decoded into a high-resolution image. Preliminary experiments under a fixed four-tick training horizon reveal a progressive reconstruction trajectory. PSNR-Y increases from 28.1045 dB at $T=0$ to 30.2817 dB at $T=4$, while PSNR-RGB increases from 26.6271 dB to 28.7781 dB and the mean $\ell_1$ error decreases from 0.034602 to 0.023545. All 100 evaluated images improve from $T=1$ to $T=4$. These initial results establish the feasibility of sparse latent thought for dense spatial reconstruction and motivate broader continuous-thought architectures for dense vision.

</details>

TL;DR: 提出UniGeo框架，通过一致性感知可靠性门和双流残差融合，实现单目3D增强的通用行人重识别。该方法将3D信息处理解耦为几何提取与动态利用，用运动关节表示投影3D参数以捕捉实例级拓扑结构，从而解决外观模糊性问题；同时将3D先验作为晚期结构残差，并由一致性感知门调控，自适应过滤几何噪声，实现对2D特征空间的稳健补充。在复杂场景下显著提升性能，同时保持对干净域的竞争力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
