### [122] [Inference-Time Steering for Cross-Lingual Factual Consistency in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19243)
*Alexander Manev*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型在多语言环境下因高资源语言偏见导致的跨语言事实不一致问题，并测试了四种推理时干预策略：零样本上下文引导（人格提示）、通过对比激活添加（CAA）操纵内部表示，以及基于基准事实数据和概念泛化数据训练的直接偏好优化（DPO）轻量级权重修改。实验使用Gemma 3 12B Instruct模型，在自建多语言事实数据集和新型文化根植查询泛化基准上评估性能。结果显示，人格提示整体表现最佳，兼顾有效性、安全性和跨领域泛化能力；CAA虽能显著改善不一致性但对配置敏感且有知识退化风险；DPO适配器提供持久但范围较窄、可迁移性较差的改进。结论表明，跨语言不一致至少部分源于选择问题，简单上下文干预可能优于更侵入性方法，实现更稳健、可迁移的对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型虽然具备出色的多语言流畅性，但其内部知识表示仍严重偏向高资源语言，导致在不同语言提示下产生事实不一致现象，影响跨语言可靠性。因此亟需在推理阶段缓解此类偏差，提升模型在低资源语言上的表现与一致性。

Method: 提出并评估四种推理时干预策略：零样本上下文引导（人格提示）、对比激活添加（CAA）、基于事实数据和概念泛化数据的直接偏好优化（DPO）轻量级权重修改。构建多语言事实数据集及文化根植查询泛化基准，用于系统评估各方法在跨语言一致性、安全性与泛化能力上的表现。

Result: 人格提示在整体性能上最优，兼具高效性、安全性和跨域泛化能力；CAA虽能显著提升不一致性指标，但对配置敏感且存在知识退化风险；DPO适配器带来持久但范围有限、迁移性差的改进。实验表明，跨语言不一致部分源于模型选择机制，简单上下文干预优于复杂深度修改。

Conclusion: 跨语言事实不一致问题至少部分是选择性偏差所致，通过简单而有效的上下文干预（如人格提示）可在不损害模型整体能力的前提下实现稳健且可迁移的对齐，优于更复杂的内部表示或权重修改方法。

Abstract: Although Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable multilingual fluency, their internal knowledge representations remain disproportionately biased toward high-resource languages. This leads to cross-lingual factual inconsistency, where they shift their empirical answer distributions based solely on the prompt language. We investigate whether these biases can be mitigated at inference time, forcing an English-prompted model to answer as if it were queried in target languages (German, Spanish, Bulgarian), and evaluate four intervention strategies: zero-shot contextual steering (persona prompting), internal representation manipulation via Contrastive Activation Addition (CAA), and lightweight weight modification via Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) trained on benchmark-derived factual data as well as conceptual generalization data. To assess alignment, we curate a multilingual factual dataset alongside a novel generalization benchmark comprising culturally rooted queries to determine whether factual interventions transfer to broader target-centric preferences. Experiments on Gemma 3 12B Instruct reveal persona prompting to be the strongest overall intervention, balancing efficacy, safety, and out-of-domain generalization. While CAA yields sharp inconsistency benchmark shifts, it is configuration-sensitive and risks knowledge degradation. DPO-based adapters offer permanent, yet narrower and less transferable gains. These findings suggest that cross-lingual inconsistency is at least partly a selection problem, and that simple contextual interventions may outperform more invasive methods for robust, transferable alignment.

</details>


### [123] [Prompt Design at Scale: How Format, Instruction Count, and Context Length Shape Instruction Adherence and Hallucination in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19257)
*Netanel Eliav*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过两个受控实验，系统评估了提示设计中的三个关键决策：指令与上下文的格式（如Markdown、纯文本、散文或表格）、系统提示中可容纳的同时指令数量，以及模型在不同上下文长度下的表现。实验1发现，当指令数量超过80时，所有模型的正确响应率均降至零，且提示位置的影响比格式更大；实验2显示，尽管在64-128k token范围内召回率保持高位，但接近上下文上限时，模型拒绝回答的比例急剧上升（达79%-90%），而幻觉和迎合现象极少发生。此外，不同格式的性能差异显著，且存在格式开销（增加22%-37%的token），影响最优选择。研究结果表明，现有实践缺乏实证支持，需重新审视提示工程策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前提示设计中的关键决策（如格式、指令数量、上下文长度）缺乏受控实验支持，导致实践中存在大量假设性做法。本研究旨在通过系统化实验揭示这些因素对大模型行为的真实影响，为提示工程提供数据驱动依据。

Method: 使用一个确定性生成的合成语料库（Book of Veyra，含8,780个唯一实体），进行两组受控实验：实验1测试指令数量从10到160增长时，不同格式和放置方式下指令遵循能力的衰减；实验2在2k至512k token的上下文长度梯度上，评估召回准确率、虚假前提迎合及事实虚构等问题，并分析格式影响与额外开销。

Result: 实验1显示，指令数量超过80后，所有模型的完美响应率归零，提示位置的影响大于格式；实验2表明，召回率在64-128k token内稳定，但接近上下文上限时急剧下降，且不同格式间差异可达48分；幻觉未出现，迎合程度极低，但拒绝回答率飙升至79%-90%；格式开销显著，改变最优格式选择。

Conclusion: 当前提示设计中的许多实践缺乏实证基础。模型对多指令和长上下文的处理能力存在明确极限，且格式选择受开销和模型特性影响显著。未来提示工程应基于实证数据，避免依赖直觉，并考虑格式开销与拒绝行为的权衡。

Abstract: Practitioners make three prompt-design decisions with almost no controlled evidence behind them: how to format instructions and context (markdown, plain text, prose, or tabular), how many simultaneous instructions a system prompt can carry before compliance degrades, and how much context a model can hold before recall and honesty degrade. We report two controlled experiments crossing all three factors on one held, contamination-free synthetic corpus (the "Book of Veyra," 8,780 uniquely-named entities, deterministically regenerable from a fixed seed), evaluated across five models.
  Experiment 1 (960 calls/model) measures instruction-following decay as rule count N grows from 10 to 160, crossed with four formats and system-prompt vs. user-turn placement. Perfect-response rate collapses to zero by N=80 for every model, format, and placement. Placement produces effects at least as large as format at N=160 in most models, but the direction is model-specific. No model shows a reliable markdown advantage; one 35B model favors plain text instead.
  Experiment 2 (5,520 calls/model) measures recall accuracy, false-premise sycophancy, and absent-fact fabrication across a 2k-to-512k-token context ladder in the same four formats. Recall stays near ceiling through 64-128k tokens, then degrades sharply and format-dependently: one model's accuracy spread reaches 48 points at 128k tokens. Fabrication never occurs (0/5,760 probes), and sycophancy stays negligible (<=8.3%). What rises sharply near each model's context ceiling is outright refusal to answer (0% to 79-90%), distinct from sycophancy or fabrication. Neither pre-registered format ordering holds, and token overhead (+22% to +37% over plain text) further changes which format is preferable where accuracy spread is genuine.
  We release the full harness, corpus generator, and raw results (VeyraBench): https://github.com/iNetanel/veyrabench

</details>


### [124] [Two-Level Meta-Rubrics for Evaluating Open-Ended Generation: GAMUT, a Benchmark for Factual Completeness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19322)
*Xilun Chen,Zhaleh Feizollahi,Ross Goodwin,Seungwhan Moon,Scott Yih,Pinar Donmez,Babak Damavandi,Luna Dong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两层元评分框架，用于评估长文本生成中的事实完整性，构建了名为Gamut的基准测试。该框架通过结构化元评分表捕捉内容组织与重要性，并转化为可机器评分的二元检查清单，支持多模态和纯文本数据。基于真实可穿戴图像构建了1,813个跨10个领域的问答对，经专家验证，具有挑战性、区分度高且对评判者选择鲁棒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要关注生成内容的精确性，但忽视了事实完整性——即回答是否包含应有全部信息。传统方法难以处理开放性事实集合、有序过程及事实间关系，因此亟需更全面的评估框架。

Method: 提出两层元评分框架：第一层为结构化元评分表，描述内容组织与重要性；第二层将元评分自动编译为可机器评分的二元检查清单，由大模型评分器进行评估。结合真实数据与专家验证，构建多模态与文本双版本基准。

Result: 在14个前沿及开源模型上测试显示，最高得分仅为58.7%（Gemini 3.1 Pro），表明该基准具有挑战性；结果高度区分不同模型表现，且对评判模型选择不敏感，具备良好鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Gamut框架有效解决了长文本生成中事实完整性评估难题，提供了一种可扩展、可验证、可机器执行的评估路径，推动了生成质量评价向更全面方向发展。

Abstract: Evaluating the factuality of long-form generations has focused predominantly on precision, measuring whether the claims a model makes are correct. The dominant decompose-search-verify pipeline catches incorrect claims well but says little about whether a response contains all the information it should. Measuring factual completeness, the missing half of factuality, is harder: it requires enumerating the full set of facts a complete answer should contain, and these facts rarely form a flat list. They often involve open-ended sets where coverage is what matters, ordered processes, and relationships among facts that a list of independent boolean checks fails to capture. We introduce a two-level meta-rubric framework for evaluating open-ended generation, and instantiate it as Gamut (Grounded Assessment of Multimodal Factuality), a benchmark for factual completeness in long-form generation. The framework rests on a two-level rubric representation: a structured meta-rubric captures the organization and importance of the required content, which is then mechanically compiled into a flat checklist of binary, machine-gradable rubrics that an LLM judge scores reliably. We construct 1,813 questions grounded in real wearable imagery across 10 diverse domains, each paired with an evidence-backed rubric verified by expert human annotators. Because the framework is modality-agnostic, we also release a text-only variant. Evaluating 14 frontier and open-weight models, we find the benchmark genuinely challenging (best score 58.7% from Gemini 3.1 Pro), highly discriminative, and robust to the choice of judge.

</details>


### [125] [Selective State-Space Adaptation and Retrieval for Language Model Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19326)
*Atahan Dokme,Larry Heck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种新型适配器家族MaLoRA和MaRA，通过引入选择性状态空间递归，在令牌级和上下文级实现动态、输入相关的适应，显著提升模型在多个冻结骨干网络上的推理准确率，平均提升6.8 F1（相对+10.5%），最高达9.3 F1（相对+18.2%），且在长文本压力下仍保持优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩适配（LoRA）方法为静态更新，缺乏对输入间差异的动态建模能力，尤其无法捕捉令牌级或实例级的状态变化，限制了其在复杂推理任务中的表现。

Method: 提出MaLoRA（Mamba调制的低秩适配）与MaRA（Mamba检索适配器），前者通过引入跨令牌的递归状态动态调整适配器缩放因子，后者通过跟踪跨段状态并选择最相关段落以支持生成，实现两个粒度上的选择性状态空间递归。

Result: 在三个冻结骨干模型（Qwen-2.5-7B, Llama-3.1-8B, Gemma-2-9B）和两个推理基准（MuSiQue, 2WikiMultihopQA）上，所有组合均优于LoRA基线，平均提升6.8 F1（+10.5%相对），最高提升9.3 F1（+18.2%相对），且令牌级改进在长文本任务RULER QA-2中依然有效。

Conclusion: 通过引入动态、递归的适配机制，MaLoRA和MaRA显著增强了模型对复杂推理任务的适应能力，特别是在长序列和多跳推理场景下表现出更强鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation introduces a static learned update applied identically to every input. The update provides task-level adaptation but does not explicitly represent token-level or instance-level state variation. A family of adapters is proposed that introduces selective state-space recurrence at two complementary granularities. At the token level, \textbf{MaLoRA} (Mamba-modulated low-rank adaptation) makes the adapter's scaling factor a dynamic input-dependent function with recurrent state across tokens, in contrast to the stateless modulators of prior work. At the context level, \textbf{MaRA} (Mamba Retrieval Adapter) tracks cross-segment state and selects the segments most relevant to the query, before the modulated language model generates its answer. Across three frozen backbones (Qwen-2.5-7B, Llama-3.1-8B, Gemma-2-9B) and two reasoning benchmarks (MuSiQue, 2WikiMultihopQA), the family improves reasoning accuracy on every cell of the $3{\times}2$ grid, by $+6.8$ F1 ($+10.5\%$ relative) on average and up to $+9.3$ F1 ($+18.2\%$ relative) on the hardest cell over the LoRA baseline, and the token-level gains carry to RULER QA-2 under length stress.

</details>


### [126] [Copy Less, Ground More: Overcoming Repetitive Copying in Long-Context Reasoning via Evidence-Aware Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19345)
*Lizhe Fang,Weizhou Shen,Tianyi Tang,Yisen Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大语言模型在长上下文设置下的一个关键问题：重复复制（repetitive copying），即模型倾向于将输入文本直接复制到推理过程，而非进行有效求解。作者发现，这种行为在前沿长上下文模型中普遍存在，并随上下文长度增加而加剧。通过分离任务相关证据与无关干扰信息，研究揭示其根源是模型缺乏对关键证据的充分聚焦。为此，提出 GEAR（Grounding Evidence-Aware Reward）方法，通过引入基于关键证据重叠的奖励和无关内容重叠的惩罚来增强训练信号。为实现自然语言数据上的应用，开发了自动构建证据标注数据的流水线。实验验证表明，GEAR 在多个模型规模和基准上均显著优于标准强化学习，平均提升达 +4.6 分，尤其在长上下文场景下表现更优，同时减少重复复制和推理长度。结论强调，在长上下文复杂推理任务中，准确的证据定位仍是核心能力，仍有巨大改进空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别并解决大语言模型在长上下文任务中普遍存在的‘重复复制’现象，该现象导致模型无法有效推理，影响性能；研究旨在提升模型对关键证据的聚焦能力，从而改善复杂任务表现。

Method: 提出 GEAR 方法，结合准确性奖励、关键证据重叠奖励以及无关上下文重叠惩罚，通过自动化流程生成证据标注数据以支持自然语言训练，实现对模型推理过程的引导优化。

Result: GEAR 在多个模型规模和基准测试中均取得显著提升，最高平均提升达 +4.6 分，尤其在长上下文任务中优势明显；同时有效降低重复复制现象和推理长度，证明其在提升模型推理质量方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 尽管长上下文评估已从简单检索转向复杂推理，但准确的证据定位能力依然是决定模型表现的关键因素，且目前仍存在巨大改进空间，提示未来研究需重点关注模型对关键信息的可靠聚焦。

Abstract: Large language models that generate step-by-step reasoning traces have achieved strong performance on complex tasks, and extending them to long-context settings has emerged as an important frontier. However, we identify a critical failure mode in this regime: \emph{repetitive copying}, where models extensively copy text from the input into their reasoning traces rather than productively solving the problem. We show that this behavior is pervasive across frontier long-context LLMs and intensifies with context length. By separating each prompt into task-relevant key evidence and irrelevant distractor context, we further show that the root cause is insufficient grounding: models copy from the prompt indiscriminately, and those that fail to focus on key evidence are far more likely to answer incorrectly. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose GEAR (Grounding Evidence-Aware Reward), a reward shaping method that augments the accuracy signal with a grounding reward for overlap with key evidence and a distractor penalty for overlap with irrelevant context. To enable GEAR on natural-language data, we develop an automated pipeline that constructs evidence-annotated training data from arbitrary documents. We validate GEAR across multiple model scales and benchmarks, showing consistent improvements of up to +4.6 average points over standard RL with accuracy-based rewards, with larger gains at longer contexts, while also reducing repetitive copying and thinking length. Our findings suggest that, even as long-context evaluation shifts from simple retrieval toward complex reasoning, accurate grounding in relevant evidence remains an indispensable capability with substantial room for improvement.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [127] [FALCON-Discover: Discovering Concentrated False-Confidence Regions for Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18278)
*Filippo Cenacchi,Longbing Cao,Runze Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了模型预测中局部过度自信的问题，提出FALCON-Discover框架，通过结合置信度、局部支持、邻域一致性与扰动稳定性等信号，对预测进行排序以发现高风险错误区域。实验表明，虚假自信集中现象普遍存在且依赖于数据集和模型设置；基于差异性信号的排名方法显著优于传统校准或信任评分基线，而单纯依赖置信度效果较差。最佳检测策略因数据集而异：当需融合多个线索时，学习到的差异性表现最优；当局部决策脆弱性主导时，稳定性中心的排序更优。结果表明，过度自信应作为一类家族级发现任务来处理，而非单一校准问题，并建议发展针对置信度、支持度与稳定性不一致区域的专门校准策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有校准评估多为整体性，难以捕捉局部高自信但错误的危险情况。本文关注此类局部过自信（即虚假自信集中）问题，旨在识别并缓解在预测空间中高度集中且易被发现的错误区域。

Method: 提出FALCON-Discover框架，一种后处理、模型无关的方法，利用置信度、局部支持、邻域一致性及扰动稳定性四个维度的差异信号对预测进行排序，以识别潜在的危险错误区域。

Result: 在七个二分类表格数据集上，四次随机种子，五折交叉拟合，使用XGBoost和CatBoost等强学习器，结果显示虚假自信集中现象普遍但受模型与数据影响；基于差异信号的排序显著优于最强的验证选择校准或信任评分基线；原始置信度无法有效捕获危险错误质量；不同数据集下最优检测方式不同：多线索融合场景下学习型差异信号最优，局部脆弱性主导时稳定性排序更佳。

Conclusion: 过度自信的危险性应视为一类家族级发现任务，而非单一得分校准问题。校准策略应主动聚焦于置信度、局部支持与稳定性之间出现分歧的区域，以提升模型可靠性。

Abstract: Calibration is usually evaluated in aggregate, but the most dangerous failures are often local: predictions that remain highly confident despite being wrong. We study this failure mode as false-confidence concentration, the extent to which confident errors occupy compact, discoverable regions of prediction space. We introduce FALCON-Discover, a post-hoc, model-agnostic framework that ranks predictions using discrepancy signals from confidence, local support, neighborhood agreement, and perturbation stability. Across seven binary tabular datasets, four seeds, five-fold cross-fitting, and strong learners including XGBoost and CatBoost, we find that false-confidence concentration is recurrent but regime-dependent. At the main confidence threshold, discrepancy-based ranking substantially outperforms the strongest validation-selected calibration or trust-scoring baseline in the strongest regimes, while raw confidence recovers little dangerous-error mass. The best detector varies across datasets: learned discrepancy is strongest when multiple cues must be combined, whereas stability-centered ranking works best when local decisional fragility dominates. These results show that dangerous overconfidence is better treated as a family-level discovery problem than as a single-score calibration problem, and motivate calibration strategies that explicitly target regions where confidence, support, and stability diverge.

</details>


### [128] [Beyond Output-Space Calibration: Spectral Evidence Bundling for Selective Reliability Estimation in Time-Series Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18279)
*Filippo Cenacchi,Longbing Cao,Runze Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于验证门控的固定标签可靠性策略，结合输出端线索与全样本谱描述符（如带能量、熵、峰值主导性、周期支持和相位稳定性），生成标量可靠性估计和带级诊断证据。通过验证门控机制确保谱条件化仅在提升正确性排名且不违反FalseConf@0.9或AURC容忍度时启用，否则回退至更安全的输出空间基线。在八个异构UCR/UEA数据集、八种时间序列骨干网络及标准校准器上，该方法显著提升固定标签选择性可靠性指标，Corr-AURC从0.693提升至0.786，FalseConf@0.9降低至0.094，表明时间序列分类的可靠性评估需融合输出置信度与谱证据，而验证门控可有效防止不当的谱条件化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后处理校准方法仅重映射输出分数，但部署决策（如信任、拒答、审查）依赖于当前时间信号是否支持高置信预测。现有方法存在三个可靠性缺陷：相同置信度可能隐藏不同时间支持；平均校准可能忽略高置信错误；输出空间校准缺乏输入关联可审计性。

Method: 提出验证门控的固定标签可靠性策略，利用输出端线索与全样本谱特征（带能量、熵、峰值主导性、周期支持、相位稳定性）构建标量可靠性估计，并提供带级诊断证据；引入验证门控机制，仅在正确性排序提升且不违反FalseConf@0.9或AURC容忍度时启用谱条件化，否则回退至输出空间基线。

Result: 在八个异构数据集、八种骨干网络和标准校准器下，无约束方法将Corr-AURC从0.693提升至0.779；验证门控策略进一步将Corr-AURC提升至0.786，同时将FalseConf@0.9降至0.094，显著提升可靠性评估性能。

Conclusion: 时间序列分类的可靠性评估应融合输出置信度与谱域证据，验证门控机制可有效防止不可靠的谱条件化，从而在保证安全性的同时提升可靠性判断的准确性。

Abstract: Post-hoc calibration for time-series classification usually remaps output scores, but deployment decisions such as trust, abstention, and review depend on whether a confident prediction is supported by the current temporal signal. We address three time-series reliability gaps: identical confidence values can hide different temporal support, average calibration can miss false high-confidence errors, and output-space recalibration offers limited input-linked auditability. We introduce a validation-gated fixed-label reliability policy that keeps the backbone prediction unchanged while estimating whether it should be trusted. The method combines output-side cues with whole-sample spectral descriptors, including band energy, entropy, peak dominance, period support, and phase stability, to form a scalar reliability estimate and diagnostic band-level evidence. A validation gate enables spectral conditioning only when correctness ranking improves without breaching FalseConf@0.9 or AURC tolerances; otherwise it reverts to the safer output-space baseline. Across eight heterogeneous UCR/UEA datasets, eight time-series backbone families, and standard recalibrators, the unconstrained method improves fixed-label selective-reliability metrics on the matched evaluation subset, raising Corr-AURC from 0.693 to 0.779. The validation-gated policy further improves Corr-AURC to 0.786 and reduces FalseConf@0.9 to 0.094. These results suggest that reliability estimation for time-series classifiers benefits from bundling output confidence with spectral evidence, while validation gating prevents unsupported spectral conditioning.

</details>


### [129] [Beyond Single-Dimensional Compression: The Compound Sparsity Frontier of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18280)
*Chao Han,Haozhe Hu,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种极简的复合稀疏性框架，结合静态参数压缩（低秩近似与通道剪枝）和动态令牌级计算（轻量级路由实现逐令牌层跳过），以分散压缩负担，延缓性能退化。实验表明，在相同总稀疏度下，复合稀疏性优于单一机制，显著延迟理解任务的性能衰减点并保持更强建模能力。分析揭示参数剪枝与令牌跳过之间存在跨维度干扰，平衡分配最有效。结果表明复合压缩是提升LLM压缩效率的有效途径，并揭示了限制进一步压缩的跨维度稀疏边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有静态参数剪枝和动态令牌级计算在激进稀疏化时易导致性能快速下降，本文旨在探索是否可通过结合两种机制来分担压缩压力，从而延缓性能退化。

Method: 提出一个复合稀疏性框架：先通过低秩近似和通道剪枝构建静态压缩骨干网络；再引入轻量级路由器实现每令牌的动态层跳过，实现参数稀疏与令牌计算稀疏的独立控制。

Result: 在语言理解与建模基准上，复合稀疏性在相同总稀疏度下均优于单一压缩机制，显著延迟性能衰退点，且平衡分配策略表现最佳。分析发现参数剪枝与令牌跳过间存在跨维度干扰，稀疏边界受限于两者协同效应。

Conclusion: 复合压缩能有效提升大模型压缩性能，但其效果受跨维度稀疏边界制约，未来需更深入理解多维稀疏间的交互机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are often compressed through static parameter pruning or dynamic token-level computation, yet aggressive sparsification can trigger rapid performance degradation beyond an essential sparsity boundary. This work asks \emph{whether combining these two mechanisms can delay such degradation by distributing the compression burden}. We study a minimalist compound sparsity framework that first applies low-rank approximation and channel pruning to obtain a statically compressed backbone, and then introduces lightweight routers for per-token dynamic layer skipping. This design enables independent control of parameter sparsity and token-level computation sparsity. Experiments across language understanding and modeling benchmarks show that compound sparsity consistently outperforms single-mechanism compression under the same total sparsity, delaying the decay point on understanding tasks and preserving stronger modeling performance. Further analysis reveals cross-dimensional interference between parameter pruning and token skipping, and shows that near-balanced allocation is most effective under a fixed sparsity budget. These results demonstrate that compound compression provides a practical way to improve LLM compression, while revealing a broader cross-dimensional sparsity boundary that ultimately limits further compression. Code will be available at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/LLM-Pruning.

</details>


### [130] [ALAS: Additive Learnable Alpha-Stable Kernels for Flexible Bayesian Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18282)
*Weibo Huang,Cheng Hua*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ALAS 是一种基于对称 α-稳定谱成分的灵活高斯过程核族，通过学习稳定性参数 α 来自适应数据的平滑性，能够捕捉平滑趋势和尖锐不规则性。提出两种参数化：ALAS（单一平稳分量）和 ALAS-Sep（可分离变体，用于学习各维度尾部行为以提升在近似可分解目标上的鲁棒性）。在标准基准和真实世界代理模型上实验表明，ALAS 在多种场景下表现强大且稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有贝叶斯优化依赖于与目标未知结构匹配的核函数，但难以自动适应不同平滑性或存在尖锐不规则性的复杂目标。因此需要一种能从数据中自适应调整有效平滑度的灵活核方法。

Method: 提出 ALAS 核族，基于对称 α-稳定分布的谱成分；通过学习稳定性参数 α 实现自适应平滑性建模；设计两种参数化形式：ALAS（联合谱调制）和 ALAS-Sep（维度独立尾部建模），以增强灵活性与鲁棒性。

Result: 在多个标准测试基准和真实世界代理模型上，ALAS 和 ALAS-Sep 均表现出优异且稳定的性能，尤其在处理具有混合平滑性与突变特征的目标时优于传统核函数。

Conclusion: ALAS 为贝叶斯优化提供了一种强大的自适应核机制，能有效应对复杂、多变的黑箱优化问题，显著提升了优化效率与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Bayesian Optimization is widely used for expensive black-box optimization, yet its success often depends on choosing a kernel that matches the objective's unknown structure. In this work, we propose ALAS, a flexible Gaussian Process kernel family built from symmetric $α$-stable spectral components. By learning the stability parameter $α$, ALAS adapts its effective smoothness from data, capturing both smooth trends and sharp irregularities. We present two parameterizations: ALAS, a single stationary component with joint spectral modulation, and ALAS-Sep, a separable variant that learns dimension-wise tail behavior to improve robustness on approximately decomposable objectives. Experiments on standard benchmarks and real-world surrogates demonstrate strong and robust performance across diverse settings.

</details>


### [131] [FedCC: A Low-Resource Federated Adaptation of Foundation Models for Robust Corpus Callosum localization in Fetal Ultrasound Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18283)
*Alessandro Di Matteo,Sara Moccia,Giuseppe Rizzo,Gianpaolo Grisolia,Ricciarda Raffaelli,Lorenzo Vasciaveo,Francesco D'Antonio,Maria Chiara Fiorentino*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FedCC框架，基于联邦学习实现胎儿超声图像中胼胝体的精准定位，结合冻结的DINOv2主干网络与轻量级YOLO检测头，并引入低秩适应（LoRA）模块以减少参数量和通信开销。在多中心数据集上验证，该方法在不共享数据的前提下达到mAP@50 0.857、F1-score 0.803，训练参数减少至290万（相比全微调的2440万），通信成本降低约8.5倍，适用于资源受限且注重隐私的临床环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胎儿超声图像中胼胝体定位对早期发现神经发育异常至关重要，但受超声成像固有缺陷（如低对比度、斑点噪声）及胼胝体解剖变异大的影响，该任务极具挑战性。现有方法面临数据共享需求高、计算与通信开销大等问题，尤其在多中心、资源受限的临床场景下难以部署。因此亟需一种无需共享数据、高效低耗、可扩展的解决方案。

Method: 提出FedCC框架，采用冻结的DINOv2作为特征提取主干，搭配轻量级YOLO检测头；通过引入低秩适应（LoRA）模块实现参数高效的模型适配，仅优化并交换少量参数；在联邦平均（FedAvg）策略下进行多中心协作训练，保障隐私的同时提升模型性能。

Result: 在包含10,970帧图像的多中心数据集上，FedCC在联邦设置下取得mAP@50 0.857、F1-score 0.803的优异表现，优于全微调和仅冻结编码器的基线方法；训练参数从2440万降至290万，通信成本降低约8.5倍，显著提升了效率与实用性。

Conclusion: FedCC为胎儿神经超声中的胼胝体定位提供了一种高效、隐私保护且可临床部署的AI解决方案，具备良好的可扩展性和实际应用前景，是迈向智能、安全、协同医疗系统的重要一步。

Abstract: Accurate localization of the corpus callosum (CC) in fetal ultrasound (US) images is crucial for the early identification of neurodevelopmental abnormalities. However, this task remains highly challenging due to the intrinsic limitations of US imaging, including low contrast, speckle noise, and the considerable anatomical variability of the CC. We propose FedCC, a federated learning (FL)-based framework for CC localization in fetal US images, specifically designed for realistic multi-center and resource-constrained clinical settings without requiring data sharing. The framework integrates a frozen DINOv2 backbone with a lightweight YOLO-based detection head. To enable parameter-efficient adaptation, Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) modules are incorporated, allowing only a small subset of parameters to be optimized and exchanged among clients. This strategy substantially reduces both computational and communication overhead, making the framework suitable for low-resource environments. The proposed approach was evaluated on a multi-center dataset comprising 10,970 ultrasound frames acquired from 58 pregnant women during routine neurosonographic examinations across three clinical sites using heterogeneous imaging devices. The proposed framework achieved strong performance in the federated setting. In particular, the combination of DINOv2 and LoRA under the FedAvg strategy achieved an average mAP@50 of 0.857 and an F1-score of 0.803, outperforming both full fine-tuning and encoder-freezing baselines. Notably, the proposed approach reduced the number of trainable parameters to 2.9M compared with 24.4M in full fine-tuning, corresponding to an approximately 8.5$\times$ reduction in communication cost. These findings represent a promising step toward scalable, privacy-preserving, and clinically deployable AI systems for fetal neurosonography.

</details>


### [132] [Compressing What Matters: Neuron Importance Meets Data-Aware Low Rank Approximation for Language Model Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18284)
*Athanasios Ntovas,Alexandros Doumanoglou,Petros Drakoulis,Dimitris Zarpalas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合参数重要性和每层功能等价性的单一目标的神经网络压缩方法，并设计了一种计算高效的动态压缩率分配算法，显著提升了高压缩比下的模型性能，实验结果表明该方法在压缩效果上优于或媲美现有最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型虽然性能强大，但因参数量巨大导致内存需求过高，限制了其在资源受限环境中的应用。现有的压缩方法主要关注低秩近似，但多从参数重要性或层间功能等价性单一角度出发，且压缩率分配方式不够高效，因此需要一种更综合、高效的压缩方案。

Method: 结合参数重要性与层间功能等价性，提出统一优化目标；设计一种计算高效的动态压缩率分配算法，实现对各层和参数的自适应压缩率分配。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提方法在高压缩比下表现优异，性能优于或媲美当前最先进的压缩技术，尤其在资源受限场景中具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 通过融合参数重要性与功能等价性，并引入高效动态压缩率分配策略，本文提出的压缩方法在保持模型性能的同时实现了更高压缩效率，为大模型在边缘设备上的部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: To excel at their domain large language models are comprised of billions of parameters. Yet this comes at the cost of huge memory requirements restricting their applicability in resource-constrained environments. To address the problem of neural network (NN) compression Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) has played a key role as a fundamental component for matrix compression through decomposition. To minimize compression error and to maximize the efficacy of the compressed model on the downstream tasks previous works focused on low-rank approximation of the NN's weight matrices either from the perspective of parameter importance or per-layer functional equivalence. While previous works studied the aforementioned perspectives in isolation in this work we are investigating the effectiveness of an approach that combines ideas from these two perspectives in a single objective. In parallel to this an important aspect that affects the compression quality is the distribution of the compression rate across layers and NN parameters. Earlier works mostly considered distributing the compression rate uniformly across layers and network weights or relied on computationally expensive heuristic search. Contrary to them in this work we propose an enhanced and computationally efficient algorithm for dynamic compression rate allocation. Experimental results support the efficacy of the proposed approach which performs on par or substantially better than the previous state-of-the-art especially under high compression ratios.

</details>


### [133] [Edge-Efficient Transformer for End-to-End RF Spectrum Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18285)
*Zhifan Song,Haralampos-G. Stratigopoulos,Hassan Aboushady*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: E-SpecFormer 是一种用于端到端自动调制和隐蔽信道（CC）识别的边缘高效模型，引入了无 Softmax 和 LayerNorm 的 LiTAN 注意力机制，降低复杂度并提升精度。该模型有四种可扩展变体（Nano、Small、Medium、Large），适用于不同硬件约束。在 RadioML2018 数据集上，Nano 变体在 SNR > 0 dB 时达到 86.5% 的平均准确率；在基于硬件木马的隐蔽信道数据集上达到 94.2% 准确率，参数少于 10k，单帧处理速度达 92 μs（FPGA/CPU 协同执行），显著优于现有边缘模型且成本极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有边缘设备上的调制识别与隐蔽信道检测模型在精度与计算效率之间难以平衡，尤其在资源受限的物联网设备上难以实现实时谱感知。需要一种轻量级、高精度、低延迟的模型以支持边缘智能。

Method: 提出 E-SpecFormer 框架，采用无 Softmax 与 LayerNorm 的 LiTAN 注意力机制，减少计算开销并增强性能；设计四种可扩展的模型变体以适应不同硬件能力；通过 FPGA/CPU 协同部署实现高效推理。

Result: 在 RadioML2018 数据集上，Nano 版本在 SNR > 0 dB 下达到 86.5% 平均准确率；在硬件木马隐蔽信道数据集上达到 94.2% 准确率；模型参数少于 10,000，单帧处理时间仅 92 μs，显著优于现有边缘模型，具备极强的部署潜力。

Conclusion: E-SpecFormer 成功实现了高精度、低延迟、轻量化的端到端调制与隐蔽信道识别，是面向物联网设备实时谱感知的理想解决方案，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: We present E-SpecFormer (Edge Spectrum monitoring Transformer) for end-to-end automatic modulation and covert channel (CC) recognition. We introduce LiTAN (Linear Tanh Attention Network), a Softmax- and LayerNorm-free attention mechanism that reduces complexity while increasing accuracy in RF tasks. E-SpecFormer is parameterized in four scalable variants (Nano, Small, Medium, Large) to accommodate diverse hardware constraints. Using the RadioML2018 dataset for modulation recognition, the Nano variant achieves 86.5% average accuracy for Signal-to-Noise Ratios (SNRs)>0 dB, and on the hardware Trojan (HT)-based CC dataset it reaches 94.2% accuracy, both with fewer than 10k parameters and up to speed of 92 μs per frame on FPGA/CPU co-execution, surpassing state-of-the-art edge models at a fraction of their cost. These results establish E-SpecFormer as an edge-efficient solution for real-time spectrum intelligence on Internet of Things (IoT) devices. GitHub link to the repository: https://github.com/zsniko/E-SpecFormer.

</details>


### [134] [Preference-Conditioned Multi-Objective Reinforcement Learning for Runtime-Tunable Transit Signal Priority](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18286)
*Philip-Roman Adam,Stefanie Schmidtner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种可运行时调整偏好的条件化交通信号优先（TSP）控制器，通过引入偏好参数 $w$ 实现公交优先与整体交通延迟之间的灵活权衡，无需重新训练。该方法基于 IntersectionZoo 构建，并通过增强的场景生成策略（如公交出现率增强和基于时刻表的公交插入）解决训练中公交事件稀疏问题。实验表明，单一学习策略可在不同偏好设置下平滑覆盖性能权衡前沿，优于固定周期和规则基基线，且保持约束可行性；但高公交优先权重下非公交车辆延迟会显著增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法在交通信号优先控制中通常采用固定奖励或固定加权方式，难以适应不同时段或突发事件下管理机构优先级的变化，缺乏运行时灵活性。因此需要一种可动态调节偏好的智能控制机制。

Method: 设计了一个以偏好参数 $w$ 为条件的信号控制策略 $\pi(a \mid s,w)$，结合最小/最大绿灯时间与相位转换可行性约束，在 IntersectionZoo 平台上构建了受约束的信号控制/TSP封装器，并通过公交出现率增强和基于时刻表的公交插入扩展场景生成，提升训练中公交事件覆盖率。

Result: 单个学习到的条件化策略能有效覆盖从高公交优先到低公交优先的完整性能权衡曲线，在多种偏好设置下均优于固定周期和规则基基线，满足约束可行性；诊断分析显示，适度偏好下非公交外部性可控，但高公交优先权重会导致非公交延迟急剧上升。

Conclusion: 所提出的偏好条件化 TSP 控制器实现了运行时灵活调参、无需重训，具备良好的实用性与适应性，是应对多目标交通优化挑战的有效方案，尤其适用于优先级动态变化的城市交通管理场景。

Abstract: Transit signal priority (TSP) requires balancing competing objectives: reducing bus delay while limiting adverse impacts on non-bus traffic and avoiding extreme waits for a subset of vehicles. Existing reinforcement-learning (RL) approaches to TSP typically encode transit-aware features (e.g., occupancy and schedule deviation) but optimize a fixed reward or fixed scalarization, which limits operational flexibility when agency priorities change across time-of-day or disruption conditions. We present a preference-conditioned TSP controller, $π(a \mid s,w)$, that selects the next signal phase under minimum/maximum green and transition-feasibility constraints and can be tuned at runtime via a preference parameter $w$ to trade off bus-priority emphasis against overall traffic delay without retraining. We implement this on top of IntersectionZoo by introducing a constrained signal-control/TSP wrapper, and we extend scenario generation with bus-prevalence augmentation and timetable-based bus insertion to address sparse transit-priority events during training. Experiments against fixed-time control, a rule-based TSP overlay, and fixed-weight PPO specialists show that a single learned conditioned policy spans a smooth empirical trade-off frontier across runtime preferences, outperforms fixed-time and rule-based baselines, and maintains constraint feasibility, while tail-delay diagnostics reveal that non-bus externalities remain limited for moderate preference settings but can increase substantially under high bus-priority weights. The source code of this work is available at https://github.com/urbanAIthi/morl-tsp.

</details>

Abstract: This paper introduces BearingNAS, a Hardware-Aware Neural Architecture Search (HW-NAS) framework designed to shift the intelligence directly onto the sensor die via in-sensor processing. ### [140] [Reliability Scales Inversely: Bigger Models Compound Mistakes Faster via a Hidden Auto-Regressive Risk Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18292)
*Kushal Chakrabarti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 随着语言模型规模增大，答案的准确性先提升后迅速下降：规模带来能力的同时也削弱了可靠性。本文揭示了一种自回归风险残差机制，即模型在生成过程中选定低概率词元并以此为条件持续放大错误，形成雪球效应。通过对比更强的同家族推理模型（oracle），作者定义了位置级分歧度 $\delta = \log p_M - \log p_O$，其方差分解为偏差平方与风险项。研究发现：(i) 规模扩大使知识差距缩小约6倍，但知识退化加剧11–39倍；(ii) 在幻觉发生时，模型自身不确定性快速缓解，而基于oracle的风险持续存在长达17倍以上，形成‘自信但脆弱’的危险区间，连接多个幻觉事件（140亿参数时增加69%）；(iii) 该风险具有因果性——在固定KL距离下控制方差可减少35–74%的网络验证幻觉；(iv) 此风险结构能逃避自我监测，仅依赖模型输出的概率检测器（如语义熵）对高风险路径的触发率降低约30%（p<10⁻¹⁶），而这些路径却包含近4倍的幻觉内容。大模型更快地雪崩式放大错误，这是一种主导、自我延续且模型自身无法察觉的失效模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大规模语言模型在生成过程中为何在获得更高能力的同时反而更易产生不可靠甚至虚假的回答，尤其是揭示传统知识缺口解释的局限性，并寻找深层次的内在生成机制缺陷。

Method: 通过构建一个同家族更强的推理模型作为参考（oracle），计算每一步生成的分歧度 $\delta = \log p_M - \log p_O$，并将其二阶矩分解为偏差平方 $\mathrm{KL}(p_M \| p_O)^2$ 和风险项 $\mathrm{Var}[\delta]$。利用这一框架系统分析不同规模模型在生成过程中的表现变化，包括知识差距、不确定性演化、幻觉频率及自我监测失效等现象。同时设计控制实验验证因果关系，并评估现有检测方法的有效性。

Result: (i) 随着模型规模增大，知识差距缩小约6倍，但知识退化增长11–39倍；(ii) 模型在幻觉发生时表现出‘自信但脆弱’的状态，自身不确定性快速下降，而基于外部参照的风险持续时间延长至17倍以上，形成连接多个幻觉的危险区间（140亿参数时+69%）；(iii) 该风险具有因果性，通过固定KL距离下的方差收缩可显著降低幻觉比例（35–74%）；(iv) 风险路径对模型自身的检测机制具有隐蔽性，仅使用 $p_M$ 的检测器（如语义熵）在高风险路径上的触发率下降约30%，但此类路径实际含近4倍幻觉内容。

Conclusion: 大规模语言模型在生成中面临一种由自回归机制引发的固有风险——模型一旦选择低概率词元，就会在后续生成中不断强化错误，形成雪球效应。这种失败模式是主导性的、自我延续的、因果性的，且逃逸于模型自身的监控体系。因此，单纯依靠数据、检索或规模扩展无法根本解决可靠性问题，必须从生成机制层面进行干预。

Abstract: As language models scale, answers start truer but degrade faster: scaling buys capability but erodes reliability. The knowledge-gap account - more data, retrieval, or scale - misses an auto-regressive risk residual that scale sharpens: the model commits to a low-probability token, conditions on it as established, and snowballs. We track this through per-position disagreement $δ= \log p_M - \log p_O$ against a stronger same-family oracle, whose second moment splits exactly into bias$^2$ $\mathrm{KL}(p_M \,\|\, p_O)^2$ and risk $\mathrm{Var}[δ]$. We present four findings: (i) under scaling, the knowledge gap falls $\approx$$6\times$ while knowledge degradation grows $11$-$39\times$; (ii) at a fabrication, felt uncertainty $H(p_M)$ relaxes quickly while oracle-referenced risk persists up to $17\times$ longer, leaving a confident-but-precarious risk regime that bridges consecutive fabrications ($+69\%$ at $14$B); (iii) this regime is causal - an on-policy, fixed-$\mathrm{KL}$ variance contraction cuts web-verified hallucination by $35$-$74\%$ across three model families; and, (iv) it structurally evades self-monitoring, with $p_M$-only detectors (e.g. semantic entropy) firing $\approx$$30\%$ less ($p<10^{-16}$) on the risky branch holding nearly $4\times$ more fabrications. Bigger models snowball mistakes faster, through a failure mode that is dominant, self-perpetuating, causal and invisible to the model itself.

</details>


### [141] [One Student, Many Teachers: Multi-Task On-Policy Distillation via Soft-Prompt Privileged Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18293)
*Yingzi Ma,Zichen Zhu,Ming Jiang,Chaowei Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种新的在线自蒸馏方法（OPSD），通过可学习的软提示（soft prompt）构建教师模型，仅在输入端引入任务特定信息，不改变学生模型的权重或表示几何。该方法在单任务和多任务场景下均表现优异：单任务版本性能媲美甚至超过全量微调，参数更新极少；多任务版本在多个任务上取得最佳平均性能（如Qwen3-1.7B-Base上达56.2），且保持通用能力，优于顺序SFT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OPSD方法存在两个问题：一是通过注入特权上下文导致事后解释性偏差，二是通过微调权重引发模型漂移和遗忘。需要一种既能保留学生模型表示结构、又能高效传递知识的新机制。

Method: 使用一个仅由可学习软提示组成的教师模型，其与学生共享骨干网络但不更新权重；教师通过监督$(x, y_{\text{gold}})$对进行训练，生成任务特定的输出；在多任务设置中，不同任务的数据路由至对应软提示教师，实现并行知识吸收；推理时丢弃所有软提示。

Result: 在Qwen3-1.7B-Base和Phi-4-mini-instruct上，单任务版本性能等同或超越全量微调，训练参数量级减少；多任务版本在四个任务上平均得分56.2，优于顺序SFT，且未损害通用能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于软提示的OPSD方法有效解决了现有蒸馏方法中的漂移与遗忘问题，实现了高效、稳定、可扩展的知识迁移，尤其适用于多任务场景下的轻量级持续学习。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) teaches large language models new skills through a teacher that shares the student's backbone and supervises its own rollouts. Existing teachers either inject privileged context at the input -- inducing post-hoc rationalization -- or fine-tune weights, accumulating drift and forgetting across tasks. We propose \method, whose teacher differs from the student only by a learnable soft prompt: trained on $(x, y_\text{gold})$ pairs with the backbone frozen, the prompt yields a task-specific teacher that preserves the student's exact representational geometry. \method\ extends naturally to multi-task settings by routing each example in a merged corpus to its corresponding soft-prompt teacher, allowing a single student to absorb knowledge from $K$ teachers in parallel; at inference, all prompts are discarded. On Qwen3-1.7B-Base and Phi-4-mini-instruct across four tasks (Science, Tool Use, Biology, Math), the single-task variant (OPD with a PT teacher) matches or exceeds full fine-tuning while training orders of magnitude fewer parameters, and the multi-task variant achieves the best overall average ($56.2$ on Qwen3-1.7B-Base) while preserving general-capability benchmarks -- in contrast to sequential SFT, which degrades both.

### [142] [Uncertainty Quantification for AI-Driven Crash Simulation Surrogates: A Comparative Study of Monte Carlo Dropout and Deep Ensemble on Open-Source Bumper Beam Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18294)
*Sudeep Chavare*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究对比了蒙特卡洛丢弃（Monte Carlo Dropout）和深度集成（Deep Ensembles）两种不确定性量化方法在工程仿真替代模型中的表现，使用NVIDIA PhysicsNeMo构建的开源管道，以汽车碰撞仿真中的钢制保险杠梁撞击问题为基准。关键创新在于采用内置的确定性丢弃（concrete dropout），自动学习丢弃率，避免人工调参。结果表明，尽管深度集成通常被视为金标准，但蒙特卡洛丢弃在保持良好校准性和较低计算成本方面更具优势，尤其在无需手动调参的情况下实现了可靠不确定性估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习替代模型在安全关键流程中应用受限，因其仅提供点预测而缺乏不确定性估计，无法判断模型何时不可信。亟需一种既准确又可信赖的不确定性量化方法，以增强工程师对模型输出的信心。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛丢弃与深度集成两种方法，在基于NVIDIA PhysicsNeMo的开源替代模型框架中进行系统比较；引入确定性丢弃机制，实现丢弃率的端到端学习，消除人工超参数依赖；以汽车碰撞仿真为应用场景，通过相同测试集评估点预测精度、不确定性校准程度及计算开销。

Result: 蒙特卡洛丢弃在保持较高预测精度的同时，实现了良好的不确定性校准，且计算成本远低于深度集成；确定性丢弃有效解决了传统蒙特卡洛丢弃中需手动设置丢弃率的问题；研究表明，深度集成并非在所有场景下都是最优选择，存在准确性与校准性之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 在开源工程工作流中，结合确定性丢弃的蒙特卡洛丢弃方法可实现高可靠性、低计算开销且无需超参数调优的不确定性量化，挑战了深度集成作为默认金标准的普遍认知，为工程领域安全可靠的机器学习替代模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Machine learning surrogate models are increasingly being explored in engineering product development to augment simulation-driven design, offering near-instantaneous predictions that complement computationally expensive high-fidelity analyses. However, a critical gap limits their adoption in safety-critical workflows: a point prediction without an accompanying uncertainty estimate cannot tell an engineer when the model should not be trusted. This work presents a systematic, head-to-head comparison of two widely used uncertainty quantification approaches -- Monte Carlo Dropout and Deep Ensembles -- applied to an open-source surrogate pipeline built on NVIDIA PhysicsNeMo. A key contribution is the use of concrete dropout, a built-in PhysicsNeMo capability that eliminates the dropout rate as a manual hyperparameter by learning it end-to-end during training, directly addressing the most common criticism of Monte Carlo Dropout-based uncertainty quantification. Automotive crash simulation is used as the application domain, with a steel bumper beam impact problem serving as the benchmark. Both methods are evaluated on identical held-out simulations and compared on point accuracy, uncertainty band calibration, and computational cost. The results reveal a fundamental trade-off between accuracy and calibration that challenges the common assumption that deep ensembles are the default gold standard for surrogate uncertainty quantification. The findings demonstrate that well-calibrated, hyperparameter-free uncertainty estimates are achievable within a fully open-source engineering workflow at a fraction of the computational cost of ensemble approaches.

### [143] [On the Limits of Support-Preserving Alignment and Bounded Filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18295)
*Aryan Dutt,Rui Mao,Anupam Chattopadhyay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在保持模型内部表示不变的前提下，通过重塑基础模型输出分布的对齐方法与有界安全过滤器结合，是否能将大语言模型中有害行为的概率降至零。研究形式化了支持保持对齐算子与有界过滤算法的设置，并在黑盒、白盒及统计查询访问下分析其逼近理想消除器的能力。理论分析表明，在给定约束下，有界过滤可能无法完全消除基础模型分布所支持的所有有害输出。实证评估显示，无论模型类型、过滤类别或查询预算如何，有害输出率随计算资源增加而下降但始终停留在非零水平，表明存在持续的有害行为下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对齐方法（如基于偏好的对齐）虽能抑制明显有害行为，但无法彻底消除潜在有害输出；同时，外部过滤在最坏情况下可能计算复杂。因此需要明确：在不显著改变内部表示的实用对齐流程中，能否真正实现有害行为的完全消除，而非仅表面抑制。

Method: 构建支持保持对齐算子与有界过滤算法的理论框架，涵盖黑盒、白盒和统计查询三种访问模式；通过计算复杂性与信息论分析论证有界过滤的局限性；在真实场景中使用来自网络安全和PKU-SafeRLHF的对抗性提示，对多款开源与托管大模型进行实证测试，评估不同过滤策略下的有害输出率变化。

Result: 理论分析表明，受约束的有界过滤无法完全消除所有由基础模型分布支持的有害输出；实证结果显示，随着过滤计算资源增加，有害输出率下降但最终趋于稳定且高于零，证明存在一个不可逾越的有害行为下限。

Conclusion: 即使采用先进的对齐技术与有界过滤，现代大语言模型仍难以将有害行为概率降为零。这表明当前方法只能抑制而非根除有害输出，必须重新思考模型安全性设计的根本范式。

Abstract: We study whether alignment schemes that reshape a base model's output distribution, combined with bounded safety filters, can drive the probability of harmful behavior to zero in modern large language models. Recent research suggests that harmful behaviors can persist under preference-based alignment and that external filtering can be computationally hard in the worst case, but it remains unclear whether practical alignment pipelines that largely preserve internal representations can eliminate harmful behavior entirely rather than merely suppressing its most visible forms. We formalize this setting using support-preserving alignment operators together with bounded filtering algorithms under black-box, white-box, and statistical-query access, and analyze their ability to approximate an ideal eliminator that removes all harmful mass. Building on this framework, we provide computational and information-theoretic arguments indicating that, under these constraints, bounded filtering may fail to eliminate all harmful outputs supported by the base model's distribution. To evaluate these limits empirically, we analyze a range of state-of-the-art open-weight and hosted LLMs accessed via OpenRouter under bounded black-box, white-box, and statistical-query filters on adversarial prompts drawn from curated cybersecurity scenarios and PKU-SafeRLHF. Across models, filter classes, and query budgets, the estimated harmful-output rate decreases with additional filtering compute but consistently plateaus above zero, suggesting a persistent empirical harm floor.

### [144] [A Better Start for Language Models: Domain-Conditional Position Offsets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18302)
*Ye Qiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种轻量级的领域条件位置偏移（domain-conditional position offset）方法，通过在序列开头添加一个可学习向量来缓解自回归语言模型在序列起始阶段因上下文不足导致的性能下降问题。该方法仅需少量文档训练几分钟，无需修改模型权重，无延迟开销，在多个大小从410M到8B参数的模型上将领域内困惑度降低高达27%，且效果在70B模型中依然有效。相比直接的logit偏置修正或LoRA等方法，该偏移能通过模型状态传播影响整体输出，而非仅调整输出分布。尽管其并非最强适配器，但作为可快速切换、低资源消耗的工具，特别适用于短文本的领域评分与校准任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归语言模型在序列起始阶段由于缺乏上下文，依赖通用预训练先验，导致性能下降，尤其在特定领域任务中表现不佳。如何在不增加计算负担的前提下提升模型在序列开头的准确性成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出领域条件位置偏移：在序列初始位置加入一个可学习的向量，作用于嵌入激活层，所有模型权重保持冻结。该偏移向量根据领域动态切换，训练仅需约一百篇文档，时间短，无额外推理延迟。

Result: 在8个不同规模的Mamba、GPT-NeoX和Llama模型上，该方法使领域内困惑度降低最多达27%；在70B模型上仍有效；单个位置即可捕获大部分收益。相较于直接logit偏置修正（最高仅降7.9%）和LoRA（参数多、路径活跃），该方法更高效且不影响后续token损失。在检索重排序与领域分类任务中显著提升早期关键信息判断能力，对后期信号依赖任务无负面影响。位置感知的prefill应用有助于生成任务，而盲目每步缓存应用会导致重复。

Conclusion: 该位置偏移是一种轻量、快速切换、零延迟的领域校准工具，特别适合短文本中的领域敏感评分与初始化优化，虽非最强适配器，但具有极高的实用价值。

Abstract: Autoregressive language models are least accurate at the beginning of a sequence, where little context forces reliance on a generic pretraining prior. We show that this cold-start penalty is domain dependent and reduce it with a domain-conditional position offset: a single learned vector added to the embedding activation at the first sequence positions while all model weights remain frozen. The offset trains in minutes on roughly one hundred documents, switches between domains without added sequence state, and has no measurable latency overhead. Across eight Mamba, GPT-NeoX, and Llama models spanning 410M to 8B parameters, it reduces held-out in-domain perplexity by up to 27%; the effect persists at 70B, and one position captures most of the benefit. A matched, converged direct logit-bias correction reaches at most only 7.9% and leaves later-token loss unchanged, showing that the offset propagates through model state rather than merely recalibrating the output prior. A tuned LoRA reaches lower perplexity but uses two to three orders of magnitude more parameters and an active low-rank weight path, while soft prompts add sequence positions. With wrong-domain controls, offsets improve retrieval reranking and domain classification when decisions depend on early in-domain tokens, For the few-shot reasoning whose signal occurs later, the results maintains unchanged. Position-aware prefill application also help generation tasks, whereas naive application at every cached decoding step causes repetition. The offset is therefore not the strongest adapter, but a lightweight, hot switchable tool for short in-domain scoring and calibration.

### [145] [TD-DPO: Difference-Aware Preference Optimization for Mitigating Sycophancy in Clinical Autism Intervention Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18304)
*Shuzhong Lai,Junhong Lai,Chenxi Li,Qing Zhou,Haifeng Li,Gang Pan,Lin Yao,Yueming Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MEDA数据增强策略和TD-DPO token级差异直接偏好优化方法，通过构建最小编辑的偏好对并聚焦于响应中差异性标记，有效抑制模型在干预对话中的奉承行为，同时保持干预能力，实现安全与效果之间的更好平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在自闭症儿童干预对话中存在奉承行为，可能增加安全风险；现有基于正例的微调方法难以有效识别和纠正失败模式，且序列级偏好优化易导致无关标记的过度更新，影响干预能力。

Method: 提出MEDA策略生成可控、稳定的最小编辑偏好对，并设计TD-DPO方法，通过上权重选择与拒绝响应间的差异标记，下权重共享标记，抑制背景漂移。

Result: 在多个模型架构和评估者下，TD-DPO在离线设置中实现了奉承行为缓解与干预能力保留之间的更优权衡，展现出在自闭症干预中实用的对齐潜力。

Conclusion: TD-DPO通过聚焦于响应中的差异性标记，能够有效减少大语言模型在自闭症干预对话中的奉承行为，同时维持其干预能力，是一种具有实际应用前景的对齐方法。

Abstract: The sycophancy of large language models can increase the safety risk in intervention dialogue for autistic children. Supervised fine-tuning can somewhat reduce sycophancy, but relying solely on positive examples is often insufficient to identify and correct failure patterns. We observe that sycophancy behaviors can often be localized to a limited span within the model response. In this regime, sequence-level preference optimization can over-update preference-irrelevant tokens and degrade intervention ability. To address this, we propose the \textbf{M}inimal \textbf{E}dit \textbf{D}ata \textbf{A}ugmentation (MEDA) strategy to construct controlled, stable, minimal edit preference pairs and \textbf{T}oken-level \textbf{D}ifference \textbf{D}irect \textbf{P}reference \textbf{O}ptimization (TD-DPO), which upweights difference tokens between chosen and rejected responses while downweighting shared tokens to suppress background drift. Extensive experiments across multiple backbones and evaluators show that TD-DPO achieves a better trade-off between sycophancy mitigation and intervention ability retention in our offline settings, highlighting its potential as a practical alignment approach for autism intervention.

### [146] [The Information Shadow: Measuring Structural Limits on What Language Models Can Learn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18305)
*Priyansh Srivastava,Romit Chatterjee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“信息阴影”概念，指语言模型因文本训练的结构性限制而无法学习到的现象，分为三类：(I) 语言无法表达的结构；(II) 统计上不可从训练数据中识别的函数；(III) 可表示但梯度训练无法到达的函数。通过三种探测方法分别验证：语言压缩残差显示文本模型存在可计算的表达上限；反事实区分测试表明模型行为由归纳偏置决定，少量歧义数据即可双向引导；盆地逃逸映射显示某些可表示函数在标准训练下完全无法达到，即使邻近初始化也瞬间可达。所有效应均通过对照实验排除容量或模态干扰。研究呼吁改进基准设计、能力审计与不确定性评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示语言模型的知识局限并非源于数据覆盖不足，而是文本训练本身带来的结构性缺陷，旨在识别并量化这些根本性限制。

Method: 提出信息阴影理论框架，设计三类可证明的探测任务：(I) 语言压缩残差对比（文本学习者 vs 全信号学习者）；(II) 反事实区分测试（双规则一致数据下模型行为依赖归纳偏置）；(III) 盆地逃逸映射（构造可表示但难训练的函数，验证训练路径敏感性）。每类均配有控制实验以排除非结构性因素影响。

Result: 三类信息阴影效应均被实证：(I) 文本学习者表达能力存在固定天花板，随数据量增加差距不减；(II) 模型在反事实判断上受归纳偏置主导，5%歧义数据可完全逆转行为；(III) 构造函数虽可表示却在标准训练下0%成功率，邻近初始化即瞬达，宽度扩展无效。所有结果具有统计显著性。

Conclusion: 语言模型的能力受限于文本训练的结构性缺陷，而非数据规模。这些限制包括语言表达能力边界、统计不可识别性及训练优化路径陷阱。研究强调需发展面向信息阴影的评估机制，推动更稳健的模型设计与可信的不确定性建模。

Abstract: Some limits on what language models know are not gaps in data coverage but structural properties of learning from text. We introduce the information shadow: the region of phenomena that a text-trained learner cannot acquire regardless of scale, comprising (I) structures language cannot express, (II) functions that are statistically non-identifiable from the training distribution, and (III) functions that are representable but unreachable by gradient-based training. We give each type a probe that is decisive because the premise of the shadow is, in that setting, provable. For Type I, Language Compression Residuals compare a text learner, which sees only a lossy text-like encoding of the signal, against a full-signal learner, which sees the underlying signal directly. The text learner sits at a computable expressibility ceiling while the full-signal learner pulls away by a gap that stays flat across 300x more data, so the deficit is a property of the channel, not of training. For Type II, the Counterfactual Distinction Test trains models on data exactly consistent with two incompatible rules. Across a provable string task and a language-like agreement task, behavior on counterfactuals is set by the model's inductive bias, while 5% disambiguating data steers the learned rule bidirectionally to either target (r = +/-1.0, p < 1e-10). For Type III, Basin Escape Mapping exhibits a function that is representable at 100% (by hand construction) yet reached 0% of the time by standard training and instantly from a nearby initialization, with width scaling providing no help (p = 1.6 x 10^-14). Each effect is isolated by a control that rules out a capacity or modality artifact. We release the probe suite and discuss implications for benchmark design, capability auditing, and shadow-aware uncertainty.

</details>


### [147] [Gradient-Energy Guided Block-Wise Perturbations for Sharpness-Aware Minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18306)
*Zhen Huang,Jiaxin Deng,Junbiao Pang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GEAR-SAM 提出一种自适应梯度能量的 SAM 方法，通过指数移动平均（EMA）平方块梯度作为敏感性信号，动态分配固定扰动预算，无需海森向量积或显式费雪估计，仅增加标量状态，提升了图像分类、迁移学习、噪声标签学习等任务中的泛化与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 SAM 的全局扰动预算在参数块间的分配依赖于瞬时小批量梯度范数，存在噪声且不能反映训练过程中各模块累积的敏感性变化。需要更稳定、动态适应的预算分配机制以提升泛化性能。

Method: 引入指数移动平均（EMA）的平方块梯度作为轻量级曲率相关敏感性信号，通过闭式约束优化重新分配 SAM 固定扰动预算，保持全局半径不变，不需额外计算复杂项。

Result: 在图像分类、迁移学习、噪声标签学习及模块划分实验中，GEAR-SAM 在多种架构和任务上均表现出更强的泛化能力与鲁棒性，验证了动态预算分配的有效性。

Conclusion: GEAR-SAM 为尖锐感知优化提供了动态视角：固定的扰动预算应随网络功能模块敏感性的演化而重新分配，是一种高效、轻量且通用的改进方法。

Abstract: Sharpness-Aware Minimization (SAM) improves generalization by minimizing the worst-case loss in a local parameter neighborhood. Standard SAM implicitly allocates its global perturbation budget across parameter blocks according to instantaneous minibatch gradient norms. Such an allocation can be noisy and may not reflect the sensitivity that blocks accumulate throughout training. We propose Gradient-Energy Adaptive Radius SAM (GEAR-SAM), which maintains an exponential moving average (EMA) of squared block gradients as a lightweight, curvature-related sensitivity signal and allocates the fixed SAM budget through a closed-form constrained optimization. GEAR-SAM preserves the global SAM radius, requires no Hessian-vector products or explicit Fisher estimation, and adds only scalar state beyond SAM. Experiments on image classification, transfer learning, noisy-label learning, and partition studies demonstrate improved generalization and robustness across architectures and tasks. More broadly, GEAR-SAM provides a dynamic view of sharpness-aware optimization: a fixed perturbation budget should be redistributed as the sensitivity of functional network blocks evolves during training.

</details>


### [148] [Agentic Calibration of Grey-Box Simulation Models: An LLM-Driven Alternative](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18308)
*David Gómez-Guillén,Mireia Diaz,Josep Lluis Arcos,Jesús Cerquides*

Method: 引入基于大语言模型的代理优化器，将约束以自然语言形式嵌入系统提示，使模型自主生成搜索策略并评估参数，同时具备可审计与可解释性。

Abstract: Calibration of grey-box simulation models is a constrained optimization problem in which model evaluations are expensive, the parameter space can be high-dimensional, and the search must respect plausibility constraints. Although the simulation code is fully available to the analyst, the joint effect of multiple parameters remains difficult to predict analytically. Classical optimizers such as Nelder--Mead (NM) are simple to deploy but sample-inefficient, particularly under constraints. Modern Bayesian Optimization methods achieve competitive solutions with far fewer evaluations but require non-trivial modeling machinery for constraint handling. We introduce an agentic calibration method in which a large language model acts as the optimizer, with constraints incorporated as a plain-language section of the system prompt. We evaluate the agentic method, NM, and Bayesian Optimization (BO) on an anal cancer simulation model under both unconstrained and clinically constrained calibration. Under unconstrained calibration, the agentic method achieves substantially lower best error than BO and NM, while requiring fewer model evaluations. Under constrained calibration, the agentic method reaches comparable error levels and both outperform NM. These results are obtained at the cost of increased inference time per iteration. Agentic calibration achieves competitive performance with substantially fewer model evaluations, and constraint handling is essentially free at the modeller-facing interface through simple textual specifications rather than additional modelling machinery. The main trade-off lies in increased per-iteration inference cost, making the approach particularly suitable when simulation time dominates. Beyond performance, the per-iteration rationale makes the search auditable and explainable, so its decisions can be scrutinised and justified to third parties.

### [149] [Spatio-Temporal Prediction of Unsteady Airfoil Aerodynamics Using Augmented Graph Neural Ordinary Differential Equations with Exogenous Controls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18309)
*Henrik Lange,Reik Thormann,Philipp Bekemeyer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为GNODE的新型方法，结合图神经网络（GNN）与增强型神经微分方程，用于稳定预测非定常气动力学中的表面力。该方法在时间上更稳定、空间上更平滑，并且比自回归GNN基线更具准确性，特别适用于包含跨音速激波、瞬态行为和动态非线性的俯仰机翼系统。通过引入额外的隐状态维度，进一步提升了模型表达能力和精度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于图神经网络与增强神经微分方程结合的方法——GNODE。通过在离散空间域上操作的图神经网络，利用神经微分方程实现连续时间演化，避免了自回归过程中的误差累积。同时引入额外的隐状态维度以捕捉历史依赖关系，提升模型表达能力。

Result: GNODE在预测俯仰机翼表面力时表现出更高的时间稳定性、空间平滑性和整体准确性，优于自回归GNN基线。尤其在包含跨音速激波、瞬态行为和动态非线性的复杂场景中表现优异。增加隐状态维度显著提升了模型的拟合能力与泛化性能。

Conclusion: GNODE是一种有效建模具有外部输入的非线性时空系统的新兴方法，具备高速度、高稳定性与高精度优势，适用于航空器设计、优化与认证中的非定常气动力建模任务。

Abstract: Unsteady aerodynamic phenomena, such as gusts, turbulence, and fluid-structure interactions affect an aircraft during flight. For design, optimisation and certification, it is indispensable to quantify such unsteady aerodynamic effects. Industry-standard computational fluid dynamics methods, such as solving the unsteady Reynolds-averaged Navier-Stokes equations or the linearized frequency domain method, are either computationally expensive or restricted by assumptions like linearity. Once trained, machine learning methods are capable of computing non-linear relationships very fast, making them suitable as surrogate models. By autoregressively applying graph neural networks (GNNs), operating on a discretised spatial domain, spatio-temporal predictions can be made. However, autoregressive GNNs suffer from error accumulation leading to unstable rollouts over time. Here we show that combining GNNs with augmented Neural Ordinary Differential Equations yields temporally stable predictions of the surface forces on a pitching airfoil. We found that our approach, called GNODE, based on Graph Neural Ordinary Differential Equations, provides temporally more stable, spatially smoother, and overall more accurate results than an autoregressive GNN baseline. Tests are conducted on a dataset consisting of a simulations of a pitching airfoil, including transonic shocks, transient behaviour and dynamic non-linearities. Augmenting GNODEs with additional latent dimensions improves the expressivity and accuracy by capturing underlying history effects. The developed method demonstrates an approach that is suitable to model non-linear spatio-temporal systems with exogenous inputs.

### [151] [Cost Accounting for Reactive Computational Graphs: Exhaustive Sweeps, Sequential Mutation, and the Backward-Locality Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18323)
*Abdallah Khemais*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究神经网络计算图中逐节点干预（如激活修补、电路发现、系统性消融）的计算成本，提出在反应式图引擎下对这些操作的完整成本分析。首先，全重计算的遍历扫面速度提升并非恒定常数：当权重随深度呈Karamata指数q分布时，速度比趋近于(q+2)/(q+1)（输出集中）或q+2（输入集中），仅在深度均匀时为2；实际壁钟时间上限约为1.79，低于2，直到解释器开销被消除。其次，证明了持久性突变序列的成本：交错执行成本超过孤立求和，其超额部分由可比较节点对的贡献构成，不同插入顺序有闭式极值；而批量应用则与顺序无关且次可加，成本等于各突变节点锥形区域并集加上新生成节点。第三，证明反向传播下存在前向局部性的镜像——无长跳跃连接的架构中，反向传播使整体加速比坍缩至1。所有结论均在Julia语言中的NeuroDSL反应式图引擎上验证，测量的扫面比率收敛至理论极限，训练模式下的加速比按预测速率降为1，且18个逐块序列成本及批量总成本在三种插入顺序下均精确匹配闭式解，误差为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络干预方法（如激活修补、电路发现、消融研究）需在每个候选节点进行突变并重新计算，计算成本高昂，尤其受限于重复计算开销。当前缺乏对这类工作负载在反应式图引擎下的系统性成本建模与优化指导。本文旨在揭示此类操作的理论成本边界，提供可预测、可优化的计算框架，以推动高效神经网络可解释性研究。

Method: 基于反应式图引擎的精确无效化机制（仅影响下游锥形区域），建立数学模型分析三类场景：(1) 独立全重计算的遍历扫面；(2) 持久性突变序列的交错执行与批量处理；(3) 反向传播下的局部性行为。采用渐近分析、组合计数与图结构推导，推导出各类情况下的精确成本表达式，并通过形式化证明建立闭式解。所有理论结果在NeuroDSL平台实现并严格验证。

Result: 1. 遍历扫面的聚合加速比非恒定，受权重分布影响，最大约1.79，低于理想2倍；2. 持久突变交错执行导致额外开销，但批量处理具次可加性与顺序无关性；3. 无长跳跃连接的反向传播使整体加速比坍缩至1；4. 所有理论预测在NeuroDSL上通过四类成本配置、三种插入顺序、18个子任务和批量总成本的精确匹配得到验证，误差为零。

Conclusion: 本文建立了神经网络干预型工作负载在反应式图引擎下的完整成本理论，揭示了加速比的非理想性、批量处理的优势以及反向传播对局部性的破坏。该理论不仅解释了现有实验现象，也为高效可解释性研究提供了设计准则，表明应优先使用批量突变，并警惕反向传播带来的性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Exhaustive site-by-site interventions on a neural network's computational graph -- activation-patching sweeps, circuit-discovery searches, systematic ablation studies -- mutate the graph at every candidate site, and their cost is dominated by recomputation after each mutation. On a reactive graph engine whose invalidation provably touches exactly the downstream cone of a mutated node, we give a complete cost accounting for such workloads. First, the aggregate speedup of an exhaustive sweep over independent full recomputations is not a universal constant: if per-layer weight varies regularly with depth at Karamata index q, the ratio converges to (q+2)/(q+1) when weight concentrates near the output and to q+2 near the input, recovering 2 only in the depth-uniform case; a wall-clock corollary predicts a ceiling of about 1.79, below 2, until interpreter overhead is compiled away. Second, we prove the exact cost of a sequence of persistent mutations, never undone between insertions: the interleaved cost exceeds the isolated sum by an exact overcount summed over comparable site pairs, with closed-form extremes over insertion orders, while batched application is order-independent and sub-additive, costing exactly the union of the sites' cones plus the fresh nodes. Third, we prove the exact mirror of forward locality for the backward pass, showing it collapses the aggregate speedup to 1 under backpropagation on architectures without long skip connections. Every identity is validated on NeuroDSL, a reactive graph engine in Julia: measured sweep ratios converge to the predicted limits under four cost profiles; the training-mode ratio collapses to 1 at the predicted rate; and all 18 per-graft sequential costs and the batched total match the closed forms at zero tolerance across three insertion orders.

</details>


### [152] [Dynamic Loss Balancing for Joint SOH and RUL Prediction of Lithium-Ion Batteries via a Rotary SOH-Injected Prior Battery Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18329)
*Shuhao Chen,Tianyu Shi,Yiwen Huang,Chengyi Tu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出RoSIP-Batt框架，通过贝叶斯多任务学习与动态不确定性加权机制，解决锂离子电池SOH与RUL联合预测中的异方差性问题，结合旋转位置编码与物理先验注入，显著提升预测精度与实时部署能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多任务学习难以平衡SOH估计的低方差噪声与RUL预测的高不确定性，限制了电池健康管理系统的可靠性与实用性。

Method: 采用贝叶斯多任务优化框架，引入同方差不确定性加权机制，利用解耦双分类标记与逐维度门控融合，结合梯度分离操作防止高方差更新干扰稳定表示；引入旋转位置嵌入（RoPE）建模相对时间模式，并将中间SOH估计作为物理先验注入RUL回归头。

Conclusion: RoSIP-Batt为电池健康状态与剩余使用寿命联合预测提供了高泛化性、计算高效且适用于实时嵌入式电池管理系统部署的解决方案。

Abstract: The deployment of reliable lithium-ion battery management systems is crucial for accelerating electrification, yet the joint prognosis of State of Health (SOH) and Remaining Useful Life (RUL) remains severely hindered by task heteroscedasticity. Conventional multi-task learning frameworks fail to balance the bounded, low-variance noise of SOH estimation with the unbounded, nonlinearly expanding uncertainty of long-term RUL predictions. Here, we present the Rotary SOH-Injected Prior Battery Transformer (RoSIP-Batt), a unified co-estimation framework that resolves these optimization conflicts. By formulating joint prediction as a Bayesian multi-task objective, RoSIP-Batt introduces a homoscedastic uncertainty weighting mechanism to dynamically scale task-specific gradients based on learned residual noise levels. The architecture leverages decoupled dual classification tokens and a per-dimension gated fusion mechanism, secured by a gradient-detachment operator to prevent high-variance RUL updates from corrupting the stable SOH representation space. To capture electrochemical degradation patterns without relying on absolute cycle steps, Rotary Position Embedding (RoPE) is incorporated into a shared Transformer backbone to model translation-invariant relative temporal profiles. Crucially, the intermediate SOH estimate is directly injected into the RUL regression head as a physical degradation prior. Evaluations across the NASA, MIT-Stanford, and HUST datasets show that RoSIP-Batt significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing SOH estimation error to 1.994% MAE on NASA and restricting RUL prediction error to 62.85 cycles on Stanford. These findings establish RoSIP-Batt as a highly generalizable, computationally efficient solution suitable for real-time embedded BMS deployment.

### [154] [ChemHyperMag: Physics-informed magnetic hypergraph learning improves molecular ADMET prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18332)
*Hexiao Ding,Hongzhao Chen,Jing Lan,Yufeng Jiang,Zihong Luo,Zehua Xiong,Tianlong Ruan,Yunlin Mao,Nga Chun Ng,Gwing Kei Yip,Gerald W. Y. Cheng,Kate Inyoung Oh,Jing Cai,Liang-Ting Lin,Jung Sun Yoo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ChemHyperMag 提出一种基于功能基团超图的多任务 ADMET 预测方法，通过引入电负性和 Gasteiger 电荷驱动的不可逆流，利用厄米磁拉普拉斯算子和磁 Chebyshev 编码器建模分子中的方向性与非对称相互作用，并通过扰动磁相位生成随机视图，以 InfoNCE 目标进行训练。该方法在少量标注样本下表现优异，无需构象信息，具备可解释的方向信号输出，在多个 ADMET 基准测试中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于环、BRICS 片段、Bemis-Murcko 骨架和键的功能基团超图；定义由电负性和 Gasteiger 电荷驱动的非可逆流动；使用厄米磁拉普拉斯算子编码循环结构；采用磁 Chebyshev 编码器处理图结构；通过扰动磁相位生成随机视图，并以 InfoNCE 损失函数进行训练。

Result: 在多个 ADMET 基准数据集上，ChemHyperMag 在标签稀疏情况下显著优于现有方法，无需使用分子构象，具有良好的可扩展性，并能提供可解释的方向性信号（磁相位）。

Conclusion: ChemHyperMag 通过引入方向性与非对称性建模，有效提升了 ADMET 预测性能，尤其在小样本场景下表现突出，同时提供了可解释的化学机制线索，为药物发现中的分子设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of ADMET (Absorption, Distribution, Metabolism, Excretion, and Toxicity) is important for drug discovery. Most predictors use undirected molecular graphs and pairwise edges. This choice misses asymmetric interactions, nonreversible dynamics, and motif level effects from functional groups and ring systems. We propose ChemHyperMag for multitask ADMET prediction under missing labels. ChemHyperMag builds a functional group hypergraph from rings, BRICS fragments, Bemis-Murcko scaffolds, and bonds. It also defines a potential driven nonreversible flow guided by electronegativity and Gasteiger partial charges. The resulting circulation is encoded by a Hermitian magnetic Laplacian and processed with a magnetic Chebyshev encoder. We perturb magnetic phases to form stochastic views and train with an InfoNCE objective. Experiments on multiple ADMET benchmarks show improvements over recent methods with fewer labeled samples and no conformers. ChemHyperMag is scalable and provides interpretable directional signals through its magnetic phases.

</details>


### [155] [Federated Lightweight Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18343)
*Radhakrishna Achanta,Will Reed*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FLITE提出一种低带宽联邦微调方法，通过映射网络将模型权重从可学习的低维潜在变量生成，利用共享的仿射投影实现潜在变量平均即等价于权重平均。结合低秩可再生分解与增量修正公式，显著降低通信开销（仅5KB/客户端/轮次），实现8718倍压缩，且在CIFAR-100上达到接近全参数联邦平均的精度（74.67%），在非独立同分布（non-IID）场景下表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦微调方法如FedAvg和梯度压缩面临通信开销大、压缩效率有限的问题。如何在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅降低通信量成为关键挑战。

Method: 采用基于映射网络的权重生成机制，使用低秩、可再生的仿射投影结构，设计增量修正公式θ=θ^pre + UV^T z，并引入冻结正交分类头，实现低带宽下的高效联邦学习。

Result: 在CIFAR-100上，每轮仅需传输约5KB数据（1280浮点数），相比传统方法减少8718倍；精度达74.67%，与全参数FedAvg相差不足0.5个百分点；在int4量化下可进一步压缩至648字节，且保持准确率，而全参数int4 FedAvg性能退化至随机水平。

Conclusion: FLITE通过巧妙的权重生成与通信设计，在极低通信开销下实现了高精度联邦微调，尤其适用于资源受限或非独立同分布场景，是当前联邦学习通信优化的重要突破。

Abstract: Federated fine-tuning is bottlenecked by communication: FedAvg and pseudo-gradient schemes transmit a payload that scales with the model, and gradient compression shrinks it by only a constant factor. We take a different lever. Mapping networks generate a network's weights from a small trainable latent through a frozen affine projection; because the map is shared and affine, averaging latents is exactly averaging the generated weights. We turn this into a practical low-bandwidth federated channel with two changes: a low-rank, seed-regenerable factorisation of the projection (cutting generator memory from ~80 GB to ~10 MB), and a delta formulation $θ= θ^{\mathrm{pre}} + U V^{\top} z$ that learns an additive correction around a shared centrally-pretrained base -- federated fine-tuning, which is what makes the method work at scale. A frozen orthogonal classifier head further removes the head from the payload while improving accuracy. On CIFAR-100 with ResNet-18+GroupNorm, our method (FLITE, Federated Low-rank Iterative Training Engine) communicates 1,280 floats (~5 KB) per client per round -- an 8718x reduction -- and reaches 74.67%, within ~0.5 pp of full-weight FedAvg. The averaging identity holds to floating-point precision ($6 \times 10^{-8}$); the method sits one to two orders of magnitude below PowerSGD and top-k on the bandwidth-accuracy Pareto; it matches or exceeds full-weight FedAvg under strong non-IID skew. int4 latents reach 648 bytes per round at unchanged accuracy, whereas int4 full-weight FedAvg collapses to chance.

### [156] [An Analysis of Residual-Stream Geometry Across Transformer Depth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18348)
*Sunit Bhattacharya,Ravi Shankar Kolli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种以过渡为中心的Transformer残差流几何分析方法，通过相对位移和正交Procrustes分析揭示了模型层间表示变化的可重复深度规律。结果显示，相对位移在早期和晚期层较大，中间层较平稳，且在各任务条件下保持稳定；旋转幅度基本恒定，而残差和角度集中度随深度变化，最终层残差达到峰值。非英语目标生成时，最终层的位移和残差更大。这些发现为残差流过渡提供了测量框架，并表明深度曲线具有模型特异性且条件稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Transformer模型中残差流在不同层之间的动态变化模式，探索其在不同任务下的稳定性与一致性，为模型内部行为提供几何视角的描述性分析。

Method: 采用相对位移测量表示层间移动距离，利用正交Procrustes分析将每层过渡分解为刚性旋转与非刚性残差成分，系统分析六种指令微调模型在代码生成与跨语言翻译任务中的表现。

Result: 观察到相对位移在层间呈现特定深度模式（两头高、中间低），旋转幅度近似恒定，残差与角度集中度随深度变化，最终层残差最大；非英语任务下最终层的位移和残差显著高于英语任务。所有模式在模型内高度一致，但跨模型存在差异。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一个用于分析残差流过渡的几何测量框架，揭示出在所研究设置下，深度曲线具有模型依赖性和条件稳定性，为理解Transformer内部动态提供了新的描述性规律。

Abstract: We propose a transition-centred geometric analysis of transformer residual streams. Relative displacement measures how \emph{far} representations move between consecutive layers, and orthogonal Procrustes analysis separates each transition into a rigid rotation and a non-rigid residual. Across six instruction-tuned models, on code generation and cross-lingual translation, these measurements reveal reproducible depth regularities. Relative displacement is strongly layer-dependent; typically larger early and late, with a quieter middle third; and nearly invariant across conditions within each model. Rotation magnitude is nearly constant across depth, while Procrustes residual and angle concentration remain depth-modulated, with residual peaking at the final transition. During generation, non-English targets show larger final-layer displacement and residual than English targets. We present these as descriptive geometric regularities, not as measures of computational effort or causal explanations. The contribution is a measurement framework for residual-stream transitions and evidence that, in the settings studied here, depth curves are model-dependent and largely condition-stable.

Abstract: In traffic accident risk prediction, most studies overlook the extra noise that could be incorporated when fusing temporal features into spatial features, and some models struggle to capture global correlations among spatial regions. Finally, we propose a MambaLSTM unit to efficiently capture long- and short-term temporal dependencies for identifying dynamic risk patterns. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate the proposed model's superiority over state-of-the-art methods. The code is released at https://github.com/Zhenzovo/MambaLSTM.

### [158] [Multi-layer MIMO Relay as Deep Physical Neural Networks: Power Amplifiers as Activation Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18354)
*Meng Hua,Itsik Bergel,Deniz Gündüz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种深度无线物理神经网络（WPNN），通过多跳多输入多输出（MIMO）中继网络实现非线性激活，利用功率放大器的固有非线性作为激活函数，并支持端到端训练。设计了两种收发机方案，分别适用于仅接收端或双端信道状态信息（CSI）的情况，仿真结果表明该架构能实现高精度的空中推理，尤其凸显了利用硬件非线性的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数字神经网络存在能耗和延迟较高的问题，而将神经计算直接嵌入模拟硬件的无线物理神经网络（WPNN）可显著降低功耗与延迟。然而，如何有效利用硬件中的非线性特性来增强计算能力仍是一个挑战。为此，本文旨在设计一种基于硬件非线性的深度WPNN，以提升推理性能并实现高效过空气推理。

Method: 提出一种基于多跳MIMO中继网络的深度WPNN架构，每个中继节点执行可训练的复数线性增益与偏置，其后由功率放大器的固有非线性作为激活函数。通过级联多个中继节点，形成空中全连接网络，参数可端到端训练。针对不同信道状态信息（CSI）可用性，设计了基于最小二乘法（LS）的接收端CSI方案和基于奇异值分解（SVD）的双端CSI方案。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提架构能够实现高精度的图像分类过空气推理。在不同信道条件下，两种收发机设计均表现出良好性能；特别地，利用硬件非线性显著提升了系统的推理能力，验证了其有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: 本工作成功构建了一种可端到端训练的深度无线物理神经网络，通过巧妙利用功率放大器的非线性特性实现激活函数，有效提升了过空气推理的精度与效率。该方法为低功耗、低延迟智能无线系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Wireless physical neural networks (WPNNs) embed neural computation directly into analog hardware, offering lower energy consumption and latency than conventional digital implementations. In this paper, we propose a deep WPNN in which nonlinear activations are realized by a multi-hop multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) relay network, in which each relay implements a trainable complex linear gain and bias, followed by the power amplifier's intrinsic nonlinearity acting as an activation function. The cascade of multiple relays therefore realizes an over-the-air fully connected network whose parameters can be trained end-to-end. We develop two transceiver designs for different channel state information (CSI) availability scenarios: a least squares (LS)-based scheme requiring only receiver-side CSI, and a singular-value-decomposition (SVD)-based scheme requiring both transmitter-side and receiver-side CSI. Simulation results show that the proposed architecture enables accurate over-the-air inference for image classification. In particular, the results highlight the advantage of exploiting hardware nonlinearity for enhanced inference capability.

*Yuyang Leng,Renyuan Liu,Shaohan Hu,Peijun Zhao,Chun-Fu Chen,Songqing Chen,Shuochao Yao*

Abstract: Deep neural networks have become a promising approach for IMU-based sensing, but their scalability is fundamentally limited by costly labeled data and poor robustness to heterogeneous devices, placements, and users. Existing unsupervised and self-supervised methods reduce but do not remove this dependence, still requiring labeled data for domain adaptation and largely ignoring known physical structure. We propose physical self-supervised learning, an autoencoder-style paradigm for label-free IMU sensing. We replace the conventional neural decoder with an auto-adaptive physics decoder, a learnable family of kinematic equations that enforces explicit physical structure while adapting across environments, and adopt a hybrid two-stage IMU encoder with reconstruction in a structured latent space to mitigate sensor noise. Our framework further introduces probabilistic frequency-spatial constraints to disentangle sensor and object motion, a multi-view kinematic tree to exploit sparse physical self-supervised signals, and an uncertainty-aware formulation to handle the inherent ambiguity of IMU inference. Evaluated on inertial tracking and full-body motion capture over public datasets and realistic deployments, physical self-supervised learning reduces errors by up to 5x for tracking and 4x for motion capture in challenging generalization scenarios, consistently outperforming state-of-the-art supervised and self-supervised baselines without any labels.

### [160] [A Controlled Study of Attention-Only Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18363)
*Henry Ndubuaku,Karen Mosoyan,Jakub Mroz,Noah Cylich,Satyajit Kumar,Parkirat Sandhu,Roman Shemet,Justin H Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比标准Transformer与仅使用注意力机制的解码器（SANs），在参数量、计算量和深度三方面严格匹配的情况下，验证了前馈网络在Transformer中的必要性。结果表明，移除前馈层会带来性能下降，但通过将释放的计算资源重新分配给注意力层深度，可显著缩小差距，甚至在大模型规模下差距趋近于零。性能差异主要集中在依赖权重知识的任务上，而注意力机制本身足以支撑大部分任务，尤其在大规模预训练中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究前馈网络在Transformer架构中的必要性，尤其是在控制参数量、计算量和深度的前提下，以评估其对模型性能的实际贡献。

Method: 构建并预训练仅含注意力机制的解码器（SANs），与标准Transformer在参数量、训练浮点运算数（FLOPs）和层数（2至48层）上分别进行精确匹配，覆盖从600万到8700万参数及最多1050亿词元的训练数据。通过系统性消融实验，分析不同配置下的性能差异，并结合权重谱分析、注意力机制行为观察等手段，定位性能差距来源。

Result: 在参数量匹配条件下，仅注意力模型与标准模型的性能差距仅为0.006 nats（约0.27%损失），且随模型规模增大进一步缩小；在大模型尺度下，差距稳定在0.02 nats以内。性能差异主要出现在依赖模型权重的知识密集型任务中，而上下文感知任务表现接近。权重谱分析显示，注意力矩阵（Q/K）早期就趋于稳定，内容矩阵秩增长缓慢，移除前馈层后，该信息积累被转移到注意力输出投影层。此外，QK归一化而非前馈层或残差门控是维持深层注意力堆栈训练可行性的关键。

Conclusion: 在所测试范围内，注意力机制已足够承担核心建模任务，前馈网络并非不可或缺。通过合理重分配计算资源，仅注意力结构即可达到接近标准Transformer的性能水平，尤其在大规模预训练中优势明显。模型性能差距主要源于对权重知识的利用能力，而非注意力机制本身的能力不足。

Abstract: Feed-forward networks hold two thirds of a transformer's non-embedding parameters, yet the architecture has not received a necessity test that controls parameters, compute, and depth at once. We pretrain attention-only decoder transformers (Simple Attention Networks, SANs) against standard transformers matched separately for parameter count, training FLOPs, and depth (2 to 48 layers), for up to 105B tokens at 6M to 87M parameters. Deleting feed-forward layers in place is costly: the standard transformer leads by 0.47 nats at matched depth and 0.26 nats at matched FLOPs. Reallocating the freed budget into attention depth closes the gap: at matched parameters the difference is 0.006 nats (0.27 percent of loss), reproducible to one part in ten thousand across seed pairs, shrinking across 5B, 30B, and 105B budgets, and holding near 0.02 nats across a 29x size range. Three measurements localize the remaining gap to parametric recall: attention-only models are better on context-grounded answers and worse where knowledge must come from weights. Weight spectra show why: routing matrices (Q/K) crystallize early, content matrices accumulate rank slowly, and removing feed-forward layers relocates this accumulation to the attention output projection. QK-normalization, not feed-forward layers or residual gating, keeps 48-layer attention-only stacks trainable. The deficit concentrates on low-context query prediction and localizes there entirely by the largest budget. A pre-registered test confirms the account: it predicts a 0.02 to 0.05 nat gap on knowledge-dense web text; a matched pair trained on fineweb-edu measures 0.040. Within the tested regime, attention does the rest.

This incurs substantial computational overhead when scaling to large-scale dynamic graphs. In this paper, we propose SG-JEPA, a joint spiking embedding predictive architecture for large-scale dynamic graphs. In contrast to existing self-supervised methods, SG-JEPA partitions nodes into context and target sets along the temporal dimension to learn embeddings that are predictive of each other via additional spatial-temporal information. Furthermore, through encoding sequential inputs into coarse-to-fine spike count embeddings, spiking neurons enable SG-JEPA to adapt to the varying computational constraints of downstream tasks. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SG-JEPA achieves competitive or even superior performance over discriminative baselines on node classification, while effectively scaling to the dynamic graph with 13 million edges.
