### [162] [PAC--Bayes Bounds on Quotient Parameter Spaces: Geometry-induced Implicit-Bias Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18422)
*Nicola Aladrah,Fabio Anselmi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出在过参数化模型中，由于存在连续的参数对称性，应将PAC-Bayesian分析应用于商预测空间。通过将先验和后验分布投影到商空间，可消除仅由参数化差异引起的非负KL散度贡献，从而获得更紧的泛化界。作者构造了一个每个预测器的规范参数化，并考虑其等价参数化的几何体积，将中性参考先验转化为反映模型隐式偏见的数据无关先验。该先验逼近理想但不可行的后验匹配先验，当其与学习到的商空间后验的KL散度更小时，所得泛化证书更紧。实验验证了该方法在傅里叶-哈达玛德回归和查询-键注意力中的有效性，显著降低了商空间中的平均KL散度和PAC-Bayes证书。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过参数化模型存在连续参数对称性，导致不同参数对应相同预测器，传统PAC-Bayesian分析因未考虑此对称性而可能产生宽松的泛化界。为改进分析精度，需在商预测空间上进行分析，并引入反映模型几何结构的先验以捕捉隐式偏见。

Method: 1. 将先验与后验分布映射至商预测空间，消除参数化差异带来的冗余KL项；2. 构造每个预测器的规范参数化形式；3. 利用等价参数化的几何体积定义数据无关的隐式偏见先验；4. 通过比较该先验与学习后验之间的KL散度评估泛化界收紧效果。

Result: 在傅里叶-哈达玛德回归实验中，隐式偏见先验使平均商空间KL下降40.69%，平均PAC-Bayes证书下降21.40%；在查询-键注意力实验中，改善较小且依赖于先验尺度，验证了该效应的条件性。

Conclusion: 基于商空间的PAC-Bayesian分析结合几何诱导的隐式偏见先验，能有效提升泛化界紧致性，尤其在具有明确对称结构的模型中表现显著，揭示了模型几何结构对泛化能力的重要影响。

Abstract: Overparameterized models often have continuous parameter symmetries, so different parameters define the same predictor. We show that PAC--Bayesian analysis should be performed on the quotient predictor space: pushing a prior and posterior to the quotient preserves the empirical and population Gibbs risks while removing the nonnegative KL contribution caused solely by how the two distributions differ among parameterizations of the same predictor.
  Quotienting alone does not determine which prior to use. We construct a canonical choice of one parameterization for each predictor and account for the geometric volume of its equivalent parameterizations. This transforms a neutral reference prior into a data-independent prior that reflects the model's implicit bias. It approximates the ideal but inadmissible posterior-matched prior, which would minimize the KL term by depending on the training data. The resulting certificate is tighter exactly when this geometry-induced prior has smaller KL divergence from the learned quotient posterior than the neutral prior.
  We test this prediction in Fourier regression with a Hadamard parameterization and in Query-Key attention, using ordinary SGD without an explicit regularizer. The implicit-bias prior reduces the mean quotient-space KL by \(40.69\%\) and the mean PAC--Bayes certificate by \(21.40\%\) in the Fourier-Hadamard experiment. The smaller, prior-scale-dependent improvement in Query-Key attention confirms the predicted conditional nature of the effect.

</details>


### [163] [Intelligence from Learnable Novelty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18433)
*Yanbo Zhang,Michael Levin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为‘可学习的新奇性’（learnable novelty）的新概念，将不同领域中智能的多种表现（如数据压缩、通用计算、自适应行为）统一到一个可微分的量化框架下。通过一个廉价且可微的储备池计算机构建了该量的闭式估计器，在无监督条件下成功复现了数十年的复杂性分类结果，例如在元胞自动机中正确识别规则110为最复杂的类型；同时作为优化目标，其梯度能引导神经元胞自动机进入具有孤子结构的计算区域，并在无监督情况下组织图像编码器对MNIST数字的表征；作为内在奖励用于强化学习时，显著提升探索能力，在十个环境中优于基线九次且无失败。这表明：复杂性生成、抽象与探索等看似独立的目标，均可由对单一可微量的上升驱动，从而为智能的不同投影提供了统一的定量基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对智能的描述分散于不同领域，如统计中的数据压缩、动力系统中的通用计算、代理中的自适应行为，但这些领域的目标常相互矛盾（如追求新奇与避免意外），根源在于未区分可转化为知识的新奇性和不可处理的新奇性。因此需要一种能统一衡量可学习信息的新指标，以弥合跨领域智能定义的鸿沟。

Method: 提出‘可学习的新奇性’概念，基于储备池计算设计一个闭式、可微的估计器。该估计器无需标签或监督信号，直接从数据中提取可被学习的部分新奇信息。将其应用于元胞自动机复杂性排序、神经元胞自动机演化、图像编码器无监督表征学习以及强化学习中的内在奖励机制。

Result: 该估计器在无监督条件下准确排序元胞自动机复杂性，成功识别出规则110为最高复杂度；作为优化目标，使神经元胞自动机演化出可计算的孤子结构；在无监督条件下完成对MNIST数字类别的表征组织；在强化学习中作为内在奖励，提升探索效率，在十项任务中九项超越基线且无崩溃。

Conclusion: 复杂性生成、抽象和探索等智能核心能力，可统一归结为对一个可微分量——可学习新奇性——的优化。这一发现为智能的多个表现形式提供了共同的定量基础，标志着跨学科智能理论的重要整合。

Abstract: Intelligence appears under different names in different fields: as data compression in statistics and machine learning, as universal computation in dynamical systems, and as adaptive behavior in agents. Each field carries its own objective, and the two most influential drives often fail in mirror image: novelty search, which seeks surprise, is transfixed by a noisy television screen, while the free-energy principle, which avoids surprise, is most content in a dark room. Both failures have a single cause: each objective treats as one quantity the surprise a learner can convert into knowledge and the surprise it never can. Here we show that the learnable part of that information, which we call learnable novelty, yields the seemingly disparate projections of intelligence, and we give a closed-form estimator of it built on a cheap and differentiable reservoir computer. Used as a measure, with no supervision of any kind, the estimator recovers decades of complexity classification, ranking the Turing-complete rule~110 highest among the elementary cellular automata. Used as an objective, its gradient carries a neural cellular automaton from simple dynamics into a regime of solitons, the traveling, colliding structures by which rule~110 computes, as well as organizes the representation of an image encoder around the ten digit classes of MNIST, fully unsupervised: no label ever enters training. Handed to a reinforcement-learning agent as an intrinsic reward, it supplies the exploration that task rewards lack, improving on the task baseline in nine of ten environments and collapsing in none. Complexity generation, abstraction, and exploration, ordinarily pursued with unrelated objectives in separate fields, thus emerge from ascent on one differentiable quantity, and the projections of intelligence gain a common quantitative footing.

</details>


### [164] [CANDOR: Chance-Calibrated Discordance in Frozen Foundation Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18451)
*Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh,Sven Nebelung,Daniel Truhn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CANDOR 是一种新的判别度度量方法，通过等大小的类别银行和标签交换对称性，将随机水平固定在0.5，解决了传统方法中因类别不平衡导致的误判问题。在22个编码器、20个数据集、605,443张图像上，该方法修正了先前结论：几乎所有编码器都未完全失效，但普遍存在特征表示弱的问题，即使表现最好的胸部模型也仅在气胸检测上达到84.5 AUROC，且18.4%的阳性病例比同类病例更接近相反标签样本。不同任务间性能差异显著，表明信息瓶颈并非根本限制，而是头选择所致。此外，特征坍缩与擦除保留相关，但与目标、尺度、新旧或病灶大小无关。由于基准固定，CANDOR可在训练头之前使用，提前识别出编码器对特定发现支持不足的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统判别度评估依赖于最近邻分类，但在类别不均衡情况下，反例邻居因密度更高而更易被选中，导致编码器看似‘失明’，实则为统计偏差。因此需要一种对类别不平衡鲁棒、且随机水平固定的评估方法。

Method: 提出CANDOR，采用等大小的正负样本银行，确保在标签互换下保持对称性，从而将随机猜测的准确率稳定在0.5，避免因类别分布不均造成的误导。

Result: 在大规模实验中，修正后发现所有编码器均未完全崩溃，但普遍表现较弱；最佳模型在气胸检测上仅达84.5 AUROC，且18.4%的阳性病例被错误地靠近相反标签样本。跨任务表现差异大，说明问题在于头部选择而非信息容量。特征坍缩与擦除保留相关，但与任务目标、尺度、时间或大小无关。

Conclusion: CANDOR提供了一个可靠、可前置使用的评估工具，能有效识别编码器对特定医学发现支持不足的情况，揭示了当前视觉模型在实际应用中的局限性主要源于头部选择而非特征表达能力本身。

Abstract: Frozen encoders are chosen by how well a lightweight head reads a finding from their features, not whether the geometry separates it. Nearest-neighbor discordance does, but with unequal banks the opposite-label neighbor wins on density, not geometry, so prevalence alone makes an uninformed encoder look blind. We introduce CANDOR, a discordance measure whose equal-size banks are symmetric under a label swap, fixing its chance level at exactly one half. Across 22 encoders, 20 datasets from 7 domains, and 605,443 images, this correction reverses the conclusion. Collapse falls below chance almost everywhere, so no encoder is blind, yet all are weak: the best chest model reads pneumothorax at 84.5 AUROC and still places 18.4% of those positives nearer an opposite-label film than its own kind in the same hospital. The same encoder that resolves bird species at 4.5 leaves chest findings at 42.8 and glaucoma at 49.8, at chance and worse than random weights. Such a case caps the normalized margin of any Lipschitz head, yet some head among eleven is correct on all but 2.8% of cases where one head misses 35.9%: the deficit is selection, not information. Erasure retention is associated with collapse; we detect no association with the objective, scale, recency, or size of the finding. Because the chance level is fixed, CANDOR can be read before any head is trained, flagging which findings a frozen encoder supports poorly.

</details>


### [165] [Estimating Rare Events in Language Models with Proper Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18454)
*Nikita Y. Parulekar,Anqi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出GA-AMLS方法和SPB损失，用于在语言模型中估计极低概率事件，解决零估计崩溃和系统偏差问题，实验表明该方法在对称评估下表现最佳，而带高估偏见的方法在非对称惩罚下更优，强调应根据部署场景选择估计器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在极端罕见事件估计中存在零估计崩溃、系统偏差及评估损失不稳定等问题，难以应对语言模型在对抗性分布偏移或大规模部署下的罕见故障风险。

Method: 引入梯度激活自适应多级分裂（GA-AMLS），利用基于梯度的MCMC核在连续激活空间中导航，替代传统输入空间搜索；同时提出具有可调不对称性的Shifted-Power Bregman损失（SPB），以稳定评估并匹配安全成本。

Result: 实验显示GA-AMLS在对称评估下达到最低损失，显著降低平均对数空间平方误差；而在非对称惩罚下，具有高估偏见的方法表现更优，验证了不同部署场景下估计器选择的重要性。

Conclusion: 激活空间是语言模型中罕见事件估计的可行域，相比离散输入空间搜索更具鲁棒性；估计算法的选择应与具体应用场景的安全需求相匹配。

Abstract: Quantifying the risk of rare failures in language models, such as those triggered by adversarial distribution shifts or very large-scale deployments, requires estimating probabilities far too small for random sampling. While recent work has formalized Low Probability Estimation, existing pipelines remain fragile in the rarest regimes: estimators can suffer zero-estimate collapse or systematic bias, and standard evaluation losses can become unstable or poorly matched to asymmetric safety costs. In this work, we introduce Gradient Activation Adaptive Multi-Level Splitting (GA-AMLS), which adapts rare-event Monte Carlo methods to the continuous activation space of language models. Specifically, GA-AMLS uses a gradient-based MCMC kernel to navigate activation space, eliminating the zero-estimate collapse of input-space search and replacing the independence assumptions of prior activation-space estimators with conditional sampling under an explicit, heavier-tailed activation prior. We also propose the Shifted-Power Bregman (SPB) Loss, a proper scoring rule that remains finite for zero-estimates and offers tunable asymmetry between underestimation and overestimation penalties. Experiments on small transformer models reveal a bias-variance tradeoff: GA-AMLS achieves the lowest loss under symmetric evaluation, reducing average log-space squared error relative to the strongest baseline across model sizes, while methods with overestimation bias prevail under asymmetric penalties. Our findings highlight that estimator choice should be matched to deployment context. More broadly, our work establishes activation space as a tractable domain for rare-event estimation in language models, circumventing the brittleness of discrete input-space search.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用图神经网络构建跨标注者上下文，融合个体标注者特征与上下文信息生成多视图标注者嵌入，解码为标注者特定的混淆矩阵，并通过包含高置信度标注者的复合目标函数进行训练，以缓解无监督学习中的挑战。

Result: 在10个涵盖NLP、CV、视频和音频的真实数据集上，AHEAD将平均标签准确率从68.75%提升至73.23%，最大提升达14.9%；大规模数据集上的可扩展性实验也验证了其优越性。

Abstract: Crowdsourced labeling provides valuable labeled data for domains across natural language processing, computer vision, and video. Label aggregation aims to infer latent true labels from noisy and biased annotations, with the key lying in annotator reliability estimation. Despite promising progress, existing approaches struggle with one real-world bottleneck: most individual annotators label only a small subset of tasks, making accurate annotator estimation highly intractable. In this paper, we focus on the considerably more challenging multi-class label aggregation and propose AHEAD (cross-Annotator learning and High-confidEnce Annotator-guideD label aggregation), a cross-annotator learning framework that advances annotator reliability estimation by leveraging the population-level data. Specifically, AHEAD first learns high-dimensional cross-annotator contexts via a graph neural network, deriving multi-view, complementary annotator embeddings by aggregating individual-level annotator features with contextual information. These embeddings are then decoded into interpretable annotator-specific confusion matrices to fit the observed labels. We formulate a composite objective incorporating high-confidence annotators to alleviate the unsupervised training issues faced by prior models. Experiments on 10 real-world datasets spanning NLP, CV, Video, and Audio show that AHEAD substantially improves label accuracy, increasing average accuracy from 68.75% to 73.23%, with gains of up to 14.9% in the best case. Meanwhile, scalability experiments on the largest dataset further demonstrate the overall superiority of our method.

### [167] [Weak-to-Strong Learning in Decision Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18467)
*Jingwei Ji,Renyuan Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种决策感知的弱到强（W2S）框架，利用有限标注数据和大量未标注数据来提升上下文随机优化的决策性能。通过弱模型生成未标注数据的预测分布作为软标签，指导强模型训练，并理论分析了其在减少决策风险方面的优势。关键因素是弱模型与强模型特征表示之间的相关维数，该维度越小，未标注数据对降低教师错误的影响越显著。实验验证了理论结果的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多运营决策依赖于基于可观测上下文预测不确定结果的模型，但存在标签数据稀缺、成本高，而上下文协变量丰富的数据不对称问题。为解决这一问题，提出一种新的框架以充分利用未标注数据。

Method: 首先使用少量标注数据训练一个弱模型；然后用该弱模型为未标注上下文生成预测结果分布，作为软监督信号训练更强的模型；结合非渐近上界和下界分析，推导出在何种条件下W2S优于仅使用强模型的基准方法。

Result: 理论证明了当弱-强特征表示的相关维数较小时，使用大量未标注数据可有效缓解弱模型误差的影响，从而降低下游决策风险；合成的新手供应商实验和基于真实数据的评论审核实验均支持该理论结论。

Conclusion: W2S框架在数据不对称场景下能有效提升决策性能，尤其当弱模型与强模型之间特征相关性高时效果更佳，为弱监督学习在实际决策任务中的应用提供了理论依据和实践路径。

Abstract: Many operational decisions rely on predictive models that estimate uncertain outcomes conditional on observable contexts. Training such models, however, often faces a fundamental data asymmetry: labeled outcomes are scarce or costly to obtain, while contextual covariates are abundant. Motivated by this data asymmetry, we develop a decision-aware weak-to-strong (W2S) framework that leverages both labeled and unlabeled data to improve contextual stochastic optimization. Specifically, we first train a weak model using limited labeled data and then use it to generate predicted outcome distributions on unlabeled contexts. These distributions provide soft supervision for training a strong model. We establish a non-asymptotic upper bound on the excess decision risk of W2S and a complementary lower bound for a strong-only benchmark. Their comparison yields explicit sufficient conditions under which W2S improves downstream decision performance. The key quantity is the correlation dimension between the weak and strong feature representations: when it is small, abundant unlabeled data reduce the effect of teacher errors along non-overlapping directions. A synthetic newsvendor experiment and a comment moderation experiment based on real-world data provide empirical evidence consistent with the theory.

### [168] [RRPO: Reference-Relative Policy Optimization with Stratified Conditional Rollouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18470)
*Yuxin Xiong,Xunyi Jiang,Rohan Surana,Xintong Li,Sheldon Yu,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Ryan A. Rossi,Jingbo Shang,Tong Yu,Julian McAuley,Junda Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RRPO通过参考相对对比比较扩展了GRPO，利用分层条件回溯构建正负锚点集，并通过集合对比目标训练度量投影头，实现无需任务真值验证器的对比优势定义，在多个任务场景中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非可验证任务中，单一正确性标准无法充分描述成功，因此需要更通用的优化方法替代基于正确性的优势构造。

Method: 提出参考相对策略优化（RRPO），使用分层条件回溯构建正负锚点集，训练度量投影头进行集合对比学习，冻结投影头后以对齐得分作为对比优势进行组内相对优化。

Result: RRPO在可验证推理、开放式生成和后SFT设置中均表现良好，优于弱监督基线，并在监督微调后提供额外增益。

Conclusion: RRPO有效扩展了组相对优化至非可验证场景，无需依赖真值验证器，具有广泛适用性和性能优势。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has shown strong effectiveness in reinforcement learning from verifiable feedback, where sampled rollouts can be compared within a group using task-provided correctness signals. However, extending group-relative optimization beyond verifiable settings is challenging because success in many tasks is not captured by a single correctness criterion. We propose \textbf{Reference-Relative Policy Optimization (RRPO)}, which generalizes GRPO by replacing direct correctness-based advantage construction with reference-relative contrastive comparisons. RRPO first uses \emph{stratified conditional rollouts} to construct positive and negative anchor sets, and then trains a metric projection head with a set-contrastive objective to compare candidate rollouts against these anchors. The resulting alignment scores directly define contrastive advantages: during policy optimization, the projection head is frozen, and the scores are centered within each rollout group in a standard group-relative objective. We evaluate RRPO using anchor-based contrastive advantages throughout policy optimization, without relying on task ground-truth verifiers. Across verifiable reasoning, open-ended generation, and post-SFT settings, RRPO remains competitive with verifier-based optimization, improves over weakly supervised baselines, and provides additional gains after supervised fine-tuning.

### [169] [Hybrid Latent-Structural Fusion (HLSF) for Cyber Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18479)
*Dorianis M. Perez,Maksim E. Eren,Bryan E. Kaiser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为混合潜在结构融合（HLSF）的加权异常融合框架，结合了CP-APR的结构异常得分与基于归一化流的潜在空间密度得分，在真实世界的企业网络数据上显著提升了异常检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在网络安全中，恶意异常活动检测面临复杂行为模式识别的挑战，现有方法如CP-APR和归一化流虽有效，但单独使用时存在局限性，需要更高效的融合机制以提升检测能力。

Method: 提出HLSF框架，通过加权融合CP-APR生成的结构异常得分与归一化流生成的潜在空间密度得分，实现多维度行为特征的联合建模与异常检测。

Conclusion: HLSF框架有效整合了统计建模与深度生成模型的优势，显著提升了对复杂恶意行为的检测能力，为网络安全中的异常检测提供了新范式。

Abstract: Malicious anomalous activity detection is a fundamental challenge for cyber security systems. In this study, we propose Hybrid Latent-Structural Fusion (HLSF), a weighted anomaly fusion framework integrating CP-APR structural anomaly scores with latent-space density scores derived from normalizing flows. In our experiments, we show that the HLSF framework improves anomaly detection performance on a dataset of real-world compromised user credentials collected from the large enterprise network of Los Alamos National Laboratory (LANL) during a red-teaming exercise, compared with using CP-APR or normalizing flows alone.

### [170] [Attractor Geometry Determines the Identifiability Limits of System Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18490)
*Matteo Gallo,Fabio Anselmi,Paolo Lazzari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了从数据中发现控制方程的极限受吸引子几何结构制约，提出一个关键指标 $\lambda_{\min}(M)$（不变测度矩矩阵的最小特征值）作为可识别性的上限。该指标基于Birkhoff遍历定理，仅需短参考轨迹即可计算，反映吸引子对函数空间的覆盖程度：当其为零时，任何算法都无法恢复方程；随其增大，稀疏回归（SINDy）与进化符号回归（PySR）性能提升。混沌虽通过扩展吸引子提高 $\lambda_{\min}(M)$，但同时放大噪声，而由于噪声对SINDy线性影响、对PySR超线性影响，二者表现可能相反，因此更深混沌并非总有益。该框架提出的无参数机制评分可跨系统迁移至Lorenz-96，验证其机制性而非拟合；方程推导出的判据可预测增加混沌是否改善条件。研究还引入Soft F1，一种系数加权的结构度量，能捕捉二元成功或预测指标无法察觉的性能差异。因此，发现的第一步不是选算法，而是判断吸引子允许什么。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有符号发现方法受限于算法设计和数据量，但更深层限制来自吸引子的几何结构——长期动力学决定哪些方程可被恢复。当前方法在不同动力学状态（如固定点、周期、混沌）下表现不一，缺乏统一的理论判据来解释为何某些状态难以恢复。研究旨在揭示吸引子几何如何决定可识别性，并建立普适的评估框架，以指导算法选择与系统设计。

Method: 基于Lorenz-84系统的内系统设计，改变单一强迫参数以生成固定点、极限环和混沌三种动力学状态，保持方程与基函数库不变。利用短参考轨迹计算不变测度矩矩阵 $M$，提取其最小特征值 $\lambda_{\min}(M)$ 作为核心指标。通过SINDy和PySR在不同状态下的符号回归实验，分析该指标与算法性能的关系。进一步将所得机制评分应用于独立的Lorenz-96系统，验证其泛化能力。引入Soft F1作为新型结构性能度量，以捕捉系数层面的差异。

Result: 1. $\lambda_{\min}(M)$ 成功刻画了方程可识别性的理论上限：其值越小，恢复越困难，甚至完全不可能；其值越大，算法性能越好。2. 混沌虽提升 $\lambda_{\min}(M)$，但伴随噪声放大，导致SINDy与PySR表现方向相反。3. 无参数机制评分可跨系统迁移至Lorenz-96，表明其反映的是真实机制而非过拟合。4. 由方程导出的判据能准确预测何时增加混沌不会改善识别条件。5. Soft F1有效揭示了传统指标忽略的性能差异。

Conclusion: 符号发现的首要问题是吸引子是否允许恢复方程，而非算法选择。$\lambda_{\min}(M)$ 提供了一个无需训练、快速计算的理论判据，用于评估系统可识别性。研究强调应优先优化系统动力学设计以改善吸引子覆盖，再匹配算法。未来工作应探索该框架在复杂系统中的应用，并发展更鲁棒的噪声处理机制。

Abstract: Symbolic discovery of governing equations from data is limited not only by algorithm design and data volume, but by the geometry of the attractor: what the long-run dynamics allow to be recovered. Using a within-system design on Lorenz-84, where one forcing parameter drives fixed-point, limit-cycle, and chaotic regimes while the governing equations and library stay fixed, we show that a single number, $λ_{\min}(M)$, the smallest eigenvalue of the invariant-measure moment matrix, sets the identifiability ceiling for both sparse regression (SINDy) and evolutionary symbolic regression (PySR). Derived from the Birkhoff ergodic theorem and obtained from a short reference trajectory before any run, $λ_{\min}(M)$ measures how fully the attractor covers function space: where it vanishes, recovery is impossible for any algorithm, sparse or combinatorial alike; as it grows, both algorithms improve. Chaos raises $λ_{\min}(M)$ by spreading the attractor, but also enlarges it and amplifies noise; because noise enters SINDy's regression bottleneck linearly and PySR's discrimination channel superlinearly, the same transition can push the two methods in opposite directions, so deeper chaos is not uniformly better. Parameter-free mechanistic scores from this framework transfer without refitting to a held-out Lorenz-96 system, confirming mechanism rather than curve-fitting; a criterion read from the equations predicts when added chaos will not improve conditioning. We also introduce Soft F1, a coefficient-weighted structural metric that resolves performance differences invisible to binary-success and predictive scores. The first question of discovery is then not which algorithm, but what the attractor permits.

</details>


### [171] [Now We Know? A Systematic Comparison of TerraMind and THOR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18504)
*Frederick Schindlegger,Kenzo Bounegta,Eva Gmelich Meijling,Johannes Jakubik,Arnt-Børre Salberg,Theodor Forgaard,Nicolas Longepe,Valerio Marsocci*

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比两个由欧洲空间局Φ-lab开发的地理空间基础模型（THOR和TerraMind），揭示了现有基准排名中被掩盖的关键差异。研究发现，架构设计（如补丁大小和解码器类型）比模型身份本身更能解释性能差异，并提出两种互补的策略：TerraMind侧重预训练阶段的尺度建模，而THOR则在推理阶段实现灵活的标记化。研究强调需结合数据集特征解读结果，提供了一套可推广至未来地理空间基础模型的诊断性消融方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前地理空间基础模型（GFMs）的基准排名仅依赖综合得分，无法揭示模型间差异的根本原因，例如架构、解码器容量或特定使用场景的影响。因此，亟需一种系统性方法来解析这些因素对性能的实际贡献。

Method: 采用受控比较方法，在十个不同应用场景下评估两种具有截然不同设计理念的GFMs（THOR与TerraMind），分别考察补丁大小、解码器复杂度、微调策略、输入模态和模型规模等维度的表现差异，并进行多维度消融分析。

Result: 架构设计（尤其是补丁大小和解码器类型）是影响性能的主要因素，超过模型本身差异；THOR和TerraMind代表了不同的优化路径（预训练时尺度建模 vs 推理时标记化灵活性）；正确理解结果需结合数据集特性；研究提出了通用的诊断性分析框架。

Conclusion: 地理空间基础模型的性能差异并非由单一模型优劣决定，而是多种设计选择共同作用的结果。本研究提供的分析框架可为未来模型开发与评估提供指导，推动更透明、可解释的模型比较。

Abstract: Benchmarks for Geospatial Foundation Models (GFMs) increasingly rank models by aggregate score, but such rankings obscure why models differ: how much of the gap is architecture, how much is decoder capacity, and how much is a use-case-specific artefact? This study addresses that gap through a controlled comparison of two GFMs developed under European Space Agency's $Φ$-lab with contrasting design philosophies: THOR, which introduces a compute-adaptive architecture supporting variable patch sizes and unifies Sentinel-1, -2, and -3 data at their native resolutions; and TerraMind, a multimodal generative GFM pretrained with a dual-scale token/pixel objective that enables any-to-any cross-modal generation (Thinking-in-Modalities) to infer missing sensors at inference time. Rather than reporting a single leaderboard, we investigate the axes along which the two architectures actually differ - patch size, decoder complexity, finetuning regime, input modality, and model scale - across ten use cases spanning segmentation and regression in diverse domains, including climate disaster response, methane leak detection, snow monitoring, or sea ice mapping. We find that architectural design choices - patch size and decoder type in particular - explain more performance variance than model identity itself, that the two models embody complementary investment strategies (pretraining-time scale for TerraMind versus inference-time tokenisation for THOR), and that correctly interpreting results requires dataset-level characterisation. The resulting picture is not a single winner but a set of hypotheses and a diagnostic ablation methodology that we expect to generalise to future GFMs beyond THOR and TerraMind.

### [173] [Signed Rectified Flow: Negativity-Controlled Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18516)
*Runlong Liao,Baiyu Su,Lizhang Chen,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Signed Rectified Flow (Signed RF) extends Rectified Flow to model signed measures, enabling generative modeling with both positive (promote) and negative (suppress) components. It creates exclusion barriers via negative mass, improving fidelity-diversity trade-offs, reducing memorization, and mitigating unwanted content in diffusion models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To incorporate negative information and exclusion constraints into generative models, allowing better control over generated outputs by suppressing undesirable regions or patterns.

Method: Signed RF generalizes the rectified flow framework to handle signed measures $\pi^{sign} = (1+\alpha)\pi^+ - \alpha\pi^-$, using a charged-particle interpretation to model exclusion barriers through negative mass in the underlying continuity equation.

Result: Experiments show improved image quality and diversity on ImageNet, reduced nearest-neighbor similarity in anti-memorization tasks, and less nudity from adversarial prompts in Stable Diffusion 3.5, while maintaining high CLIP and aesthetic scores.

Conclusion: Signed RF provides a principled, theoretically grounded method for incorporating suppression and exclusion in generative modeling, enabling more controllable and reliable generation without sacrificing quality.

Abstract: We introduce Signed Rectified Flow (Signed RF), a generalization of Rectified Flow that targets the signed measure $π^{sign} = (1+α)π^+ - απ^-$, where $α>0$, $π^+$ is the distribution to promote, and $π^-$ is the distribution to suppress. Although direct sampling from a signed measure is not well-defined, Signed RF induces a valid generative process that concentrates probability in regions where the signed measure is positive while provably excluding regions dominated by its negative component. It therefore provides a principled framework for incorporating negative information and exclusion constraints into generative modeling. We analyze the signed continuity equation underlying Signed RF and use a charged-particle interpretation to explain how negative mass forms exclusion barriers. This theory further motivates practical adaptive guidance algorithms. Across several applications, Signed RF improves the fidelity-diversity trade-off on ImageNet, reduces nearest-neighbor similarity in anti-memorization experiments, and reduces nudity induced by adversarial prompts in Stable Diffusion 3.5 while preserving CLIP and aesthetic scores.

Across linear and non-linear models, the proposed two-stage architecture achieves the best precision-recall trade-off, attaining the highest recall, F1-score, and AUC at acceptable false positive rates. ### [176] [Operational Proto-Introspection in Looped Language Models: Process-Quality Taps, Executable Branching, and the Readout-Control Boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18553)
*Jan Kirin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨语言模型是否能读取计算过程的质量，以及外部干预能否将这种读出转化为更好结果。在冻结的2.6B参数循环Transformer模型Ouro-RLTT上，通过预答案探测发现，即使不包含答案区域和真实值，隐藏状态结合长度与概率捷径仍可预测最终成功（AUROC 0.797），优于仅使用捷径的0.731（增量+0.066）。低容量探测还能读取任务特异性属性，如分支存活率达0.9697，内容排序准确率0.6310，生成分支正确性达AUROC 0.7755。非循环对照组也表现出候选质量读出能力，表明递归并非必需。研究构建了分支/延续/剪枝机制，利用192槽循环缓存实现分支专属缓存谱系与比特精确残差捕获拼接，仅重算受影响后缀，节省高达88%的每分支层计算。然而，所有冻结干预均未产生验证的能力提升；定向引导为已知负面效应；四任务匹配采样比较排除了冻结分叉收益证据，但无法估计普遍缺陷；终端选择问题仍未解决且统计功效不足；有限LoRA调整改变行为但未提升整体可达性。双重空模型审计也不支持最简单的跨度错位解释。研究提出“操作性前内省”概念：模型虽可被读取，但当前干预无法将其转化为有效能力。预答案结果局限于单一领域。关键评估采用源项不相交划分与反对称化评估设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言模型在计算过程中是否具备自我感知能力，即能否读取自身内部状态以判断计算质量，并检验外部干预是否能将这种读出转化为实际性能提升。旨在揭示模型内在可读性与可操控性之间的差距，推动对模型内部机制的理解。

Method: 采用冻结的2.6B参数循环Transformer模型Ouro-RLTT，在GSM8K数据集上进行预答案探测，分析隐藏状态、长度和概率捷径对最终成功的预测能力；构建基于192槽循环缓存的分支/延续/剪枝机制，实现分支专属缓存谱系追踪与比特精确残差拼接，减少计算开销；设计多种干预策略（如方向性引导、有限LoRA、终端选择等）并评估其有效性；使用匹配采样、双空模型审计与源项不相交评估验证结果稳健性。

Result: 预答案探测显示，隐藏状态加长度与概率捷径可实现AUROC 0.797的预测能力，显著优于仅用捷径的0.731；低容量探测能有效读取任务特异性属性，如分支存活率、内容排序与生成正确性；非循环控制组亦具候选质量读出能力，说明递归非必要；尽管构建了高效分支机制并节省高达88%计算，但所有冻结干预均未带来验证性能力提升；定向引导为负效应，匹配采样排除冻结分叉增益，终端选择与有限LoRA未改善净可达性；双重空模型审计不支持跨度错位解释。

Conclusion: 模型具备‘操作性前内省’能力——其内部状态可被外部读取以预测计算质量，但当前干预手段尚无法将这些读出转化为有效性能提升。这揭示了可读性与可操控性间的根本断层，提示未来需发展更精细的干预机制以激活模型潜在能力。

Abstract: Can a language model read the quality of ongoing computation, and can an external intervention turn that readout into better outcomes? We test both questions in a frozen 2.6B looped transformer, Ouro-RLTT. On GSM8K, a strict pre-answer probe excludes the answer region and gold value yet predicts eventual success: hidden states plus length and log-probability shortcuts reach AUROC 0.797, versus 0.731 for the shortcuts alone (incremental +0.066; task-clustered 95% CI [+0.021, +0.112]; 170 tasks, 680 candidates). Low-capacity taps also read role-specialized properties: task-disjoint branch survival reaches 0.9697 oracle retention, content ranking reaches 0.6310 macro top-1, and generated-branch correctness reaches AUROC 0.7755. A non-looped control replicates a candidate-quality readout, so recurrence is not required for every signal.
  We build branch/carry/prune machinery over Ouro's 192-slot recurrent cache, including branch-specific cache lineage and a bit-exact residual-capture splice that recomputes only the affected suffix and saves up to 88% of per-branch layer passes. No frozen intervention produces a validated capability gain. Directional steering is an established negative; a four-task matched-sampling comparison removes evidence for a frozen-fork gain but cannot estimate a general deficit; terminal selection remains unresolved and underpowered; and bounded LoRA changes surface behavior without improving net reachability. A two-null audit does not support the simplest span-misalignment explanation.
  We call this readable-but-not-yet-usable property operational proto-introspection. The model is not consulting our probes: we read its hidden trajectories, and our interventions fail to convert those readouts into validated capability. The pre-answer result is limited to one domain. Load-bearing values use source-item-disjoint splits and antisymmetrized evaluation where applicable.

</details>


### [177] [Robust Multi-View Classification under Noisy Supervision via Global Anchor Consensus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18561)
*Yuliang Yang,Hongzhe Zhang,Huiru Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种名为GALA的多视图分类方法，通过构建全局锚点来抵抗噪声标签的影响。该方法在每个视图中为每类构造全局锚点，利用其对全类样本的聚合特性提供稳定参考；通过比较样本到自身标签锚点与最近竞争锚点的距离，结合分类器置信度生成跨视图审计得分，进而对可疑样本赋小权重，并仅在候选标签与分类器预测一致时进行自适应修正。修正后的标签反向优化锚点并指导鲁棒表示学习。在六个数据集上的实验表明，GALA在高噪声率下显著优于八种先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大多数多视图分类方法依赖于精确标注以保证性能，但在实际应用中噪声标签普遍存在，且基于此类不准确监督训练的模型会逐渐失去可靠性的精炼信号。因此需要一种能够抵抗噪声标签影响的新方法。

Method: 构建每个视图中每类的全局锚点，作为全类样本的聚合代表；计算样本到其观测标签锚点与最近竞争锚点的距离比，结合分类器置信度生成跨视图审计得分；根据审计得分对可疑样本赋予较小权重，并采用自适应修正策略仅当候选标签与分类器预测一致时才更新标签；修正后的标签用于反向优化锚点，促进噪声鲁棒表示学习。

Result: 在六个数据集上，GALA均优于八种现有最先进方法，尤其在高噪声率条件下表现突出，验证了其对噪声标签的强大鲁棒性。

Conclusion: GALA通过全局锚点机制和自适应标签修正策略，有效缓解了多视图分类中噪声标签带来的负面影响，实现了更稳健的表示学习，是一种高效且鲁棒的多视图分类方法。

Abstract: In recent years, multi-view learning has attracted increasing attention, as it integrates the complementary information of heterogeneous views. Most existing multi-view classification methods rely on accurate annotations to guarantee performance. However, noisy labels are ubiquitous in practice due to imperfect annotation, and the refinement signals that existing methods derive from models trained on such noisy supervision can gradually lose their reliability. To deal with this problem, we propose a novel Global Anchor-based Label Auditing method (GALA) for multi-view classification to resist the negative impact of noisy labels. Specifically, we construct a global anchor for each class in every view, which aggregates the samples of the whole class and thus offers a stable reference insensitive to individual predictions. Then, each view measures how close an instance is to the anchor of its observed label relative to the nearest competing anchor, and the per-view evaluations are fused with the classifier confidence into a cross-view audit score. Based on the audit scores, suspicious samples are assigned small weights, and an adaptive correction strategy rewrites a label only when the anchor-based candidate agrees with the classifier prediction. Finally, the corrected labels in turn refine the anchors and supervise noise-robust representation learning. Extensive experiments on six datasets demonstrate that GALA outperforms eight state-of-the-art methods, especially under high noise rates.

</details>


### [178] [AMICA-Python: Adaptive Mixture Independent Component Analysis with Anderson Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18568)
*Scott Huberty,Christian O'Reilly*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AMICA-Python is a Python implementation of the AMICA algorithm with a scikit-learn-conformant API, enabling integration into scientific Python pipelines. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original AMICA algorithm was only available via a Fortran implementation in EEGLAB/MATLAB, limiting accessibility for users outside the MATLAB ecosystem. This hinders integration into modern, non-MATLAB scientific workflows.

Method: AMICA-Python replicates the reference algorithm closely while adopting modern software engineering practices and a user-friendly Python interface. It includes an optional Anderson acceleration to speed up convergence.

Result: AMICA-Python achieves nearly identical numerical results to the Fortran version (median normalized log-likelihood: 11.572), with a negligible relative difference of $1.07\times10^{-8}$. It is 17.7% faster than the reference, and 34.1% faster with Anderson acceleration.

Conclusion: AMICA-Python provides high-precision reproduction of the original AMICA algorithm with competitive performance and enhanced accessibility through a modern Python interface, enabling broader use in diverse analytical pipelines.

Abstract: Adaptive Mixture Independent Component Analysis (AMICA) is widely used in EEG research and has long been associated with strong empirical performance for blind source separation. Despite its impact, practical use has historically depended on a single Fortran implementation, accessed via the EEGLAB toolbox for MATLAB, limiting its accessibility for analytical pipelines not designed within the MATLAB ecosystem. Here we present AMICA-Python, a Python implementation of the AMICA algorithm, with a scikit-learn-conformant API designed for integration with existing scientific Python pipelines. The implementation follows the reference algorithm closely while adopting modern software engineering practices and an interface familiar to Python users. Additionally, we introduce an optional Anderson acceleration scheme that can dramatically reduce the time to convergence for this relatively slow algorithm. To evaluate numerical agreement and practical performance, we benchmarked AMICA-Python against the reference Fortran implementation on 14 open EEG recordings. After averaging 3 runs of each implementation on all 14 recordings, AMICA-Python closely matched the reference, with a median final normalized log-likelihoods of 11.572 for both the Fortran and Python implementations, and a negligible median relative absolute difference of only $1.07\times10^{-8}$ when normalized by the absolute Fortran value. Runtime was also competitive. Relative to the reference implementation, AMICA-Python was 17.7\% faster, while the Anderson-accelerated variant was 34.1\% faster. AMICA-Python reproduces the reference implementation to high numerical precision with competitive runtime, while making AMICA available through a more accessible and extensible Python interface.

### [179] [Conditioned Direct Feedback Alignment via Activity and Error Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18574)
*Houman Safaai,Varun Reddy,Bernardo L. Sabatini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了直接反馈对齐（DFA）训练中的一种独特失败模式，即由于局部权重更新通过外积计算，导致前突触活动或局部误差方向的各向异性引入问题。通过受控合成实验，发现当高方差方向包含任务无关干扰时，活动条件化可带来约40个百分点的性能提升；而误差条件化则能额外提升1.77–7.53个百分点，结合两者可再增0.40–0.90个百分点。研究提出归一化DFA（nDFA）家族，包括活动、误差和K-nDFA三种形式，基于谱分析与范数匹配推导出其理论基础。结果显示，误差因子在欠阻尼时脆弱，批量归一化是有效的活动侧替代方案，但卷积网络的增益仍不完全。因此，本研究聚焦于局部外积规则失效的因子层面机制，而非将DFA作为反向传播的通用替代或解决所有层卷积信用分配问题的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索直接反馈对齐（DFA）训练中的失败机制，特别是由外积更新带来的各向异性问题，旨在理解并改进局部学习规则的稳定性与有效性。

Method: 通过控制合成环境分析活动与误差方向的各向异性影响；设计并验证归一化DFA（nDFA）变体，包括活动预条件、误差预条件及双侧联合调节；采用线性后对齐分析、谱特性与范数匹配进行理论解释；在多种数据集（MNIST、Fashion-MNIST）与模型结构（ReLU/softmax, tanh/one-vs-rest）上进行多轮复现测试。

Result: 活动条件化显著提升性能（+40个百分点），误差条件化带来1.77–7.53个百分点增益，两者结合进一步提升0.40–0.90个百分点；提出的nDFA框架有效缓解外积更新缺陷，其中误差因子在欠阻尼下表现不稳定，批量归一化为有效替代；卷积网络中性能提升部分保留，表明当前方法仍非通用解决方案。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了局部外积规则在DFA中因各向异性导致的失败机制，强调应从因子层面理解学习规则局限性，而非将其视为反向传播的全面替代。归一化策略虽有效，但尚不能完全解决深层卷积网络中的信用分配挑战。

Abstract: Direct feedback alignment (DFA) trains hidden layers with fixed random projections of the output error, avoiding the transposed-weight backward pass of backpropagation (BP). We study a failure mode of DFA training that is distinct from feedback quality: the local weight update is calculated by an outer product, so anisotropy can enter through either its presynaptic-activity factor or its local-error factor. Our analyses with controlled synthetic regimes isolate the first failure mode and show an approximately 40-percentage-point activity-conditioning gain when high-variance directions contain task-irrelevant nuisance. Three clean confirmations isolate a different regime: error conditioning improves raw DFA by 1.77--7.53 percentage points, and combining independently selected activity and error factors adds 0.40--0.90 points over activity conditioning. The signs hold for tanh/one-vs-rest MNIST and preregistered Fashion-MNIST, and replicate on eight fresh seeds in a ReLU/softmax MNIST model. This factorization yields a symmetric block-local family of normalized DFA (nDFA): activity nDFA right-preconditions by an inverse activity second moment, error nDFA left-preconditions by an inverse local-error second moment, and K-nDFA applies both factors with separately tuned damping. A linearized post-alignment calculation gives an exact input-side spectral identity and a Kronecker-factor motivation for the two-sided rule, whereas norm matching rules out a scalar step-size explanation. The error factor is fragile when under-damped, BatchNorm is a strong activity-side alternative, and convnet gains remain partial. We therefore frame conditioned DFA as a factor-level study of when local outer-product rules fail, not as a general replacement for BP or a solution to all-layer convolutional credit assignment.

### [180] [On the Diverse Dynamical Behaviors Arising in Deep Linear Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18584)
*Sixu Li,Thomas Jacob Maranzatto,Jan Peszek,Trevor Teolis,Semih Akkoc,Konstantin Riedl,Sennur Ulukus,Nicolás García Trillos*

TL;DR: 本文从粒子系统角度研究了深度线性编码器仅变压器在推理时的行为，将标记视为通过连续线性自注意力层动态交互的粒子。在嵌入维度为二的情况下，动态可重新表述为具有纯二次谐波耦合的广义 Kuramoto 模型，并可通过 Watanabe--Strogatz 理论揭示其内在低维性。对于与 Ott--Antonsen (OA) 流形相关的标记初始化类，参数矩阵诱导出线性变压器中多样的长期行为，包括聚类、振荡和分岔。振荡和分岔通过揭示动态中的隐藏哈密顿结构得以表征。通过建立结构稳定性结果，进一步表明靠近 OA 流形的初始化表现出与精确位于流形上的初始化相同的长期行为。基于二维理论，我们在高维变压器中进行了数值实验，结果表明理论所描述的长期行为在更高维度中依然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解深度线性编码器仅变压器在推理阶段的动态行为，特别是其长期演化特性，探索其背后的数学机制和潜在规律。

Method: 将令牌建模为相互作用的粒子，利用广义 Kuramoto 模型和 Watanabe--Strogatz 理论分析二维嵌入空间下的动态行为；结合 Ott--Antonsen 流形和哈密顿结构分析长期行为；通过结构稳定性证明推广至近似初始条件；并在高维情形进行数值实验验证理论结果的普适性。

Result: 在二维情况下，动态具有内在低维性；参数矩阵可引发聚类、振荡和分岔等复杂长期行为；这些行为在高维情形中仍被观测到，且靠近 OA 流形的初始化表现出相似动力学。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了线性变压器在推理阶段的深层动态结构，表明其长期行为由低维流形主导，并受隐藏哈密顿结构控制。理论分析与数值实验共同支持其在高维情形的可推广性，为理解变压器模型行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the inference-time behavior of deep linear encoder-only transformers through the lens of interacting particle systems. In this perspective, tokens are modeled as particles that interact dynamically through successive linear self-attention layers. We show that in embedding dimension two, for any key, query, and value matrices, the dynamics can be reformulated as a generalized Kuramoto-type model with pure second-harmonic coupling. This formulation is amenable to Watanabe--Strogatz theory which reveals the dynamics are intrinsically low-dimensional regardless of the parameter matrices. For a class of token initializations associated with the Ott--Antonsen (OA) manifold, we show that the parameter matrices induce a diverse variety of long-time behaviors in linear transformers, including clustering, oscillations, and bifurcations. The oscillations and bifurcations are characterized by uncovering a hidden Hamiltonian structure in the dynamics. By establishing a structural stability result, we further show that dynamics initialized near the OA manifold exhibit the same long-time behavior as those initialized exactly on the manifold. Motivated by our theory in dimension two, we conduct numerical experiments for analogous parameter regimes in higher-dimensional transformers. Our numerical experiments suggest that the long-time behaviors characterized in our theoretical results persist in higher dimensions.

### [181] [Planning as Emergent Behavior in Reinforcement Learning with Relational Hidden States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18589)
*Armin Sommer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在纯奖励最大化目标下，模型无关强化学习中为何会出现规划行为。研究发现，神经网络的隐状态结构是决定性因素：具有关系型隐状态并沿学习到的关系交换信息的网络能够恢复环境转移结构，并在决策时通过学习到的图进行规划。相比之下，需要额外发现哪些单元代表哪些状态的对照组则无法形成此类绑定，也无规划行为。研究认为这解释了模型无关强化学习中涌现规划现象，并推测该机制可能也适用于人类大脑中的规划产生过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究模型无关强化学习中规划行为如何从纯粹的奖励最大化目标中涌现，此前这一现象的内在机制尚不明确。

Method: 设计了一种具有关系型隐状态的神经网络架构，其中每个隐状态锚定于环境状态并通过学习的关系进行消息传递；同时设置对照实验，要求代理额外识别状态对应的单元。通过比较两者的性能和内部表征，分析其是否具备规划能力。

Result: 具有关系型隐状态的网络成功恢复了环境的转移结构，并在决策时表现出规划行为；而对照组因缺乏状态-单元绑定，未能形成有效规划机制。

Conclusion: 隐状态的结构设计是模型无关强化学习中涌现规划的关键因素。该机制或可解释人类大脑中通过神经架构先验实现规划的原理，提示此类规划可能比预期更普遍。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning is conventionally divided into model-based and model-free methods. In this taxonomy, model-based methods perform lookahead planning over a learned world model, whereas model-free methods learn a reactive state-action mapping. Recent work, however, has shown that planning can emerge from model-free reinforcement learning alone. The conditions under which this behavior emerges from a pure reward-maximization objective have so far remained unclear. In this paper, we present evidence that, in the observed cases, the hidden-state structure of the neural architecture is the deciding factor. We find that a network of relational hidden states, each anchored to an environment state and exchanging messages along learned relations, acquires a planning mechanism. These hidden states recover the environment's transition structure in their learned relations, and improve the policy at decision time by planning over the learned graph. In a matched control agent that must additionally discover which cells represent which states, no such binding arises, and no planning follows from it. We argue that this explains the observed phenomenon of emergent planning in model-free reinforcement learning and raises the question of how common such emergent planning might be more generally. Finally, we hypothesize that the discovered mechanism could describe how planning emerges from pure reward maximization in the human brain through a neural architectural prior.

Abstract: Counterfactual credit assignment has proven effective in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) for discrete action spaces, yet its extension to continuous-action cooperative tasks remains challenging. Existing methods that approximate the counterfactual baseline via Monte Carlo sampling often introduce bias into policy gradients and fail to guarantee convergence to local optima, as the sampled actions may not have been sufficiently trained. To address these limitations, we propose SAFE, a novel MARL framework that employs a counterfactual baseline conditioned on a self-evolving default action sampled from each agent's experience buffer. This design naturally extends to continuous action spaces without relying on additional simulations, reward models, or environment-specific prior knowledge. The baseline accurately quantifies each agent's contribution, and introduces no bias into the deterministic policy gradient, ensuring convergence to local optima. ### [183] [Mark, Don't Erase: Token Inoculation for Dual-Use Knowledge in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18639)
*Seunghyun Lee,Dongyoon Han,Sangdoo Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种名为Token Inoculation的新方法，通过在预训练阶段用特殊标记绑定有害内容，并在微调阶段利用该标记实现选择性拒绝，从而在保留模型良性任务性能的同时显著降低有害行为。相比传统删减或输出层抑制方法，该方法在安全与效用之间取得更好平衡，且拒绝行为可通过条件信号质量调控，证明了安全对齐应视为条件控制问题而非遗忘问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全干预方法要么破坏有害知识（如去学习、过滤），要么在输出层抑制（如拒绝训练），均导致邻域能力下降或过度拒绝；本文旨在解决这一权衡问题，提出保留有害知识但通过特权控制标记进行行为约束的思路。

Method: Token Inoculation采用双阶段策略：1）在持续预训练中，于双用途文档旁插入特殊控制标记，使模型将该标记与有害语义绑定；2）在监督微调中，训练模型在标记存在时正确回答有害问题，在标记缺失时拒绝回答，实现选择性拒绝而不删除知识。

Result: 在有害领域（如WMDP-Bio）上，准确率从79%降至18%，同时保留93%的基础模型良性任务性能（如MMLU），在1B-14B模型规模下优于去学习和拒绝微调基线，表现出最优的安全-效用权衡；且拒绝选择性可由条件信号质量调节，预训练中的领域特定语义绑定对泛化至关重要。

Conclusion: 安全对齐更应被看作一个条件控制问题而非遗忘问题：保留敏感知识并受控访问，比彻底销毁更能实现精确的行为控制，为大模型安全提供新范式。

Abstract: Safety interventions on dual-use knowledge typically choose between destroying hazardous content (e.g., unlearning, filtering) and suppressing it at the output layer (e.g., refusal training); both pay a tax in adjacent-domain competence or over-refusal. We argue that the right operation is conditioning, not reduction: we show that hazardous knowledge can be retained in the model and behaviorally gated by a privileged control token. Our method, Token Inoculation, introduces a binding-and-branching approach. First, during continued pre-training, we mark hazardous content by inserting a special token alongside dual-use documents, so the model binds the marker to the underlying semantics of the hazardous domain. Second, during supervised fine-tuning, we teach the model to answer hazardous queries correctly when the special token is present and to refuse them when it is absent, thereby enabling selective refusal without removing dual-use knowledge. On hazardous domain (e.g., WMDP-Bio), Token Inoculation reduces accuracy from 79% to 18% while retaining 93% of the base-model's benign-domain performance (e.g., MMLU), achieving the best safety-utility trade-off against unlearning and refusal-tuning baselines across 1B-14B model scales. We further show that refusal selectivity is controllable through the quality of the conditioning signal and that domain-specific semantic binding during pre-training is critical for the conditional behavior to generalize beyond memorized triggers. Our results suggest that safety alignment is better cast as a conditioning problem than a forgetting one: behavioral control is more precise when sensitive knowledge is retained under controlled access than when it is destroyed.

</details>


### [184] [BRIDGE: Bottleneck-Aware Regulator-Set Inference and Diagnosis for Cooperative Gene Regulatory Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18602)
*Maryam Rahimimovassagh,Clayton Thomas Barham,Ivan Garibay,Niloofar Yousefi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出BRIDGE框架和TRACE诊断工具，用于完整恢复协同调控子集合，并通过无泄漏机制不匹配的协同压力测试评估其性能。采用残差高阶集评分（Residual HOS2）在原始表达向量上进行评分，避免了人为构建的乘积相关特征，相比传统成对集评分方法（PairS2），显著提升Jaccard相似度（0.382→0.460）、召回率（0.522→0.597）和精确恢复率（0.053→0.113）。但精确恢复仍较低，表明集级排序错误是主要瓶颈。通过候选集筛选可减少94-97%的候选集，同时保持精确恢复行为，说明调控子边排名、候选检索、集级评分与精确恢复应作为独立目标处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基因调控网络推断方法多输出成对调控子-靶标排名，难以捕捉协同调控中多个调控子共同作用的本质，亟需完整恢复调控子集合并准确评估协同效应的方法。

Method: 提出BRIDGE框架实现调控子集合的完整恢复，结合TRACE诊断工具，引入无泄漏机制不匹配的协同压力测试，使用残差高阶集评分（Residual HOS2）在原始表达数据上进行评分，避免特征与机制的循环依赖。

Result: 在30个匹配的种子协同设置下，Residual HOS2显著优于PairS2，提升多项指标；在SERGIO DS3数据集上，发现候选覆盖虽必要但不足，集级排序错误是精确恢复失败的主要原因；通过先生成候选集再用Residual HOS2重排序，可大幅减少候选集数量（94-97%），同时保持精确恢复性能。

Conclusion: 调控子边排名、候选检索、集级评分和精确协同调控子集合恢复应被视作独立任务，需分别优化。本研究为协同基因调控的系统性建模与诊断提供了新范式。

Abstract: Cooperative gene regulation often depends on groups of regulators acting jointly, but most gene regulatory network (GRN) inference methods output pairwise regulator-target rankings. We introduce Bottleneck-Aware Regulator-Set Inference and Diagnosis (BRIDGE), a framework for complete regulator-set recovery, and Targeted Recovery Attribution for Cooperative Evaluation (TRACE), a diagnostic suite that attributes failures to retrieval, set-level scoring, decoding, and evaluation bottlenecks.
  TRACE includes a leak-free mechanism-mismatch cooperativity stress test in which cooperative targets are generated by random nonlinear mechanisms rather than product interactions. This design avoids feature-mechanism circularity: Residual higher-order set scoring (Residual HOS2) operates on raw expression vectors without handcrafted product-correlation features. Across 30 matched seed-cooperativity settings, Residual HOS2 improves Jaccard similarity from 0.382 to 0.460, recall from 0.522 to 0.597, and exact recovery from 0.053 to 0.113 over a decomposable pairwise set scorer (PairS2), although exact recovery remains low.
  On SERGIO DS3, oracle retrieval and TRACE show that candidate coverage is necessary but insufficient because set-level misranking remains the dominant source of exact-recovery failure. PairS2 proposal followed by Residual HOS2 reranking reduces HOS2-scored candidate sets by 94-97% while largely preserving exact-recovery behavior. These results distinguish edge ranking, candidate retrieval, set-level scoring, and exact cooperative regulator-set recovery as separate objectives.

This is particularly relevant to the Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP), where solver performance is strongly instance-dependent. We introduce GNNAS-TSP, a Graph Neural Network (GNN)-based AS framework that learns TSP instance representations directly from raw graph data, avoiding manual feature engineering. GNNAS-TSP formulates AS as a joint cost-prediction and ranking task. We evaluate cost-based (mean squared error (MSE), mean absolute error (MAE), and Huber), rank-based (RankNet, ListNet, and LambdaRank), and hybrid learning objectives for a portfolio comprising Chained Lin-Kernighan, Edge Assembly Crossover, Lin-Kernighan-Helsgaun, Multiagent Optimization System, and Concorde. For the 10s budget, AS achieves substantial and statistically significant cost improvement over SBS. Overall, the results suggest that GNNAS-TSP is a useful meta-solving strategy when exploitable variation exists across solver performance.

### [186] [Stale but Stable: Staleness-Adaptive Trust Regions for Stabilizing Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18722)
*Junyao Yang,Yucheng Shi,Zongxia Li,Zhongzhi Li,Ruhan Wang,Xiangxin Zhou,Kishan Panaganti,Haitao Mi,Leowei Liang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Staleness-Adaptive Trust Region (SAT)的新方法，用于解决异步强化学习中因延迟导致的策略不一致问题。SAT利用采样对数比率作为延迟代理，通过基于延迟的核缩放识别每批数据中的高不匹配尾部，并仅收缩名义PPO区间中符号选定的端点，从而在普通令牌上保持基线行为，同时对新捕获的外向区域实施更保守的更新。理论证明了局部区间包含性和相对于PPO的点态悲观性，表明该自适应规则在异质延迟下重塑了更新几何结构。实验在基于Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base、SGLang推理引擎和Megatron训练框架的异步设置中进行，SAT-GSPO结合R3实现了最佳性能，在延迟为1和8时分别达到35.83和34.79的AIME24 avg@8得分，验证了自适应裁剪与路由重播作为互补稳定机制的有效性。整体而言，将裁剪区间与延迟异质性对齐能有效稳定异步强化学习过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异步强化学习虽提升吞吐量，但面临由策略滞后、引擎延迟和混合专家路由引起的延迟问题，导致训练-推理偏差加剧，传统PPO裁剪仅控制采样外向更新，无法有效约束高延迟更新，造成稳定性下降。

Method: 提出Staleness-Adaptive Trust Region (SAT)，使用分离的采样对数比率作为延迟代理，通过延迟驱动的核缩放识别批次内高不匹配区域，并仅对名义PPO区间的符号选定端点进行收缩，实现对延迟敏感区域的保守更新，同时保留正常区域的基线行为。

Result: 在异步设置下，SAT-GSPO + R3在延迟1和8时分别取得35.83和34.79的AIME24 avg@8最高分；自适应裁剪与路由重播分别缓解了不匹配尾部和路由不一致性问题，显著提升系统稳定性。

Conclusion: 将裁剪区间与延迟异质性对齐是稳定异步强化学习的关键，SAT通过动态调整更新约束，有效应对高延迟带来的挑战，为异步架构提供了更强的理论保障与实践性能。

Abstract: Asynchronous reinforcement learning improves throughput by decoupling rollout generation from optimization, but staleness is an inevitable byproduct compounded by policy lag, engine delays, and mixture-of-experts routing. From a trust-region perspective, this mismatch is critical: training-inference divergence governs approximation error in finite-horizon bounds, whereas PPO clipping only gates sampled outward updates, acting as a sampled surrogate rather than a full-policy constraint. As a result, high-staleness updates remain weakly controlled in the asynchronous regime where stale rollouts matter most.
  We introduce the Staleness-Adaptive Trust Region (SAT), which uses the detached sampled log-ratio as a practical staleness proxy, identifies high-mismatch tails within each batch via staleness-based kernel scaling, and contracts only the sign-selected endpoint of the nominal PPO interval. This preserves baseline behavior on ordinary tokens while enforcing more conservative updates on newly intercepted outward bands. We prove local interval containment and pointwise pessimism relative to PPO, showing how the adaptive rule reshapes update geometry under heterogeneous staleness.
  We evaluate SAT in a decoupled asynchronous RL setup built on Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base, using SGLang as the inference engine and Megatron for training. In this setting, SAT-GSPO w/ R3 achieves the best observed AIME24 avg@8, reaching 35.83 at lag 1 and 34.79 at lag 8, while SAT-GSPO reaches 34.17 at lag 1. Adaptive clipping and routing replay act as complementary stabilizers targeting mismatch tails and routing inconsistency, respectively. Overall, aligning clip intervals with staleness heterogeneity effectively stabilizes asynchronous RL.

Here, using a neuropsychology-informed paradigm, we find that existing EEG2Text benchmarks have neglected EEG instability, a flaw that has confounded inference and sparked debate. In comparisons with multiple existing benchmarks, COFETT achieves SOTA ability to distinguish among model performances and enables robust, teacher-forcing-free evaluation, thereby opening a path toward practical EEG2Text applications. ### [188] [Spaghetti Architect: A Contamination-Resistant, By-Construction-Labelled, Multi-Language Code Dataset Generator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18642)
*Yuxiang Ji*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Spaghetti Architect 是一个用于生成受控代码数据集的工具，通过反优化编译器将干净的、语言无关的 JSON 中间表示转换为五种语言（Python、JavaScript、Go、Java、C++）中冗余且完全扁平化的程序。每个程序经过编译、运行并验证正确性，确保其正确性。该方法提供已知最优参考（干净 IR）、可调节的“混乱度”（基于严格嵌套的反模式配置）、两个独立的难度维度（内在问题规模与外在呈现复杂度），并通过私有种子生成新变体以防止数据污染。实验表明，该数据集能有效区分模型性能，揭示出即使最强模型在特定任务上也会因内在难度而失效；开发集与保留测试集表现高度一致（差异小于0.012），且自注释机制对弱模型提升显著（优于强模型约一个数量级）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码语料库虽然丰富但缺乏控制，存在语义模糊、表面混乱、难度不可控等问题，且公共样本可能已被模型训练数据包含，导致评估失真。因此需要一种可控制、可重复、无污染的代码数据生成机制。

Method: 使用反优化编译器将语言无关的清晰中间表示（JSON IR）转化为五种目标语言中冗余、扁平化且结构混乱的程序；通过编译、执行和参考断言验证每条程序的正确性；引入严格嵌套的反模式配置来控制‘混乱度’；定义两个正交难度轴（内在问题规模与外在呈现复杂度）；利用私有种子生成新样本以避免训练集污染；对生成程序添加自注释以评估其对模型的影响。

Result: 实验结果显示：随着模型规模增大，精确匹配率上升，但内在难度调控会将最强模型在算术聚合任务上的准确率降至零；开发集与保留测试集得分极为接近（|Δ| ≤ 0.012 和 ≤ 0.011）；重构任务中等价性从0.73提升至0.99，且不受规模影响；而输出预测能力随规模下降；自注释机制对最弱模型的增益远大于最强模型（-0.173 vs -0.017），说明其能有效解决原本难以区分的模型差距。

Conclusion: Spaghetti Architect 提供了一种高质量、可控、抗污染的代码数据生成框架，能够真实反映模型在理解与重构任务中的能力边界，适用于公平、可重复的模型评估。项目开源（MIT许可），无依赖，可通过持久 DOI 访问。

Abstract: Mined code corpora are abundant but uncontrolled: a snippet's semantics, surface "messiness," and difficulty are whatever the wild contained; there is no known-optimal reference to grade against; and any public sample may already sit in a model's training set. We present Spaghetti Architect, a tool that mints code datasets with the control such corpora lack. An anti-optimization transpiler maps a clean, language-agnostic JSON intermediate representation to deliberately redundant, fully-flattened programs in five languages (Python, JavaScript, Go, Java, C++); every program is compiled, run, and checked against a reference oracle, so each instance is correct by construction. The clean IR is a known-optimal reference, messiness is dialed by strictly-nested anti-pattern profiles, each instance is labelled along two orthogonal difficulty axes, intrinsic (problem size) and incidental (presentation at fixed semantics), and contamination is resisted by minting fresh variants from a private held-out seed. We give construct-validity evidence that the quality order moves established complexity and readability metrics, and report baselines on a four-model open ladder: exact match rises with scale, and the intrinsic knob collapses arithmetic-aggregation accuracy of even the strongest model to zero. Further, development-set scores equal freshly re-minted held-out counterparts within $|Δ|\le 0.012$ (comprehension) and $\le 0.011$ (refactoring); on identical programs, refactoring equivalence ($0.73 \rightarrow 0.99$) is scale-invariant while output prediction collapses; and ablating the generator's self-annotations shows they inflate the weakest model an order of magnitude more than the strongest ($-0.173$ vs $-0.017$): the annotated ladder resolves one of three adjacent pairs where the unannotated resolves all three. Open source (MIT), dependency-free, archived under a persistent DOI.

</details>


### [189] [Exposure-Based Reinforcement Learning to Rank](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18689)
*Harrie Oosterhuis,Rolf Jagerman,Zhen Qin,Xuanhui Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于暴露（exposure）的强化学习（RL）方法，用于学习排序（LTR），避免使用复杂的自定义梯度计算。通过方差减少和部分边际化技术，实现了高样本效率，并利用文档曝光分布抽象，使梯度估计与自动微分无缝集成。该方法只需实现一个关于曝光的可微损失函数，即可通过自动微分进行优化，显著提升收敛速度和排序性能，且在GPU上无额外计算开销。相比现有方法，新方法更稳定、高效且易于应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准强化学习在学习排序任务中因动作空间巨大而计算成本高且效率低；现有方法依赖复杂自定义梯度，难以实现且与自动微分冲突，限制了其在实践中的应用。因此亟需一种更高效、易用且稳定的替代方案。

Method: 提出基于文档曝光分布的梯度估计抽象，结合基线修正与部分边际化以降低方差，实现高样本效率；将损失函数设计为曝光的可微函数，从而完全依赖自动微分进行优化，无需手动实现梯度。

Result: 实验表明，新方法在收敛速度、排序性能上显著优于现有自定义梯度方法，且在GPU上无额外计算开销；同时避免了传统方法在多轮训练中的严重不稳定性问题。

Conclusion: 本文提出的暴露驱动的强化学习框架显著提升了学习排序方法的有效性、效率与易用性，为实际应用提供了更可靠、高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) methods for learning-to-rank (LTR) can optimize (almost) any ranking goal, e.g., from precision or discounted cumulative gain to fairness-of-exposure or ranking distillation. However, standard RL is ineffective and computationally costly due to the enormous action space in LTR settings. Existing methods reach computational efficiency through custom gradient computation algorithms, but they are very complex to implement and often clash with auto-differentiation. Consequently, existing RL for LTR is not attractive to many practitioners. We reconsider RL for LTR while actively avoiding reliance on custom gradients. Contrary to the existing approaches, we focus on variance reduction and GPU computation. In doing so, we discover that high sample-efficiency can be reached through baseline corrections and partial marginalization. Furthermore, we propose an abstraction that places gradient estimation behind a document-exposure distribution, this enables seamless plug-and-play integration with auto-differentiation. Thereby, one only has to implement a loss as a differentiable function of exposure and RL for LTR can optimize it using auto-differentiation. Our experimental results reveal that our new exposure-based RL for LTR approach converges considerably faster and at significantly higher ranking performance than existing custom gradients, with no additional costs in computation time when using GPUs. In contrast, existing custom gradients result in severe stability issues when converging over many epochs, which never occur for our methods. Thus, we considerably improve RL for LTR methodology by increasing its effectiveness, efficiency, and ease of application.

</details>


### [190] [Contraction-Gauge Preconditioning for Quantized Matrix Multiplication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18745)
*Piyush Sao,Narasinga Miniskar,Pedro Valero-Lara,Keita Teranishi,Sudip Seal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了双因子量化下的低精度矩阵乘法 C=AB 的计算，推导出在独立零均值逐元素误差（已知方差场）下期望平方乘积误差的精确有限维恒等式，适用于非溢出减法抖动和独立随机舍入，并对确定性舍入到最近（RTN）进行实证评估。通过利用乘积保持等价性 AB=(AT)(T^{-1}B)，提出收缩度量预处理：在量化前联合选择因子表示及其共享模式。预处理可降低乘积误差，但可能需要额外的、经过变换并量化的对端操作数副本——共享变换需一份，块特定变换最多每块一份。在正对角度量（折叠）的有界族中，可通过几何规划求解全局最优共享折叠，线性规划判断单位折叠是否已最优。对于其他族，推导出可计算的选择统计量——缩放的尾指数、划分的轮廓散布、旋转的相干性和加权格拉姆能量、层次深度的切片能量协方差，并给出排名启发式候选者的上界。在训练好的三块图像分类器的十二个线性乘积中，抖动模型预测与确定性RTN误差之间的组内秩相关系数在8位时为0.937，4位时为0.918。GP折叠方案在8位时将保留乘积误差平均降低18.0%，4位时降低20.5%；优于SmoothQuant风格的网格基线，在两个精度下均在十个乘积中表现更优，并使组合logit MSE分别降低15.4%和26.4%。因此，本文提供了精确的随机乘积误差核算、对角族内的认证选择，以及评估可重用变换候选者在RTN下的统一目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低精度矩阵乘法在双因子量化下的误差分析缺乏精确建模，且预处理策略选择缺乏理论指导。本文旨在建立精确的误差分析框架，提供可优化的预处理方法，以提升量化后矩阵乘法的精度和效率。

Method: 基于乘积保持等价性构造收缩度量预处理框架，采用几何规划和线性规划求解最优对角预处理参数；针对不同预处理族设计可计算的选择统计量（如尾指数、轮廓散布、相干性等），并结合上界用于启发式候选者排序。同时通过抖动模型推导精确误差恒等式，并实证验证其在确定性舍入到最近（RTN）下的有效性。

Result: 在十二个来自三块图像分类器的线性乘积上，抖动模型预测与实际RTN误差的秩相关性高达0.918（4位）至0.937（8位）；所提出的几何规划折叠方案在8位和4位下分别实现18.0%和20.5%的几何平均误差降低，优于SmoothQuant基线，并显著降低组合logit MSE（15.4%和26.4%）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了低精度双量化矩阵乘法的精确误差分析框架，提出了有效的收缩度量预处理机制，实现了对角族内的全局最优选择，并提供统一的目标函数用于评估可重用变换候选。该方法在多个真实任务中表现出优异的误差控制能力和性能提升。

Abstract: We study low-precision computation of C=AB with both factors quantized. We derive an exact finite-dimensional identity for the expected squared product error under independent, zero-mean entrywise errors with known variance fields; it holds exactly for non-overloading subtractive dither and for independent stochastic rounding, and we empirically assess deterministic round-to-nearest (RTN). Using the product-preserving equivalence AB=(AT)(T^{-1}B), we formulate contraction-gauge preconditioning: jointly choosing a factor representation and its sharing pattern before quantization. Preconditioning can reduce product error but may require extra transformed, quantized copies of the opposite operand: a shared transform needs one copy, a block-specific transform up to one per block. Within the bounded family of positive diagonal gauges (folds), a geometric program computes a globally optimal shared fold and a linear program decides whether the identity fold is already optimal. For other families we derive computable selection statistics -- tail index for scaling, profile spread for partitioning, coherence and weighted-Gram energy for rotations, slice-energy covariance for hierarchy depth -- with upper bounds for ranking heuristic candidates. Across twelve linear products from a trained three-block image classifier, median within-product rank correlations between dither-model predictions and deterministic-RTN errors are 0.937 at 8 bits and 0.918 at 4 bits. The GP fold cuts held-out product error over the identity fold by 18.0% (8-bit) and 20.5% (4-bit) in geometric mean, beats a SmoothQuant-style grid baseline at both precisions and on ten of twelve products, and lowers composed logit MSE by 15.4% and 26.4%. We thus provide exact stochastic product-error accounting, certified selection within the diagonal family, and a common objective for evaluating reusable transform candidates under RTN.

### [191] [HindsightBench: A Black-Box Behavioral Audit Protocol for Parametric Hindsight in Time-Indexed LLM Decision Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18867)
*Haozhe Jia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HindsightBench，一种低成本黑盒行为审计协议，用于检测大语言模型在时间索引金融决策任务中是否存在参数化事后知识泄露。该协议通过四维日期操纵矩阵、双重记忆探测和六项指标实现高效审计，无需回测、日志概率或语料库访问。在15个来自7家供应商的模型上测试发现：（i）日期触发反射与训练生成年份相关，而非模型规模；（ii）有效截止点比厂商报告日期提前最多8个月；（iii）服务配置（如量化方式、推理模式）显著影响审计结果，需明确指定操作要求。研究释放了数据集、预注册记录、审计结果、成本记录及一键复现工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏廉价有效的手段来审计大语言模型是否在历史金融决策任务中泄露了实际发生结果的参数化知识。尽管此类知识泄露存在已被确认，但缺乏实用的检测工具。

Method: 设计并实现HindsightBench协议，结合四臂日期操纵矩阵（揭示/仅日期/掩码/移植）、双记忆探测（日期恢复与结果回忆）以及六项量化指标，构建一个可扩展、低开销的黑盒审计流程，不依赖回测、日志概率或外部语料库。

Result: 在258节点的时间校正宏观面板上对15个模型进行审计，发现：（1）日期触发反应与训练生成年份一致，与模型规模无关；（2）有效知识截止时间普遍早于厂商报告时间达8个月；（3）不同服务配置（如BF16 vs FP8、AWQ-INT4、推理模式）显著影响审计稳定性，提示必须固定量化和推理策略。

Conclusion: HindsightBench提供了一种高效且可靠的黑盒审计方案，能精准识别大语言模型中的参数化事后知识泄露问题，并揭示当前模型部署中存在的隐性偏差来源。其成果强调了在实际应用中必须严格控制模型服务配置以确保审计有效性。

Abstract: Large language models leak parametric knowledge of realized outcomes into historical financial decision tasks. Existence is settled; what users lack is a cheap way to audit a given model for it. We present HindsightBench, a black-box behavioral audit protocol that profiles parametric hindsight in any time-indexed LLM decision task at probe-level cost (no backtests, no logprobs, no corpus access). The protocol chains a four-arm date-manipulation matrix (revealed/date-only/masked/transplanted), dual memory probes (date recovery; outcome recall), and six per-model metrics -- trigger strength, transplant effect, post-cutoff placebo, recoverability, behaviorally effective knowledge cutoff, and a recall-accuracy dissociation coefficient -- with explicit gates where identifiability is data-dependent. Applying it to 15 models from seven vendors on a 258-node vintage-correct macro panel yields three headline patterns: (i) the date-trigger reflex tracks training generation, not scale -- absent across the 2024 open-weight generation from 1B to 70B, present in every tested 2026-generation model, and switching on within one vendor lineage (Qwen3 -> Qwen3.6) at fixed MoE architecture and 3B active parameters; (ii) effective cutoffs span 22 months across vendors and precede vendor-reported dates by up to eight months, invalidating calendar-window placebo designs; (iii) audit results are not invariant to serving -- BF16 serving of an FP8-referenced model breaks the trigger estimate's stability while AWQ-INT4 preserves it, and a provider-locked reasoning regime makes one probe non-convergent -- so the protocol ships with operational requirements (pin quantization and thinking regime; disclose parser and sampling policy). We release the panel, frozen preregistrations, per-model audit rows with measured dollar costs, transcripts, and one-command regeneration.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ConceptCF通过时间序列分解提取可解释的概念（如尺度、频率带），并使用遗传算法优化这些概念的变异，生成符合要求的反事实解释。

Abstract: This paper proposes ConceptCF, a method for counterfactual generation that operates on human-interpretable concepts. In high-stakes domains such as healthcare and predictive maintenance, artificial intelligence models can increase efficiency and safety. Explainability is key to ensure these models rely on causal relationships rather than spurious correlations. Counterfactual explanations identify minimal modifications that would change a model's predictions. Existing methods for time series operate on individual points or subsequences without ensuring interpretability of the mutations. ConceptCF instead modifies meaningful concepts. As a result we can provide explanations in terms of these concepts, for example ``the model's prediction would be `Sit' instead of `Walk' if you increase the scale of the movement''. In this paper, the concepts are constructed through time series decomposition, resulting in concepts such as scale, and frequency bands. Counterfactuals are generated using a genetic algorithm that optimizes the concept mutations. Evaluation against five state-of-the-art approaches demonstrates that ConceptCF consistently achieves top-tier performance across validity, confidence, proximity, sparsity and plausibility metrics.

### [193] [H$^2$SD: Hybrid Hindsight Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18955)
*Qiye Cai,Yichuan Ma,Linyang Li,Peiji Li,Yongkang Chen,Qipeng Guo,Yicheng Zou,Tao Gui,Xiaocheng Feng,Bing Qin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: H²SD提出了一种混合事后自蒸馏框架，通过根据轨迹正确性差异化使用教师信号，在成功轨迹中调节更新幅度，在失败轨迹中通过最小化反向KL散度进行显式纠正，从而实现更稳定且高效的强化学习与可验证奖励结合的推理能力提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法多采用标量奖励，导致监督稀疏且难以进行细粒度的信用分配；OPD虽提供密集监督但依赖额外教师模型和共享词汇表；OPSD虽无需外部教师但直接匹配教师分布易引发信息泄露与优化不稳定；RLSD虽缓解此问题但缺乏失败时的明确修正方向。因此需要一种既能保持稳定性又能提供有效指导的新方法。

Method: H²SD采用分情况处理策略：对于成功轨迹，利用重新表述指令下的教师输出概率调节学生模型的更新幅度，不改变由奖励决定的方向；对于失败轨迹，则以关键推理步骤和验证答案为提示，将教师作为参考，最小化学生到教师的反向KL散度，实现显式修正。

Result: 在多个高难度推理基准测试中，H²SD consistently 超过代表性RLVR、OPSD和RLSD基线方法，在保持优化稳定性的同时展现出良好的生成效率。

Conclusion: H²SD通过智能区分成功与失败轨迹并相应调整教师信号的使用方式，有效平衡了优化稳定性与信用分配精度，显著提升了大语言模型在数学推理与代码生成等任务中的表现。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning capabilities of large language models on tasks such as mathematical reasoning and code generation. However, most RLVR methods assign a scalar outcome reward to an entire trajectory, resulting in sparse supervision and limited token-level credit assignment. On-policy distillation (OPD) provides denser supervision by distilling token-level distributions from a stronger teacher model, but requires an additional teacher and typically assumes a shared vocabulary. On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) removes this dependency by conditioning the same model on privileged information to construct a teacher policy. However, directly matching the teacher distribution may cause information leakage and unstable optimization. RLSD avoids direct matching by using the teacher signal only to modulate update magnitudes, but it cannot provide an explicit correction direction when the sampled reasoning fails. To address this tradeoff, we introduce $\mathrm{H}^{2}\mathrm{SD}$, a hybrid hindsight self distillation framework that uses the teacher differently according to trajectory correctness. For successful trajectories, the teacher receives the student response confirmed as correct together with a rephrasing instruction, and its probabilities on the original response tokens are used to modulate update magnitudes without changing the direction determined by the reward. For failed trajectories, we condition the teacher on a reference hint containing key reasoning steps and a verified answer, and minimize the reverse KL divergence from the student to the teacher. Experiments on multiple challenging reasoning benchmarks show that H$^2$SD consistently outperforms representative RLVR, OPSD, and RLSD baselines while maintaining stable optimization and favorable generation efficiency.

### [195] [Relative Positions Generalize, Absolute Positions Memorize: An Implicit-Bias Account of Length Generalization in Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18759)
*Subham Singh,Ashutosh Mishra,Subha Raut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了使用相对位置编码的Transformer模型在序列长度外推方面的优势，提出从优化偏差的角度解释这一现象。研究发现，旋转编码（rotary encodings）使注意力权重仅依赖于相对偏移，实现精确等变性，从而在训练长度之外仍能保持一致的行为；而学习的绝对位置编码则导致模型在训练范围外的位置无法约束，倾向于固定在训练范围内的某个绝对位置。研究还揭示了一种低秩“载体”核结构，并提出了注意力稀释定律来描述精度随长度变化的衰减规律，这些预测在不同随机种子和偏移量下均得到验证。此外，线性注意力实验表明该机制依赖于softmax归一化，若无归一化，则梯度下降会选择最小范数插值解，不具备外推能力。最终，这些发现可推广至多层多头Transformer模型，并连接了注意力的隐式偏差、递归模型中的外推偏差以及RASP-L猜想的学习层面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解为何使用相对位置编码的Transformer模型能够有效外推到比训练时更长的序列，而使用学习的绝对位置编码的模型通常不能。现有解释主要集中在表达能力上，但本文旨在提供一个基于优化偏差的新视角。

Method: 通过设计一个最小化的固定偏移检索任务，隔离出位置选择问题，分析梯度下降在短序列上选择的解决方案如何影响长序列上的外推性能。采用理论证明与实验验证相结合的方法，考察旋转编码与绝对编码在注意力得分函数上的差异，分析其隐式偏差，并引入‘载体’核和注意力稀释定律进行建模与验证。进一步通过线性注意力控制实验排除归一化的作用，最后将结论扩展至多层多头架构。

Result: 旋转编码使注意力得分仅依赖于相对偏移，具有精确等变性，使得训练中学习到的选择规则可直接复制到任意更长序列上，实现良好外推；而绝对编码则导致模型在超出训练范围的位置无约束，选择固定绝对位置作为锚点，无法外推。实验验证了低秩载体核的存在及注意力稀释定律对精度衰减的预测。线性注意力实验表明，该机制依赖softmax归一化。多层多头模型中，上述现象、等变性和载体结构均可转移。

Conclusion: 本文从优化偏差角度解释了相对位置编码在序列长度外推中的优势。旋转编码通过实现注意力得分的精确等变性，确保训练学到的规则可无缝迁移至更长序列；而绝对编码因缺乏这种等变性，导致模型在长序列上表现退化。该机制不仅适用于简单任务，也适用于完整序列长度泛化任务，为理解深度模型的外推能力提供了新视角，并连接了注意力学习、递归模型外推与RASP-L猜想。

Abstract: Transformers with relative positional encodings often extrapolate to sequences longer than those seen during training, whereas transformers with learned absolute encodings typically do not. This is a robust empirical regularity, and the explanations offered for it so far are chiefly about expressivity, that is, about whether a length-generalizing solution exists. We give an optimization explanation. On a minimal fixed-offset retrieval task that isolates positional selection, the gap is governed by the implicit bias of the trained attention head: among the many solutions that fit short sequences, which one gradient descent actually selects. We prove that rotary encodings make the attention logit a function of relative offset alone, an exact equivariance, so whatever selection rule is learned at training lengths is reproduced verbatim at every longer length. Learned absolute encodings instead leave out-of-range positions unconstrained, and the trained head pins to a fixed absolute position inside the training range. We characterize the learned rotary rule as a low-rank ``carrier'' kernel aligned with the target offset, and we derive the resulting graceful accuracy decay as an attention-dilution law; both predictions are confirmed across seeds and offsets. A linear-attention control shows the mechanism is specific to softmax: without normalization, training selects a min-norm interpolant that does not extrapolate. The phenomenon, the equivariance, and the carrier all transfer to a multi-layer, multi-head transformer trained on a full-sequence length-generalization task. The account connects the implicit bias of attention, implicit bias for extrapolation in recurrent models, and the learning side of the RASP-L conjecture.

</details>


### [196] [AdaFlash: Adaptive Speculative Decoding via On-Policy Distilled Diffusion Drafters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19223)
*Yu-Yang Qian,Hao-Cong Wu,Chen Chen,Jiacheng Sun,Zhenhua Dong,Peng Zhao,Zhi-Hua Zhou*

TL;DR: AdaFlash提出解决扩散草稿模型中双向注意力带来的方差问题，通过基于反KL散度的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）和自适应长度头，显著提升推理速度与稳定性，尤其在高并发场景下性能超越现有最佳方法约66%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现扩散草稿模型因双向注意力导致领域级和词元级方差大，影响生成稳定性和验证效率，亟需优化以提升推理性能。

Method: 提出AdaFlash框架，包含：(i) 针对扩散草稿器设计的基于反KL散度的在线策略蒸馏（OPD），实现稳定收敛并降低领域级方差；(ii) 动态调整候选序列长度的自适应长度头，减少目标模型验证开销并缓解词元级方差。

Result: 实验表明AdaFlash在部署中持续提升加速比，尤其在高并发场景下吞吐量较当前最优方法提升约66%。

Conclusion: AdaFlash有效解决了扩散草稿模型中的方差问题，显著提升了大语言模型推理效率与鲁棒性，是当前最先进的推理加速方案之一。

Abstract: Speculative decoding, in which a lightweight draft model first generates a draft sequence that is then verified in parallel by the target model, has become a prevalent paradigm for accelerating large language model inference. Recent work such as DFlash further boosts drafting efficiency by leveraging diffusion drafters, whose parallel denoising mechanism enables draft generation in a single forward pass. In this work, we uncover a central pitfall of diffusion drafters: bidirectional attention is a double-edged sword. On one hand, it endows the model with parallel generation and global contextual modeling capabilities; on the other hand, this inherent global dependency introduces high variance at both the domain-level and the token-level: acceptance rates fluctuate substantially across different domains, and draft token quality also varies heterogeneously at different token positions. To tackle this issue, we propose AdaFlash framework, comprising two components: (i) an on-policy distillation (OPD) algorithm with reverse-KL divergence tailored for diffusion drafters, bringing stable convergence and effectively reducing domain-level variance; and (ii) an adaptive length head that dynamically adjusts the candidate sequence length on the fly, substantially lowering the verification cost of the target model and handling token-level variance. Experiments demonstrate that AdaFlash consistently improves speedup rate during deployment, with especially significant gains in high-concurrency scenarios, achieving up to approximately 66% higher throughput than previous state-of-the-art methods.

### [197] [Formulation-Level Auto-Tuning for QUBO-Based Machine Learning: A Case Study Across Multiple Quantum-Inspired Annealers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18774)
*Naoya Mizuki,Takahiro Katagiri,Daichi Mukunoki,Tetsuya Hoshino*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Optuna的公式级自动调优框架，用于在多种量子启发退火器上实现支持向量机（SVM）。通过将连续对偶变量离散化并转化为无约束二次二值优化（QUBO）模型，引入三类耦合参数：表示参数（编码基B和位深K）、RBF核参数γ和等式约束惩罚ξ。该框架将联合选择问题建模为混合离散-连续黑箱优化问题，采用内外两层优化结构：内层退火器最小化生成的QUBO，外层Optuna循环重构公式并最大化验证准确率。该方法适用于Fixstars Amplify、Toshiba SQBM+和Fujitsu Digital Annealer，并与传统网格搜索对比，在线性和非线性分类任务中分别获得约0.8和2.1个百分点的平均提升。结果表明，公式质量与后端能力需协同评估，任务级反馈可补偿离散化误差、惩罚失衡及后端近似优化带来的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子启发退火器上的SVM实现受限于离散化过程引入的多类参数耦合，且缺乏高效参数调优机制，导致性能受限。传统网格搜索效率低，难以应对复杂参数空间，亟需一种自动化、智能化的调优框架以提升分类性能。

Method: 将SVM的连续对偶变量离散化为QUBO形式，构建包含表示参数、核参数和惩罚参数的混合离散-连续黑箱优化问题；采用双层优化结构：内层由退火器求解QUBO，外层使用Optuna（TPE和高斯过程采样器）进行全局参数搜索，通过验证准确率反馈重构公式并优化参数组合。

Result: 在含0-20%标签噪声的线性和非线性分类任务中，相比传统网格搜索，平均准确率分别提升约0.8和2.1个百分点；验证了框架在不同退火器上的通用性与有效性，证明任务级反馈可有效缓解离散化误差与后端近似优化的影响。

Conclusion: 公式设计质量与后端计算能力必须协同评估，而基于任务反馈的自动调优能够显著提升量子启发退火器上SVM的分类性能，为未来混合量子经典算法的优化提供了有效范式。

Abstract: This paper presents an Optuna-based formulation-level auto-tuning framework for support vector machines (SVMs) implemented on multiple quantum-inspired annealers. In an annealing-based SVM, continuous dual variables are discretized and converted into a quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) model. This transformation introduces three coupled classes of parameters: representation parameters-the encoding base B and bit depth K-which determine numerical range, resolution, and QUBO size; the RBF kernel parameter γ, which determines classifier geometry; and the equality-constraint penalty ξ, which controls feasibility and coefficient balance. We formulate their joint selection as a mixed discrete-continuous black-box optimization problem. The framework has two optimization levels: an inner annealer minimizes the generated QUBO, while an outer Optuna loop reconstructs the formulation in every trial and maximizes validation accuracy. The same solver-agnostic procedure is applied to Fixstars Amplify Annealing Engine, Toshiba SQBM+, and Fujitsu Digital Annealer using TPE and Gaussian-process samplers and is compared with conventional grid search. Experiments on linear and nonlinear classification tasks with 0-20% label noise show mean gains over grid search of approximately 0.8 and 2.1 percentage points, respectively. The results demonstrate that formulation quality and backend capability must be evaluated jointly and that task-level feedback can compensate for discretization, penalty imbalance, and backend-dependent approximate optimization.

### [200] [QScheduler: Adaptive Gradient Sampling for Zeroth-Order On-Device Training on INT8 NPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18802)

<details>

Method: 提出 QScheduler 算法，通过监测训练过程中的损失变化趋势动态调整梯度采样数 q；结合 INT8 量化技术，在 STM32N6 的 NPU 上实现低功耗、低内存占用的模型训练。

Result: 实验表明，QScheduler 在 ResNet18 与 MobileNetV2 上均达到与精心调优的固定 q 配置相当的性能，且无需额外的超参数搜索，显著提升了设备端训练的实用性与效率。

Conclusion: QScheduler 成功实现了无需人工调参的自适应零阶优化，为在资源受限的 NPU 微控制器上开展高效、可扩展的设备端学习提供了可行路径，是迈向轻量级边缘智能的重要一步。

Abstract: Zeroth-Order (ZO) optimization enables On-Device Learning (ODL) on NPU-equipped microcontrollers by estimating gradients through forward passes alone, bypassing the need for backpropagation primitives and reducing memory requirements. The number of gradient samples q critically affects training: insufficient samples produce noisy gradients that plateau early, while excessive samples consume more computational resources. However, finding an optimal q typically requires costly hyperparameter searches. This work introduces QScheduler, an adaptive algorithm that adjusts q based on training progress, and provides the first proof-of-concept of INT8 quantized on-device training on the STM32N6's Neural-ART NPU. Experiments on EuroSAT and STL-10 show that QScheduler matches well-tuned fixed-q configurations for both ResNet18 and MobileNetV2, without requiring prior q hyperparameter optimization.
